# Calendarly — Design-Parity Audit (iOS ⟷ Android ⟷ Design)

> Generated by a 3-way fan-out audit (82 designed screens + shared primitives). Design truth = `Calendarly/*-frames.jsx` (360pt-wide phone, **1px = 1pt iOS = 1dp Android**). Tokens = `colors_and_type.css`.
> Raw structured data: `parity-audit-raw.json`. Status legend: matches / minor / major / missing / notfound. `better` = which platform is closer to the design (the other should catch up).

## Headline

- Total designed screens audited: **82**
- **iOS closer on 64**, **Android closer on 13**, equal 5, both-poor 0
- iOS major/missing: **19** · Android major/missing: **47**
- notfound: iOS 1, Android 1

**Verdict:** iOS is the stronger port overall. Root cause is structural — iOS extracted shared scheduling chrome into single sources of truth (status pill, top bar, section-card modifier, slot row, identity theme, numbered wizard step-rail), while Android re-implemented these per-screen, so the same element drifts across dozens of screens. Design **tokens** (type scale, spacing, radii, pillar accents) are in full parity on both platforms — the divergence is entirely at the composite-primitive + per-screen-content layer.

## Fix progress

Branch `claude/calendarly-parity-fixes` (off `feature/calendarly`).

- ✅ **Phase 1a — Android shared primitives** (commit `3cea2ae7`): created `_shared/SchedulingStatusPill.kt` (canonical text-only chip mirroring iOS) + `_shared/SchedulingChrome.kt` (`SchedulingTopBar` 56dp, `schedulingCard()` modifier, `SchedulingMiniToggle`). Migrated ~10 drifting status chips (Hub, BookingPage, Bookings inbox/detail, roster, Manage booking, My bookings, Reschedule/cancel policy, Workflows list) onto `SchedulingStatusPill`. Verified: `:app:compileDebugKotlin` green. NOT yet visually verified on emulator.
- ⏳ **Phase 1b — adopt `SchedulingTopBar` + `schedulingCard()`** across the Material3-`CenterAlignedTopAppBar` screens (default 64dp vs design 56) and the ~60 bespoke card composables. Bigger blast radius (restructures Scaffold topBar slots) → do with emulator screenshot verification.
- ⏳ **Phase 1c — numbered `WizardStepRail`** for onboarding/setup wizards (Android currently uses a segmented bar; design + iOS use numbered discs + per-step labels + "step X of N" overline).
- ✅ **iOS baseline repair** (commit `10024f67`) — the iOS branch **did not compile** (XcodeGen globs all sources into one target; Calendarly collided with Homes/ContentDetail). Fixed 4 filename + 4 type collisions, 2 missing `import SwiftUI`, a Swift-6 actor-isolation init, a Text-only modifier on a TextField, a non-associative comparison, a misplaced `.disabled` on a closure, and added `accentBg` to ~17 VMs. `make build` → **BUILD SUCCEEDED** (Xcode 26.2). This was the prerequisite for ALL iOS parity work.
- ✅ **Phase 2 — iOS catch-up** (commits `1d63d1fc`, `df9897f2`, `5e955941`): A1 Hub (tab-root bar), B1 event-types list (bespoke: toggle/dot-row/segmented filter/template chips), B2/B3, Availability (schedules/weekly/limits/block-off), D/E Reschedule, E12 Manual, F9 Resources list/F13 Visit setup, C1 landing, slot-states, F6 poll, G11 packages, G12/G13 invoices — all `make build` green. Remaining iOS: A12 onboarding-business (minor), G7 Payouts (minor), F14 Visit detail, B8 connected calendars (minor), + shared SlotPicker/Icons.swift slot-states frames (cross-cutting), + data-blocked group/team/composed frames.
- 🔄 **Phase 3 — Android content catch-up** (47 major/missing), batched by section. Verification is **compile-only** per user direction (no emulator this pass).
  - ✅ batch 1 — invitee **Confirm/Edge/Customer** (commit `ba3c81d1`): D1 intake (prefill chip, existing-account banner, phone reorder, typed Select, expired/submitting dim), D2 review (refund-policy link, confirming dim+shimmer CTA), D3 confirmed (halo geometry, mono TXN receipt line, email-sending state, reduce-motion confetti), D4 manage (expired footer CTAs, contact-host, accent book-again, spec skeleton), Edge sheets (add-to-cal/open-in-app/payment-failed/policy-blocked/recurring/slot-taken/terminal), My bookings. Data-contract-limited frames deferred (documented, not faked). Compiles green.
  - ✅ batch 2 — **Bookings core + extras** (commit `3dcfcda0`): E2 detail (status timeline, per-status dock, conflict banner, follow-up promo), cancel/refund (segmented presets, restore-credit, terminal frames), E7/E8/E9/E10/E11/E13 extras. Split oversized BookingFilterSheet under the 64KB method limit. Compiles green.
  - ✅ batch 3 — **Find-a-time + Resources/Visits** (commit `78ab45d2`): F4/F6/F7 + F9–F14. Compiles green.
  - ✅ batch 4 — **Event-types + Discovery** (commit `ea33740b`): B2 editor (Collect segmented, Stripe retint), B3 intake (drag-reorder, identity overline), B8 connected-calendars (provider rows + variants), C1 landing, slot-states. Compiles green.
  - ✅ batch 5 — **Business/Payments/Packages/Invoices/Onboarding** (this commit): G5 (skeleton geom + Stripe disc), G6 (SchedulingTopBar + receipt chip + tax toggle), G11 my-packages, G12/G13 invoices (design-primary), A12 onboarding-home (removed off-spec flow toggle). Compiles green.
  - ⏳ remaining: Home calendar **F2/F3** (in `homes/calendar` module — separate care), and the deferred **top-bar 56dp chrome** migration (needs inset handling + per-screen action variation — best with emulator verification).

**Build notes (critical):** use `JAVA_HOME=…/temurin-17`, kill stray Gradle/Kotlin daemons before each build, set `-Pkotlin.daemon.jvmargs="-Xmx10240m …"` (the project's 4g OOMs on full compile), and never let fan-out agents run their own `./gradlew` (single-worker deadlock). See memory `calendarly-android-parity`. ktlint/detekt/token gates are pre-RED on untouched files (out of scope).

## Remaining work & verification notes

- **Resolved — Embed widget (was "notfound both"):** the design itself states it is **web-only** ("Embed / inline booking widget settings (web)" — surfaces /book onto external sites). Correctly absent on iOS/Android; not a gap.
- **Needs emulator verification (deferred from compile-only pass):** the Android **top-bar 56dp chrome** — ~10 screens use Material3 `CenterAlignedTopAppBar` (64dp). `SchedulingTopBar` (56dp) exists, but migrating requires per-screen status-bar-inset handling (Scaffold-topBar-slot vs in-content) + a trailing slot for the screens with text "Save"/progress actions; compile can't catch under-status-bar rendering, so this should be done with an emulator. Screens: visits/VisitDetail+VisitSetup, resources/Book+Detail+Editor, bookings_extra/Waitlist+ManualBooking+BookingSearchFilter+PostMeetingFollowup+GroupRoster.
- **Polish (low value):** numbered `WizardStepRail` (Android wizards use a segmented bar; needs shared-WizardShell coordination); icon-glyph nits (Android Material has no exact lucide calendar-range/git-commit/etc.; iOS calendarSearch SF remap is 1 line).
- **Data-blocked (no DTO/VM/backend fields — never faked):** group/team/composed-availability frames, itemized fees/tax + saved-card/3DS payment frames, visit offer/reserve/booking-link lifecycle, per-member Free/Busy, live calendar-conflict detection, masked bank/tax-rate literals. Documented per-screen above.
- **Product decision:** the A5 "THIS MONTH" summary card is injected on the hub by BOTH platforms but the A1 design doesn't show it — confirm whether to keep (consistent across platforms) or remove.

## Detailed findings by section

## Primitives

### SHARED PRIMITIVES & CHROME — iOS `minor` / Android `major` → better: **ios**
- iOS files: `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Scheduling/SharedUI/SchedulingIdentityTheme.swift`, `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Scheduling/SharedUI/SchedulingStatusPill.swift`, `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Scheduling/SharedUI/SchedulingSlotRow.swift`, `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Scheduling/Setup/Shared/SetupKit.swift`, `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Scheduling/Setup/Shared/WizardStepViews.swift`, `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Core/Design/Radii.swift`, `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Core/Design/Typography.swift`
- Android files: `frontend/apps/android/app/src/main/java/app/pantopus/android/ui/screens/scheduling/_shared/OwnerPillarChrome.kt`, `frontend/apps/android/app/src/main/java/app/pantopus/android/ui/screens/scheduling/_shared/SlotPicker.kt`, `frontend/apps/android/app/src/main/java/app/pantopus/android/ui/screens/scheduling/_shared/PausedExpiredUnavailableState.kt`, `frontend/apps/android/app/src/main/java/app/pantopus/android/ui/screens/scheduling/hub/HubComponents.kt`, `frontend/apps/android/app/src/main/java/app/pantopus/android/ui/screens/scheduling/invitee/customer/MyBookingsScreen.kt`, `frontend/apps/android/app/src/main/java/app/pantopus/android/ui/screens/scheduling/resources/BookResourceScreen.kt`, `frontend/apps/android/app/src/main/java/app/pantopus/android/ui/screens/homes/calendar/HomeSchedulingKit.kt`, `frontend/apps/android/app/src/main/java/app/pantopus/android/ui/components/StatusChip.kt`
- **Verdict:** iOS centralizes the shared chrome into single canonical primitives (one status pill, one slot row, one identity theme, one 56pt top bar, one numbered StepRail) that track the design archetypes closely; Android lacks most of these shared primitives, so the status pill, top bar, section card, and wizard step rail are each re-implemented inconsistently across dozens of screens and drift from the design grammar.
- **Cross note:** Token foundations are in full parity and both correct: type scale (h1 30/h2 24/h3 20/body 16/small 14/cap 12/overline 11 +0.06em), spacing (4/8/12/16/20/24/32), and radii (xs4/sm6/md8/lg12/xl16/xl2 20/xl3 24/pill) are defined identically in iOS (Typography.swift, Radii.swift) and Android (Typography.kt, Radii.kt, Spacing.kt) and match colors_and_type.css exactly; pillar accents #0284c7/#16a34a/#7c3aed are correct on both. The divergence is entirely at the composite-primitive layer: iOS extracted shared scheduling chrome (status pill, slot row, identity theme, top bar, step rail, card modifier) into single sources of truth, while Android only extracted a subset (OwnerPillarChrome, SlotPicker, terminal-state) and left the status pill, top bar, section card, and wizard step rail to be re-implemented per-screen — which is why the same visual element drifts across many Android screens. The systematic fix is to port iOS's shared primitives (SchedulingStatusPill, a SchedulingTopBar, a SchedulingCard modifier, and a numbered WizardStepRail) into Android's scheduling/_shared and migrate the per-file copies onto them.

**iOS deviations:**
- `low`/`chrome` — iOS SetupTopBar is fixed at exactly 56pt for hub/settings screens, but the design archetypes vary the bar height by surface: home-shell/event-editor TopBar=46, settings-archetype=52, onboarding=56. iOS standardizes on the onboarding height everywhere, so the editor/detail surfaces read slightly taller than their frames. **Fix:** This is a reasonable simplification (one canonical 56pt bar) and arguably better than slavishly matching 46/52; keep as-is unless a specific frame review flags the editor bar as too tall.
- `low`/`icon` — The Business pillar glyph is intentionally split: SchedulingIdentityTheme.icon uses .briefcase (editors/onboarding/links) while SetupKit's SchedulingPillarChoice.icon overrides to .store for the A1 hub switcher. This matches the design (event-editor uses briefcase; hub-frames use store) but the two-source-of-truth split is a parity hazard Android must mirror exactly. **Fix:** Document the briefcase-vs-store split as the canonical contract so Android's pillar() and hub chrome reproduce it; no code change needed on iOS.
- `low`/`color` — SchedulingStatusPill maps .pending and .draft to the warning (amber) tone, matching the design's amber pending/draft chip. This is correct, but it is the single source that Android's many pills must match — Android currently disagrees (see Android findings). **Fix:** No change; this is the reference behavior.

**Android deviations:**
- `high`/`chrome` — No canonical scheduling status pill exists. The status chip is re-implemented at least 5+ times with divergent grammar: HubStatusPill (HubComponents.kt) adds a leading icon, has NO border, font 10sp, and colors 'Completed' green; MyBookingsScreen.StatusPill is text-only WITH a hairline border (closest to spec) but colors 'Pending' info-blue; HomeSchedulingKit.SchedulingStatusBadge is text-only, NO border, font 9.5sp; BookResourceScreen.StatusPill is a full-width icon+text row. The design + iOS SchedulingStatusPill spec is: text-only (no icon), font 10/weight 700, 3x8 padding, tinted fill + 1px tone-light hairline border, neutral grey for paused/cancelled/completed/past/expired. None of the Android variants fully match and they disagree with each other across screens. **Fix:** Add a single SchedulingStatusPill composable in scheduling/_shared mirroring iOS SchedulingStatusPill (SchedulingPillStatus enum with backend-alias init, text-only, tone fill + hairline border, neutral grey for terminal/completed states, testTag scheduling.statusPill.{status}). Replace HubStatusPill, MyBookings.StatusPill, SchedulingStatusBadge, BookResource.StatusPill usages with it.
- `high`/`chrome` — No shared scheduling top app bar primitive. OwnerPillarHeader exists but is used by only 4 of ~229 scheduling files; everything else mixes Material3 CenterAlignedTopAppBar (10+ files: ResourceEditor, VisitSetup, ManualBooking, Waitlist, etc.) which defaults to 64dp (taller than every design frame: 46/52/56) and Material navigationIcon spacing, plus bespoke Row top bars at 44/56dp (Hub, Settings, sheets). The design uses a consistent chevron-left + centered 16/600 title + ~56 height bar. iOS funnels all non-wizard surfaces through one SetupTopBar (56pt, chevron, centered semibold title, optional trailing icon). **Fix:** Introduce a shared SchedulingTopBar composable (height 56dp, chevron-left leading 36dp hit target, centered title PantopusTextStyle h3/16-600, optional trailing icon, 1px bottom appBorder) and migrate the CenterAlignedTopAppBar + bespoke-Row screens onto it so height, title weight, and back-affordance match the frames and iOS.
- `high`/`chrome` — No shared section-card primitive — ~60 scheduling files each define their own private Card composable (HubCard, EventTypeKit card, BusinessKit, AvailabilityComponents, InsightsComponents, etc.). The design's card is fixed: white surface, 1px #e5e7eb border, 16px (xl) radius, shadow-sm. Most Android copies hardcode CARD_RADIUS=16.dp locally (HubComponents) and replicate the border/shadow by hand, so radius/border/shadow can drift per screen. iOS centralizes this as the View.setupCard(radius:shadow:) modifier reused everywhere. **Fix:** Add a shared SchedulingCard composable or Modifier.schedulingCard() (appSurface, 1dp appBorder, Radii.xl, pantopusShadow .sm) and replace the per-file Card definitions so the surface contract is single-sourced like iOS setupCard.
- `med`/`chrome` — Wizard step chrome diverges from the design archetype. The onboarding-shell defines a numbered StepRail inside a card body: 22px numbered discs, check-on-done, 2px connectors, active-disc double ring, per-step labels, and a 'You're on step X of N' overline. iOS reproduces this exactly via WizardStepRail (WizardStepViews.swift). Android's shared WizardShell instead renders a continuous SegmentedProgressBar in the chrome plus a plain 'N of M' caption in the top bar — there are no numbered discs, no per-step labels, and no 'You're on step X of N' overline. **Fix:** Either add a WizardStepRail block composable (numbered discs + labels + overline) for scheduling onboarding/setup steps to match the design and iOS, or accept the segmented bar as an intentional Android-wide wizard idiom and confirm with design — but currently the scheduling wizards read materially different from the frames.
- `med`/`color` — Status-pill tone mapping is wrong/inconsistent on several Android variants vs the design+iOS spec. HubStatusPill colors 'Completed' with successBg/success green (design+iOS = neutral grey); MyBookings.StatusPill colors 'Pending' with infoBg/info blue (design+iOS = warning amber). The design grammar is: green=confirmed/active, amber=pending/draft, red=declined/no-show, neutral grey=cancelled/completed/past/paused/expired/etc. **Fix:** When consolidating onto a single SchedulingStatusPill, adopt the iOS tone table verbatim: pending/draft -> warning, confirmed/active -> success, declined/noShow -> error, and all terminal states (cancelled/completed/past/paused/secret/expired/unavailable/waitlisted) -> neutral grey.
- `low`/`color` — SlotPicker selected/today accent defaults to primary600 (sky) and SlotRow's chosen text uses primary700 regardless of pillar, whereas the design tints the selected slot / today disc with the host's pillar accent (e.g. Home green in home-shell). The accent param is plumbed through but several call sites and the chosen-text color fall back to sky rather than the pillar. **Fix:** Ensure every SlotTimeList/MonthCalendar call passes pillar.accent, and make the chosen-row text color derive from the accent (not hardcoded primary700) so Home/Business slots read green/violet as in the frames; iOS SchedulingSlotRow already takes accent for both fill and text.
- `low`/`sizing` — Toggle sizing is inconsistent across Android scheduling chrome: OwnerPillarChrome has no toggle, biz-kit-equivalent screens use Material3 Switch (HubComponents imports Switch/SwitchDefaults ~51x31), while the design + iOS use a compact 32x18 mini-toggle (SetupMiniToggle) for wizard rows and a 36x20 / 51x31 toggle for settings rows depending on surface. Android leans on the Material Switch default, which is visually heavier than the design's 32x18 wizard toggle. **Fix:** Add a shared SchedulingMiniToggle (32x18, pillar/accent fill, 14dp knob) mirroring iOS SetupMiniToggle for wizard/weekly-hours rows; reserve the larger toggle for settings rows to match the two design idioms.

## Setup

### A1 Scheduling Hub — iOS `major` / Android `minor` → better: **android**
- iOS files: `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Scheduling/Setup/Hub/SchedulingHubScreen.swift`, `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Scheduling/Setup/Hub/HubComponents.swift`, `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Scheduling/Setup/Hub/HubSummaryCard.swift`, `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Scheduling/Setup/Shared/SetupKit.swift`
- Android files: `frontend/apps/android/app/src/main/java/app/pantopus/android/ui/screens/scheduling/hub/SchedulingHubScreen.kt`, `frontend/apps/android/app/src/main/java/app/pantopus/android/ui/screens/scheduling/hub/HubComponents.kt`, `frontend/apps/android/app/src/main/java/app/pantopus/android/ui/screens/scheduling/hub/HubStates.kt`, `frontend/apps/android/app/src/main/java/app/pantopus/android/ui/screens/scheduling/hub/SummaryCard.kt`
- **Verdict:** Both platforms render the full A1 hub layout faithfully (pill band, booking-link card with live preview, pause/paused/read-only status rows, agenda, Manage chevron group, pinned footer) and all six frame states, but both inject an extra "THIS MONTH" A5 summary card at the top that the A1 design never shows; iOS additionally renders a back chevron and drops the trailing overflow-dots that the design's tab-root top bar specifies, which Android gets right.
- **Cross note:** Shared deviation: both platforms inject the A5 'THIS MONTH' summary card at the top of the loaded hub, which the A1 spec does not include; both otherwise cover all 6 frames (default/empty/skeleton/paused/home/permission-gated). Key divergence: Android renders the correct trailing more-horizontal/info overflow action in the top bar while iOS omits the trailing action entirely; both wrongly show a back chevron the tab-root design lacks.

**iOS deviations:**
- `high`/`chrome` — SetupTopBar is invoked with leading: .back, rendering a chevronLeft back button; the design's TopBar is a tab-root with an empty 36px leading spacer (no back chevron). **Fix:** Pass leading: .none so the leading control is Color.clear, matching the tab-root frame.
- `high`/`chrome` — trailingIcon is nil when canEdit, so the editable hub has no trailing action; the design always shows a more-horizontal overflow button in the top bar. **Fix:** Set trailingIcon: model.canEdit ? .moreHorizontal : .info and wire an overflow menu action.
- `med`/`extra-element` — loadedBody renders HubSummaryCard (the A5 'THIS MONTH' stats card) above the booking-link card; the A1 FrameDefault goes IdentityPills -> BookingLinkCard -> PauseRow with no summary card. **Fix:** Remove HubSummaryCard from the A1 hub (or gate it behind a separate A5 surface) to match the spec ordering.
- `low`/`icon` — Empty-state 'Connected calendars' placeholder uses .calendarClock; the design's collapsed placeholder and Manage row use calendar-sync. **Fix:** Use the calendarSync glyph for the Connected calendars placeholder row.
- `low`/`color` — HubPausedBanner background uses warningBg.opacity(0.4) to approximate the design's warningSoft (#fffbeb); the design uses a distinct dedicated soft-amber token, not a 40% tint. **Fix:** Use a warningSoft token rather than an opacity tint of warningBg.

**Android deviations:**
- `high`/`chrome` — HubTopBar leading is a ChevronLeft back button (testTag schedulingTopBarBack); the design's tab-root TopBar has an empty 36px leading spacer with no back chevron. **Fix:** Replace the leading ChevronLeft box with an empty 36dp Spacer/Box to match the tab-root frame.
- `med`/`extra-element` — HubLoadedBody renders SummaryCard (the A5 'THIS MONTH' stats block) above BookingLinkCard; the A1 FrameDefault has no summary card before the booking-link card. **Fix:** Remove SummaryCard from the A1 hub body to match the spec section ordering.
- `med`/`sizing` — HubPauseRow uses a Material3 Switch (~52x32dp track, large thumb); the design Toggle is a compact 32x18 track with a 14px thumb. **Fix:** Replace the Material3 Switch with a custom 32x18dp pill toggle matching SetupMiniToggle on iOS.
- `low`/`icon` — Business pill uses PantopusIcon.Briefcase; the design PILLAR.business icon is 'store'. **Fix:** Use a store/storefront glyph for the Business identity pill.
- `low`/`icon` — Empty-state placeholder rows use Grid3x3 and CalendarCog; the design uses layout-grid and calendar-sync for Event types / Connected calendars. **Fix:** Swap to layoutGrid and calendarSync glyphs to match the spec placeholders.
- `low`/`color` — HubPausedBanner uses warningBg as its fill; the design's PausedBanner background is warningSoft (#fffbeb), a lighter amber than warningBg (#fef3c7). **Fix:** Use a warningSoft token for the paused-banner background.

Both omit the 4th front-desk teammate and the step rail on the success screen.

**iOS deviations:**
- `med`/`typography` — Team-seats counter in OnboardingTeamList shows "\(seatedTeam.count) seated" but the design (TeamList) reads "3 of 5 seats used" — drops the plan-capacity copy. **Fix:** Change the trailing Text to "\(model.seatedTeam.count) of 5 seats used".

- `low`/`missing-element` — Success step (successBody) renders only WizardSuccessHero; design BizSuccess also shows the StepRail (all 4 done) above the hero. **Fix:** Render WizardStepRail with current=4/done=[1..4] above WizardSuccessHero on the success branch.
- `low`/`state` — Price field is gated behind model.paidEnabled, so it can be absent; design Field shows Price ($120) unconditionally beside Duration. **Fix:** Always render priceField in OnboardingServicePicker (or confirm paidEnabled defaults true for business).

**Android deviations:**
- `med`/`layout` — DurationStepperChips renders four 15/30/45/60 chips; design Field shows a single dropdown reading "30 min" with a chevron-down adornment. **Fix:** Replace the chip row with a dropdown/menu field mirroring iOS durationField (value text + ChevronDown).
- `med`/`sizing` — ServiceTile icon size = 18.dp inside the 30-icon-tile pattern; design ServiceTile glyph is width:15/height:15 (iOS uses 15). **Fix:** Set PantopusIconImage size = 15.dp in ServiceTile.
- `low`/`missing-element` — PriceField omits the trailing pencil adornment; design Field for Price has adorn="pencil" (iOS renders Icon(.pencil)). **Fix:** Add a trailing PantopusIcon.Pencil (14.dp, appTextMuted) after the BasicTextField.
- `low`/`missing-element` — Business team seeds only 3 teammates; design TeamList includes a 4th "Dana W." Front-desk (Not seated) row that demonstrates the front-desk role from the subcopy. **Fix:** Add Triple(SeededPerson("t4","Dana W.","Front desk","DW"),"FRONT DESK",false) to BUSINESS_TEAM.
- `low`/`missing-element` — OnboardingSuccess renders SuccessHeroBlock + link card only; design BizSuccess also keeps the StepRail (all done) above the hero. **Fix:** Render WizardStepRail(current=4, all done) above SuccessHeroBlock in OnboardingSuccess.
- `low`/`color` — Service/team divider uses appBorderSubtle (#f3f4f6); design TeamRow/ServiceTile borders use the stronger N.border (#e5e7eb / appBorder). **Fix:** Use PantopusColors.appBorder for the inter-row dividers in SeededPersonRow/InviteRow to match the design hairline.

- **Verdict:** iOS faithfully reproduces the 3-step Home wizard (chrome, step rail, headline 22/700, member list, mode tiles, RR rule, composed-availability card, layered success hero) with only minor nits; Android shares the same step content but adds an out-of-spec Home/Business flow toggle and renders the headline/subcopy and success hero at the wrong sizes/colors.

Key divergence: iOS reuses the spec-accurate WizardSuccessHero + WizardHeadline, while Android substitutes generic SuccessHeroBlock/HeadlineBlock/SubcopyBlock that drift on size and color, and Android adds an extra flow toggle the design does not have.

**iOS deviations:**
- `low`/`typography` — Step-2 collective sub in homeStep is hardcoded "Choose how members' availability turns into one set of bookable times." — spec HomeCollective sub is "Three members are scheduled. Choose how their availability turns into one set of bookable times." **Fix:** Make the step-2 sub conditional on combineMode like Android does (collective vs round-robin copy) to match the spec frames.
- `low`/`extra-element` — OnboardingMemberList loops with `if idx < members.count` so a divider Rectangle is also drawn after the last member, just above the invite row, yielding a double rule there vs the spec's single borderTop on the invite button. **Fix:** Change the guard to `idx < members.count - 1` so the trailing divider is the invite row's own top border only.
- `low`/`icon` — Mode tiles use generic SF-style glyphs (.users / .arrowsRepeat) where the spec draws bespoke CollectiveGlyph (overlapping circles w/ vesica) and RoundRobinGlyph (3 dots + dashed arc) at 40x26. **Fix:** Acceptable platform substitution; optionally add custom Shapes to match the spec diagrams if pixel parity is required.

**Android deviations:**
- `high`/`extra-element` — OnboardingHomeBusinessScreen renders OnboardingFlowSwitch (a Home/Business segmented toggle) on stepIndex==1; the design's Home onboarding (onboarding-home-frames.jsx) has no flow picker — it is a dedicated 3-step Home wizard launched with the Home pillar. **Fix:** Drop OnboardingFlowSwitch from the step-1 layout (resolve Home vs Business from the owner/route as iOS does), leaving only the PillarChip.
- `high`/`sizing` — Success uses SuccessHeroBlock: a flat 96dp successBg circle with a 48dp CheckCircle — spec SuccessHero is a layered 96px radial-gradient halo with a solid accent inner disc (~60px), a 32px white check, and a pillar drop-shadow (iOS WizardSuccessHero matches this). **Fix:** Render the success hero with the layered halo+inner-disc+white-check geometry (mirror WizardSuccessHero) instead of the generic flat-circle block.
- `med`/`color` — Success hero on Android paints the disc/icon with semantic green success (#059669) regardless of pillar; spec Home success uses the Home pillar accent #16A34A for the inner disc and shadow. **Fix:** Pass the pillar accent/accentBg into the success hero so the Home flow reads home-green, not generic success-green.
- `med`/`typography` — HeadlineBlock uses PantopusTextStyle.h2 (24sp/600) for the step titles; spec Headline is 22px/700 (iOS WizardHeadline uses 22/700). **Fix:** Use a 22sp Bold headline for these wizard steps (or a dedicated wizard headline style) instead of h2.
- `med`/`typography` — SubcopyBlock uses PantopusTextStyle.body (16sp) for the step sub-copy; spec Headline sub is 13.5px (iOS uses 13.5). **Fix:** Drop the wizard sub-copy to ~13.5sp with ~19px line height to match the spec and iOS.
- `low`/`color` — Member avatars use a flat appSurfaceSunken gray fill with appTextStrong initials; spec MemberRow uses per-member gradient avatars (iOS uses SchedulingHubModel.avatarTone). **Fix:** Apply per-member avatar tones/gradients instead of a single gray fill.

- **Verdict:** Both platforms faithfully reproduce the wizard chrome, StepRail, handle field (all slug states), type picker, hours grid and timezone chip; iOS is closer because Android's success hero uses a green check-circle on a flat successBg disc instead of the spec's sky-accent badge with radial-gradient ring + inner filled disc.
- **Cross note:** Both platforms omit the spec's Resume frame/banner (Frame 6) entirely — a shared cut, not a divergence. The real divergence is the success hero: iOS reproduces the sky radial-gradient badge with inner filled disc + white check, while Android substitutes a generic green check-circle on a flat successBg disc (wrong color, missing inner disc, wrong icon).

**iOS deviations:**
- `low`/`missing-element` — No Resume frame/banner: spec Frame 6 (FrameResume) shows a ResumeBanner (rotate-ccw disc, 'Pick up where you left off', steps 1-2 done) re-entering at step 3; FirstRunWizardModel always starts at .link with no resume path. **Fix:** If resume is in scope, add a ResumeBanner section above the headline when re-entering at step 3 with steps 1-2 done; otherwise accept as a shared cut.
- `low`/`icon` — WizardSuccessLinkCard / Copy chip border uses accentBg as the stroke color (overlay stroke(accentBg)) where the spec's copy chip border is primary100; visually near-identical for personal but technically off-token. **Fix:** Stroke the copy chip with Theme.Color.primary100 to match spec's 1px primary100 border.
- `low`/`sizing` — WizardStepRail active disc uses a double Circle().stroke overlay (2px accent + 26x26 accentBg ring) approximating the spec's 2px+2px focus ring; the outer accentBg ring is drawn as a stroke not a halo so it reads slightly thinner than the spec's box-shadow 0 0 0 4px primary100. **Fix:** Acceptable approximation; optionally widen the outer ring to lineWidth 2 on a 30x30 circle for a fuller halo.

**Android deviations:**
- `high`/`color` — SuccessHeroBlock paints the hero badge with PantopusColors.successBg (green tint) + PantopusColors.success green CheckCircle icon; spec SuccessHero is sky — radial-gradient primary50→primary100 ring with a primary600 filled inner disc and a white check (iOS does this correctly). **Fix:** Replace successBg/success with the pillar sky accent: outer 96dp gradient ring (primary50→primary100), inner filled disc in pillar.accent, white Check icon.
- `med`/`missing-element` — Android success badge has no inner filled disc + shadow: spec nests a 60px primary600 disc (with 0 8px 20px shadow) inside the 96px ring; SuccessHeroBlock draws a single flat 96dp circle with a 48dp icon directly on it. **Fix:** Add the inner ~60dp accent disc with a drop shadow inside the 96dp ring, matching iOS WizardSuccessHero's ZStack.
- `med`/`icon` — SuccessHeroBlock uses PantopusIcon.CheckCircle (a glyph with its own ring) at 48dp; spec/iOS use a bare Check stroke (strokeWidth 3) at 32dp inside the disc, so Android renders a double-ring look. **Fix:** Use PantopusIcon.Check at 32dp, white tint, inside the inner accent disc.
- `low`/`spacing` — SuccessHeroBlock wraps the hero in vertical Spacing.s8 (32dp) and spaces children by s4 (16dp); spec SuccessHero pads 24px top, 22px below the badge and 8px under the title — Android's uniform 16dp gaps compress the badge-to-title rhythm. **Fix:** Match spec rhythm: ~24dp top pad, 22dp under badge, 8dp under headline, 22dp under subcopy before the link card.
- `low`/`sizing` — WizardTypePicker LocationTile icon is 18dp on Android vs 15pt in the spec/iOS (the spec tile glyph is 15px in a 30px square); minor oversize. **Fix:** Set LocationTile PantopusIconImage size to 15.dp to match the spec/iOS.
- `low`/`chrome` — WizardTopBar trailing step readout renders '1 of 4'; spec TopBar shows '1/4' (slash form) and iOS matches with '\(current)/\(total)'. **Fix:** Render the readout as "${current}/${total}" to match the spec and iOS.
- `low`/`missing-element` — No Resume frame/banner (spec Frame 6) on Android either — FirstRunWizardViewModel starts at step 1 with no resume entry; shared gap with iOS. **Fix:** If resume is in scope, mirror a ResumeBanner above the headline at step 3; otherwise accept as a shared cut.

- `low`/`state` — NotifPauseBanner text is static 'Notifications paused' and its 'Resume' pill has no clickable/onClick; spec shows duration 'Paused for 2 hours', 'Resumes 11:42 AM · …' and a working Resume action. **Fix:** Wire the Resume pill to an unpause callback and surface the resume time/duration from the booking page.
- `low`/`color` — NotifPauseBanner uses warningBg/warningLight/warning (yellow #FFFBEB/#FDE68A/#D97706) instead of the spec's warm orange amber (#fff7ed/#fed7aa/#9a3412/#b45309). **Fix:** Use the warmer amber values for the banner band, circle, title and subtitle to match the spec hue.

### A5 Scheduling summary card — iOS `matches` / Android `minor` → better: **ios**
- iOS files: `/Users/yingpengwang/pantopus/native/pantopus/frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Scheduling/Setup/Hub/HubSummaryCard.swift`, `/Users/yingpengwang/pantopus/native/pantopus/frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Scheduling/Setup/Hub/SchedulingHubScreen.swift`, `/Users/yingpengwang/pantopus/native/pantopus/frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Scheduling/SharedUI/SchedulingIdentityTheme.swift`
- Android files: `/Users/yingpengwang/pantopus/native/pantopus/frontend/apps/android/app/src/main/java/app/pantopus/android/ui/screens/scheduling/hub/SummaryCard.kt`, `/Users/yingpengwang/pantopus/native/pantopus/frontend/apps/android/app/src/main/java/app/pantopus/android/ui/screens/scheduling/hub/SchedulingHubScreen.kt`, `/Users/yingpengwang/pantopus/native/pantopus/frontend/apps/android/app/src/main/java/app/pantopus/android/ui/screens/scheduling/_shared/OwnerPillarChrome.kt`
- **Verdict:** Both platforms reproduce the embedded summary card faithfully (4 stat cells + hairline dividers, sparkline, breakdown chips, period chips, "See insights"), with all four states; iOS mirrors the loading skeleton's full footprint exactly while Android's loading state drops the header/period and "See insights" shimmers and its in-hub Retry is a no-op.
- **Cross note:** Both correctly source pillar accents (sky/green/violet) from identity tokens and reuse the same stat-cell/sparkline/breakdown geometry; the key divergence is the loading skeleton — iOS reproduces the spec's full shimmer footprint (header + cells + sparkline + link) while Android's is partial, and Android's in-hub Retry is unwired.

**iOS deviations:**
- `low`/`color` — Card uses .setupCard(radius: Radii.xl) which matches spec radius 16 and shadow 0 1px 3px; delta vs-last-month threshold uses delta>=0 → success even when delta is 0, but spec shows up/down arrows only with a sign — cosmetic. **Fix:** Treat delta==0 as neutral (no arrow, fg1) to match spec's StatCell delta semantics.
- `low`/`spacing` — statCell uses spacing 3 + label fontSize 10.5 matching spec; divider height is 34 vs spec divider align-self:stretch (cells are ~taller), so the hairline is slightly shorter than the cell — negligible. **Fix:** Optionally make divider stretch to the row height instead of fixed 34pt.

**Android deviations:**
- `med`/`state` — SummaryLoading() renders only four stat shimmers + a 40dp sparkline box; it omits the spec loading frame's header shimmers (88×11 kicker + 120×26 period pill) and the trailing right-aligned 86×12 'See insights' shimmer, so the skeleton footprint doesn't mirror the loaded card. **Fix:** Add a header Row with two shimmer boxes (88×11, 120×26 pill) and a trailing 86×12 shimmer row, mirroring iOS loadingBody.
- `med`/`state` — In SchedulingHubScreen.HubLoadedBody the SummaryCard is given onRetry = { } (no-op), so the Error frame's Retry button does nothing, unlike iOS which calls model.refresh(). **Fix:** Wire onRetry to viewModel.load()/refresh() like the iOS hub does.
- `low`/`chrome` — For non-Data states SummaryHeader still renders a real 'THIS MONTH' kicker during Loading (showPeriod=false), whereas the spec's CardLoading replaces the whole header with shimmer rects. **Fix:** Skip SummaryHeader for the Loading branch and render header shimmers inside SummaryLoading instead.
- `low`/`color` — Card container uses RoundedCornerShape(16.dp) + 1dp border only, with no shadow; spec CardShell adds boxShadow 0 1px 3px rgba(0,0,0,0.06). **Fix:** Add a subtle shadow (e.g. PantopusShadow.sm / Modifier.shadow 1dp) to match the card elevation; use Radii.xl token instead of literal 16.dp.
- `low`/`sizing` — StatDivider height is 36dp vs iOS 34 and spec align-self:stretch; minor but the two platforms differ from each other by 2dp. **Fix:** Align divider height between platforms (or stretch to row height) per spec.

## Event types

### B1 Event types list — iOS `major` / Android `minor` → better: **android**
- iOS files: `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Scheduling/EventTypes/List/EventTypeListView.swift`, `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Scheduling/EventTypes/List/EventTypeListViewModel.swift`, `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Shared/ListOfRows/ListOfRowsView.swift`, `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Shared/ListOfRows/RowModel.swift`, `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Core/Design/Components/EmptyState.swift`
- Android files: `frontend/apps/android/app/src/main/java/app/pantopus/android/ui/screens/scheduling/eventtypes/EventTypeListScreen.kt`, `frontend/apps/android/app/src/main/java/app/pantopus/android/ui/screens/scheduling/eventtypes/EventTypeKit.kt`, `frontend/apps/android/app/src/main/java/app/pantopus/android/ui/screens/scheduling/eventtypes/EventTypeListViewModel.kt`, `frontend/apps/android/app/src/main/java/app/pantopus/android/ui/screens/shared/identity/IdentitySwitcherPillRow.kt`, `frontend/apps/android/app/src/main/java/app/pantopus/android/ui/screens/scheduling/_shared/OwnerPillarChrome.kt`
- **Verdict:** Android is a faithful bespoke build of the design's List-of-Rows event-type screen, while iOS forces the design into the generic ListOfRowsView shell and drops the screen's signature per-row toggle, the 6px dot row, the segmented Active/Hidden filter, the section overline, and the empty-state template chips.
- **Cross note:** Both omit the design's inline 'N hosts' users-badge on business rows (iOS VM notes the list DTO lacks an assignee count; Android EventTypeRowCard renders no hosts pill either) — a shared data-blocked gap, not a pure UI miss.

**iOS deviations:**
- `high`/`missing-element` — Design EventRow has a 36x20 product-blue Toggle as the primary trailing affordance; iOS row uses RowTrailing.kebab only (active/hidden buried in the overflow menu) so the inline toggle is absent. **Fix:** Add a per-row toggle: either a new RowTrailing case carrying the toggle, or render the toggle in the row trailing slot wired to viewModel.toggleHidden.
- `high`/`icon` — Design row leading is a 6px colored dot; iOS uses RowLeading.typeIcon = a 40pt rounded tinted location-icon tile (LeadingView renders 40x40), changing the entire row anatomy. **Fix:** Introduce a small color-dot leading variant (6pt) and drop the 40pt icon tile for this screen.
- `high`/`layout` — Design filter is a segmented Active/Hidden pill control (sunken track, white selected segment, blue700 label); iOS uses the shell's underline TabStrip (horizontal scroll, text+count+2px primary600 underline). **Fix:** Render a segmented control in the customHeader instead of relying on the shell tab strip, or add a segmented tab style to the shell.
- `med`/`missing-element` — Design draws a pillar-accented uppercase section overline ('Your event types' / 'Bookable services'); the VM builds RowSection with header:nil so no overline renders. **Fix:** Set RowSection.header to the pillar-accented overline string (and render it uppercase tinted with the pillar accent).
- `med`/`missing-element` — Design empty state (FrameEmpty) includes a 'START FROM A TEMPLATE' overline plus 15/30/60-min clock template chips below the CTA; iOS uses generic EmptyState which has only icon+headline+subcopy+CTA (VM comment acknowledges the gap). **Fix:** Extend EmptyContent/EmptyState with a template-chip row, or render a bespoke empty view for this screen.
- `med`/`chrome` — Design top bar is a centered 15pt-semibold title with a blue600 '+' (strokeWidth 2.4); iOS uses native navigationTitle (left/inline) and the shell tints the topBarAction icon appText, not primary600. **Fix:** Use a centered inline title and tint the + action primary600 to match the design's product-blue add affordance.
- `low`/`icon` — Design row overflow glyph is ellipsis-vertical; iOS RowTrailing.kebab renders .moreHorizontal (horizontal dots) at 20pt. **Fix:** Render ellipsis-vertical for the kebab in this row context.
- `low`/`sizing` — Design rows are individually-bordered 14px-radius cards spaced 8px apart; iOS .card section groups rows into one Radii.lg(12) card with hairline dividers, so radius and inter-row gap differ. **Fix:** Render free-standing 14pt-radius row cards with 8pt spacing rather than a single grouped card stack.

**Android deviations:**
- `med`/`extra-element` — Design FilterHeader shows a single static identity pill (small uppercase pill, pillar bg+text); Android renders a full-width 3-segment IdentitySwitcherPillRow (Personal/Home/Business) that fills the active segment with solid accent — a different, interactive control plus an extra Home option. **Fix:** Replace with EtIdentityPill (the static pillar pill already defined in EventTypeKit) to match the design, keeping owner switching elsewhere.
- `med`/`color` — SchedulingPillar.accentBg maps Personal to PantopusColors.primary50 (#f0f9ff); the design's personal pill/header bg is personalBg #dbeafe. **Fix:** Map Personal accentBg to the personalBg (#dbeafe) token used by the design.
- `low`/`sizing` — Design empty-state CTA is a content-hugging pill button; Android EtPrimaryButton is fillMaxWidth, so 'Create your first event type' spans full width. **Fix:** Render the empty-state CTA as a wrap-content pill rather than full-width.
- `low`/`color` — Design copied-toast check glyph is appTextInverse (white on dark pill); Android Toast tints the check PantopusColors.success (green). **Fix:** Tint the toast check icon appTextInverse to match the design's monochrome toast.
- `low`/`state` — Design includes Reordering (drag handles, lifted row) and Permission-gated (lock banner, disabled toggles) frames; Android covers populated/business/empty/all-hidden/loading/error but not reorder or the read-only gated banner (canEdit only disables controls). **Fix:** Add a reorder mode and a lock/read-only banner for non-owner catalogs to cover the remaining design frames.
- `low`/`sizing` — Design empty hero is an 84px gradient disc with a radial-gradient fill; Android uses an 84dp linear-gradient (primary50->primary100) disc — close but a linear rather than radial gradient. **Fix:** Use a radial gradient for the empty-state hero disc to match FrameEmpty.

### B2 Event type editor — iOS `major` / Android `major` → better: **ios**

### B3 Intake questions editor — iOS `major` / Android `major` → better: **android**
- iOS files: `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Scheduling/EventTypes/IntakeQuestions/IntakeQuestionsEditorView.swift`, `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Scheduling/EventTypes/IntakeQuestions/IntakeQuestionCard.swift`, `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Scheduling/EventTypes/IntakeQuestions/IntakeQuestionsEditorViewModel.swift`, `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Shared/Form/FormShell.swift`

- **Verdict:** Both platforms re-implement the design's bottom-sheet-over-dimmed-editor as a full-screen FormShell and both drop the drag-to-reorder handle, but Android matches the design's inline-EditGroup + segmented type selector + pillar subtitle far more faithfully, whereas iOS substitutes an accordion card, a Menu type picker, and arrow-button reordering.
- **Cross note:** Both platforms made the same two systemic substitutions: (1) full-screen FormShell instead of the design's bottom-sheet-over-dimmed-editor with grabber/scrim/pillar overline, and (2) no real drag-to-reorder grip handle (iOS uses up/down arrows, Android has none) so FrameReorder's lifted-row + dashed drop-slot is unimplemented on both. Divergence: Android faithfully reproduces the inline blue EditGroup, the 3-column segmented TypeSelector, the bordered required-toggle row, and the Save-question/secondary-button pair; iOS instead uses an accordion card + Menu dropdown + arrow reorder, drifting further from the Form field-group idiom.

**iOS deviations:**
- `med`/`chrome` — FormShell renders a full-screen routed editor with a centered title and no pillar overline/subtitle; design is a bottom sheet (grabber, 24px top radius, scrim, 'Personal · Intro call' accent overline above title, 'Done' trailing button). **Fix:** Present as a sheet (or at minimum pass subtitle: eventName) and tint an overline with the pillar accent; this is a deliberate full-screen port, accept chrome idiom but add the missing subtitle/overline.
- `high`/`interaction` — Custom rows expand via a chevron accordion (IntakeQuestionCard.header toggles isExpanded) and reorder via arrowUp/arrowDown footer buttons; design uses an inline blue EditGroup that replaces the row and a grip-vertical drag handle per row for drag-to-reorder. **Fix:** Replace the accordion+chevron with the design's inline EditGroup-replaces-row pattern and add a grip-vertical drag handle (DragGesture/onMove) instead of up/down arrows.
- `high`/`missing-element` — No grip-vertical drag handle on QuestionRow (design QuestionRow renders a 30×30 grip-vertical at trailing edge); reorder is arrow-button only. **Fix:** Add a trailing grip-vertical handle wired to drag reorder.
- `high`/`interaction` — Answer-type uses a SwiftUI Menu dropdown (typeMenu) rather than the design's 3-column segmented TypeSelector grid (sunken track, 30px cells, selected = white surface + blue700, radius 7). **Fix:** Replace the Menu with a 3-column segmented control matching TypeSelector geometry.
- `med`/`missing-element` — EditGroup is missing the design's 'Save question' primary button and red 'Delete' text button row; iOS edits live-bind with only a footer Delete and no explicit Save-this-question CTA. **Fix:** Add a 'Save question' blue button + red Delete row to the expanded editor.
- `med`/`color` — Expanded editor uses plain appSurface card (IntakeQuestionCard background) instead of the design EditGroup's blue50 fill with 1.5px blue200 border; the active/editing affordance is lost. **Fix:** Give the expanded/editing state a primary50 background and 1.5px primary200 border.
- `low`/`extra-element` — 'Make this required' uses a bare SwiftUI Toggle row, not the design's bordered white surface row (1px border, radius 8, 9/11px padding) containing the label + toggle. **Fix:** Wrap the toggle in a bordered surface row matching the spec.
- `low`/`icon` — Per-row delete affordance is only present in the expanded footer; collapsed QuestionRow shows no inline trash-2 (design shows a trash-2 button on every row beside the grip). **Fix:** Add an always-visible trash-2 delete icon to the collapsed row.

**Android deviations:**
- `med`/`chrome` — IntakeContent uses full-screen FormShell (centered title + subtitle = eventName, 'Done' action) rather than the design bottom sheet (grabber, 24px radius, scrim, pillar accent overline 'Personal · Intro call'). Subtitle is present but uncolored/not an overline. **Fix:** Accept full-screen port but render the subtitle as a pillar-accent overline ('Personal · {name}') above the title, or present as a sheet.
- `high`/`missing-element` — QuestionRow has no grip-vertical drag handle and the screen exposes no reorder affordance at all (only onEdit click + a trailing trash-2); design FrameReorder shows active grip handles, a lifted row, and a dashed drop slot. **Fix:** Add a trailing grip-vertical handle and implement drag reorder (reorderable list); add the lifted-row shadow + dashed placeholder states.
- `med`/`layout` — QuestionRow is drawn as a standalone white card with 1px border + 12px radius; design QuestionRow is a flat row inside the single white ListBlock card separated by 1px bottom borders (no per-row card/border). **Fix:** Render custom questions as flat rows with bottom dividers inside one card, matching the locked-defaults card treatment.
- `med`/`state` — FrameReorder lifted-row (heavy shadow, scale 1.015, rounded) and the dashed blue200 drop-slot placeholder are not implemented anywhere. **Fix:** Add the drag-lifted styling and a 52px dashed blue200/blue50 drop-slot placeholder during reorder.
- `low`/`interaction` — EditGroup secondary action is a 'Cancel' text button; design uses a red 'Delete' button (trash-2 + 'Delete', color E.error) as the secondary action in the edit field group. **Fix:** Change the secondary action to a red trash-2 'Delete' button to match the spec (Cancel can stay as well, but Delete is the speced affordance).
- `low`/`spacing` — Helper caption uses Spacing.s2 (8) item spacing and the 'YOUR QUESTIONS' group label sits with top = Spacing.s2 (8); design GroupLabel margin is 14px top / 4px bottom. **Fix:** Set the group-label top margin to ~14dp to match the design rhythm.

- `med`/`missing-element` — Helper line 'Connect a calendar to check for conflicts and add bookings automatically.' (spec fontSize 11.5, fg3) is missing. **Fix:** Add the helper Text above the provider rows in the empty/connect state.

## Availability

### C Availability schedules — iOS `major` / Android `minor` → better: **android**
- iOS files: `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Scheduling/Availability/ScheduleList/AvailabilityScheduleListView.swift`, `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Scheduling/Availability/ScheduleList/AvailabilityScheduleListViewModel.swift`, `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Shared/ListOfRows/ListOfRowsView.swift`

- **Verdict:** Android renders the spec per-card list, vertical-ellipsis kebab, boxed info note and two-row matching skeleton faithfully, while iOS delegates to the generic ListOfRowsView shell and diverges on card grouping, icon/title sizing, kebab glyph, skeleton, and the single-schedule note.

**iOS deviations:**
- `high`/`layout` — ListOfRowsView section style .card merges all schedules into one shared card with hairline dividers; spec ScheduleRow is a separate white card per schedule with 10px gap. **Fix:** Render each schedule as its own standalone card with 10pt gap.
- `high`/`icon` — Row kebab uses .moreHorizontal (horizontal dots); spec uses a vertical ellipsis (ellipsis-vertical, 18px, fg4) at top-right. **Fix:** Switch the kebab glyph to a vertical ellipsis.
- `high`/`state` — Loading shows six shimmer rows with a 40px circular avatar; spec is two skeleton rows with a 36px rounded-square icon block. **Fix:** Render two skeletons matching the row geometry with a 36pt md-radius block.
- `med`/`missing-element` — Single-schedule note renders as plain section footer text with no info icon and no raised card; spec note is a raised bordered card with a 14px info icon. **Fix:** Render the note as a bordered raised card with a leading info icon.
- `med`/`sizing` — Row icon tile is 40x40 with a 19-20px glyph and title uses body 16pt; spec tile is 36x36 with 18px glyph and name about 13.5pt. **Fix:** Use a 36pt tile, 18pt glyph, and 13.5pt semibold name.
- `med`/`color` — Top-bar add action draws the plus in appText; spec plus is blue600. **Fix:** Tint the add icon primary600.
- `low`/`sizing` — Grouped card uses Radii.lg (12) radius; spec ScheduleRow radius is 16. **Fix:** Use a 16pt corner radius.
- `low`/`extra-element` — helperHeader is always rendered, including on Empty and Error; spec omits the helper line on the Empty frame. **Fix:** Hide the helper line on empty and error states.

**Android deviations:**
- `low`/`typography` — Summary plus timezone renders in one fg3 color; spec bolds the timezone in fg2 with an fg4 separator. **Fix:** Bold the tz segment (appTextStrong) and tint the separator appTextMuted.
- `low`/`sizing` — Top bar is 52dp tall with a 22dp chevron and 16sp title; spec bar is 46px, 20px chevron, 15px title. **Fix:** Use a 46dp bar, 20dp chevron, 15sp title.
- `low`/`state` — Skeleton row omits the small trailing kebab shimmer bar the spec includes. **Fix:** Add a thin trailing shimmer bar.
- `low`/`chrome` — Top bar lacks the spec 1px bottom border under the bar. **Fix:** Add a 1px appBorder bottom divider under the top bar.

- `high`/`missing-element` — Entire screen absent on iOS: no embed-type segmented control (Inline/Popup/Floating), no Appearance card (brand color/theme/hide-header/button-label/calendar-layout), no <script> embed-snippet block with Copy snippet, no 'Show inline on /b/yourname' toggle, and no live preview pane. **Fix:** This is a web-only host-settings archetype (desktop two-column block editor); confirm with design whether a native mobile equivalent is in scope before building — likely intentionally web-only.

**Android deviations:**
- `high`/`missing-element` — Entire screen absent on Android: same as iOS — no segmented embed-type switcher, Appearance card, code-snippet/Copy snippet block, 'Show inline' toggle, or live preview. ShareLinkSheet.kt is a separate C3 'Share your link' bottom sheet (URL/QR/share targets), not the embed settings screen. **Fix:** Web-only archetype; confirm scope with design. If a mobile port is wanted, model it as a Form/settings screen rather than the desktop two-column+preview layout.

### C One-off booking link — iOS `minor` / Android `major` → better: **ios**
- iOS files: `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Scheduling/BookingPage/OneOffLinkGeneratorView.swift`, `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Scheduling/BookingPage/BookingPageSupport.swift`
- Android files: `frontend/apps/android/app/src/main/java/app/pantopus/android/ui/screens/scheduling/bookingpage/OneOffLinkGeneratorScreen.kt`, `frontend/apps/android/app/src/main/java/app/pantopus/android/ui/screens/scheduling/bookingpage/BookingPageComponents.kt`, `frontend/apps/android/app/src/main/java/app/pantopus/android/ui/screens/scheduling/bookingpage/ShareLinkSheet.kt`
- **Verdict:** iOS faithfully reproduces the bottom-sheet form (no chrome, grabber from parent, all four states) with only minor spacing/sizing nits, while Android adds a non-spec top bar with a close button and converts the wrapping chip groups to horizontal-scroll rows.
- **Cross note:** Both platforms color the generate-error note copy with the flat error token (#DC2626) instead of the spec's darker #991b1b/#b91c1c reds, and both default the pillar chip to Personal; the key divergence is Android's extra top-bar/close-button chrome and horizontal-scroll chip rows versus iOS's spec-accurate grabber sheet with wrapping chips.

**iOS deviations:**
- `low`/`sizing` — OneOffShareTile uses frame(maxWidth:.infinity).aspectRatio(1) so each share tile fills its full third of the row; spec ShareTarget caps the square tile at maxWidth 54px and centers it. **Fix:** Constrain the tile square to .frame(maxWidth:54) and center it in the column.
- `low`/`spacing` — generatedCard VStack spacing is Spacing.s4 (16); the spec GeneratedSheet uses gap:13 between hero/url/meta/send-via blocks. **Fix:** Use a 13pt spacing in the generated VStack to match the spec.
- `low`/`color` — OneOffGenerateErrorNote colors the title with Theme.Color.error (#DC2626) for both lines; spec uses #991b1b title / #b91c1c body (darker reds). **Fix:** Introduce darker error-fg tokens for the note title/body, or accept as a non-palette nuance.
- `low`/`missing-element` — Error frame in spec replaces the lower form with just an inline 'Generate link' button after the error note; iOS keeps the full configuring form plus the pinned generate bar (no second inline button), a slightly different error layout. **Fix:** Acceptable since the pinned bar still affords retry; optionally collapse the form when generateError is set to mirror the spec frame.

**Android deviations:**
- `high`/`extra-element` — OneOffTopBar renders a 32dp X close button row at the top; the spec is a bottom sheet with only a grabber and has no top bar or close button (header is title + pillar chip only). **Fix:** Remove OneOffTopBar; present the screen as a ModalBottomSheet with a drag handle so dismissal matches the spec.
- `med`/`layout` — ExpiryChips and ChipScrollRow wrap their pills in Modifier.horizontalScroll(); the spec Chips group uses flexWrap:wrap, so '24 hours / 7 days / 30 days / No expiry' should wrap to a second line on 360-wide, not scroll horizontally. **Fix:** Replace the horizontalScroll Rows with a FlowRow (wrapping) layout at 7dp spacing.
- `med`/`icon` — OptionsCard 'Single use' row uses PantopusIcon.Tag; the spec OptionsCard uses the 'ticket' glyph (the MetaChip already uses Ticket). **Fix:** Switch the Single-use row icon to PantopusIcon.Ticket.
- `low`/`icon` — ErrorNote 'Try again' uses PantopusIcon.RefreshCw; the spec uses 'rotate-ccw'. **Fix:** Use a rotate-ccw / counter-clockwise glyph for the retry affordance.
- `low`/`layout` — ConfigBody places the generate-error ErrorNote last (after Options); the spec error frame positions the inline error note directly after Event type, above Availability. **Fix:** Render cfg.error between the Event type and Availability sections to match the spec order.
- `low`/`spacing` — MetaChip uses vertical Spacing.s1 (4dp); spec MetaChip padding is 6px vertical. **Fix:** Use 6dp vertical padding on the MetaChip row.
- `low`/`state` — BLHeaderPill is hardcoded to SchedulingPillar.Personal; spec accent follows the host pillar (Personal sky / Business violet) and iOS drives it from viewModel.theme. **Fix:** Pass the host's resolved pillar into BLHeaderPill instead of the literal Personal.
- `low`/`typography` — ErrorNote title/body are colored PantopusColors.error (#DC2626) for both lines; spec uses #991b1b title / #b91c1c body. **Fix:** Use darker error text tokens for the note copy.

### C Share booking link — iOS `matches` / Android `minor` → better: **ios**
- iOS files: `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Scheduling/SharedUI/ShareLinkSheet.swift`, `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Core/Design/Radii.swift`, `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Core/Design/Shadows.swift`

- **Verdict:** Both platforms faithfully reproduce all five spec frames (default, draft, copied toast, QR fullscreen, regenerate confirm) with correct sections, order, tokens and icons; iOS matches the spec almost exactly while Android has a handful of minor radius/icon/color nits and an unscannable QR.
- **Cross note:** Both platforms diverge identically on the draft-banner headline color (#92400e in spec); iOS renders a real scannable CoreImage QR while Android's QR is a decorative synthetic grid.

**iOS deviations:**
- `low`/`color` — draftBanner headline uses Theme.Color.appText (#111827) but spec sets banner ink to dark amber #92400e and border to WARNING_BORDER #FDE68A (iOS uses warning.opacity(0.4) for the border). **Fix:** Use a #92400e-equivalent token for the banner headline and the warningLight (#FDE68A) token for the border stroke.
- `low`/`state` — Regenerate confirm uses a native SwiftUI .alert rather than the spec's centered card with a 44px red-circle rotate-ccw medallion and a red Regenerate button; acceptable native idiom but loses the medallion/destructive styling. **Fix:** Optional: render a custom centered confirm card to match the icon medallion + destructive button treatment, as Android does.

**Android deviations:**
- `med`/`icon` — RegenerateButton and RegenerateConfirmDialog use PantopusIcon.RefreshCw (clockwise) but spec specifies rotate-ccw (counter-clockwise) in both places. **Fix:** Swap to a RotateCcw / rotate-ccw glyph to match the spec intent.
- `low`/`sizing` — UrlCard Copy button uses RoundedCornerShape(Radii.md)=8dp vs spec borderRadius 10; QR thumb plate uses Radii.md=8 vs spec 10; 'Show QR' pill uses Radii.md=8 vs spec 9. **Fix:** Use a 10dp radius for the Copy button and QR plate and 9-10dp for the Show QR pill instead of Radii.md.
- `low`/`color` — DraftBanner headline text is PantopusColors.warning (#D97706) but spec uses dark amber #92400e for the banner copy. **Fix:** Introduce/use a #92400e token for the draft-banner headline text.
- `low`/`color` — SettingsCard toggle-row divider (BLToggleRow) uses PantopusColors.appBorderSubtle (#f3f4f6) but spec uses E.border (#e5e7eb). **Fix:** Use the appBorder (#e5e7eb) token for the inter-row divider.
- `low`/`interaction` — ShareLinkSheet toggles (showOnProfile/addToSignature) are local mutableState only and not surfaced via callbacks, so changes don't persist (iOS exposes onToggleShowOnProfile/onToggleSignature callbacks). **Fix:** Hoist the two toggle states to callbacks/parameters so the presenting screen can persist them, matching iOS.
- `low`/`other` — QR on both the thumb and fullscreen is a synthetic decorative grid (qrCells, not scannable), whereas iOS generates a real CoreImage QR; spec QR is decorative so acceptable but functionally weaker. **Fix:** Optional: generate a real QR (e.g. ZXing) so 'Point a camera here' actually works.

(credit-card). **Fix:** Remove the 'Preview your page' row from LinksCard (or surface preview elsewhere) so the card matches the spec's 2-row layout.

- **Verdict:** Both platforms reproduce the picker chrome + loading skeleton + a single no-availability card faithfully, but each collapses the design's five distinct slot-states (notably the team-"composing" caption and the framed Home composed-empty card with Free/Busy member dots + explainer pill) into one generic empty state, so both are major; iOS edges ahead because its EmptyCard supports the spec's secondary CTA + count chip while Android's primary no-availability card drops the secondary action entirely.

- `high`/`missing-element` — Frame 5 composed-empty (Home intersect) is absent: SlotPicker.swift has no framed soft-tinted (p.soft + accent33 border) card, no Free/Busy member-dot row, and no calendar-x variant — only a generic dashed no-availability card. **Fix:** Add a framed variant to SlotPickerEmptyCard (soft bg, accent-tinted border, white halo) plus the three-member Free/Busy avatar row for the Home collective-intersect empty state.

- `med`/`state` — The two distinct empty frames (no-times-in-range vs no-times-anywhere) are collapsed: noAvailabilityCard only renders the 'no times in month' copy with a See-next-month CTA and 'Get notified' secondary; the 'No times are open right now' / 'Notify me' + 'Join waitlist' + '3 waiting' chip variant is never produced. **Fix:** Add a second LoadState (or flag) for the truly-empty case with bell-primary, waitlist secondary, and count chip.
- `med`/`icon` — Spec uses calendar-search for no-times-in-range, but noAvailabilityCard passes .calendarClock (a code comment concedes calendar-search was unavailable); separately .calendarSearch in Icons.swift maps to a bare magnifyingglass SF symbol, losing the calendar glyph intent. **Fix:** Use .calendarSearch and remap it to calendar.badge SF symbol so the empty-range card shows a calendar-search glyph.
- `low`/`layout` — dayFullCard (SlotPicker.swift) is a borderless centered icon+text+link with s8 vertical padding, not the spec's dashed-border card with 44pt halo, bold title and body line used by the composed-empty/day-full framing. **Fix:** Wrap dayFullCard in the same dashed RoundedRectangle(Radii.xl) card geometry as the empty card for visual consistency.
- `low`/`typography` — Empty-card title uses .system(size:15,weight:.bold) but design title line-height is 20px and max-width 230; without explicit lineSpacing the two-line Home title ('Everyone's calendars don't overlap…') may not match the 20px leading. **Fix:** Set lineSpacing to hit 20pt and clamp width to ~230 to match spec wrapping.

**Android deviations:**
- `high`/`missing-element` — Frame 5 composed-empty is absent: NoAvailabilityState.kt only draws a dashed surface card; no framed soft-tinted (pillar.soft + accent33 border) variant, no white halo, and no three-member Free/Busy avatar-dot row for the Home intersect case. **Fix:** Add a framed parameter to NoAvailabilityState (soft bg + accent border + white circle halo) and a MemberFreeBusyRow composable.
- `high`/`missing-element` — Frame 2 composing is absent in SlotPickerScreen.kt: the SlotRegion loading branch shows only DiscoverySkeletonSlots — no AvatarCluster + 'Finding times that work for everyone' caption and no ComposedPill (calendar-range icon, accent-soft tinted pill). **Fix:** Add a composing caption + ComposedPill above the skeleton when the host is collective/Home.
- `high`/`missing-element` — The month-empty NoAvailabilityState call site (SlotPickerScreen.kt line 438) passes no secondaryLabel/onSecondary, so the spec's 'Get notified when times open' bell secondary button (frame 3) and the 'Join waitlist' + '3 waiting' chip (frame 4) never render — only the primary See-next-month button shows. **Fix:** Pass secondaryLabel/onSecondary (and a count-chip slot) so the no-range and no-anywhere variants carry their secondary CTA + chip.
- `med`/`icon` — For no-times-in-range Android passes PantopusIcon.CalendarX, but the spec uses calendar-search for that frame (calendar-x is reserved for the composed-empty frame 5); the intent glyph is wrong. **Fix:** Use PantopusIcon.CalendarSearch for the month-empty card and reserve CalendarX for the composed-empty state.
- `med`/`extra-element` — SlotPickerScreen.kt adds a 'Pick a day with open times' empty state (selectedDay == null) that has no design frame, and a 'No times left this day' DayFullyBookedNotice whose body copy ('Every slot on this day is booked.') diverges from spec which keeps day-full inside the picker rather than a separate dashed card. **Fix:** Confirm the selectedDay==null branch matches a design state; align day-full copy/treatment with the spec's calm inline framing.

- `high`/`missing-element` — No group-event card: BookerLandingContent only defines EventTypeRow; the spec's GroupEventCard (fixed-time tile, '4 of 8 spots left' / 'Fully booked' pill, 'Save your spot' CTA, 'Join waitlist' secondary) is absent. **Fix:** Add a GroupEventCard composable mirroring the spec for group/seated event types.
- `high`/`missing-element` — No team cluster or composed pill: HostAvatar is single-disc only and there is no ComposedPill; spec FrameTeam needs the 3-avatar overlapping cluster, 'Meet with the team' headline, and the violet 'Round-robin' explainer pill. **Fix:** Render an overlapping multi-avatar cluster + ComposedPill for team/round-robin pages.
- `high`/`missing-element` — LandingFooter omits the 'View {name}'s profile' link with arrow-up-right icon; it renders only the 'Powered by Pantopus' row. Spec Footer shows both. **Fix:** Add a primary600 'View {hostName}'s profile' button with PantopusIcon.ArrowUpRight above the Powered-by row.
- `med`/`extra-element` — In LandingLoaded the OpenInAppBanner is rendered unconditionally for every loaded page (including single-type, paused, and empty), but the spec shows the open-in-app banner only on the multi-type default frame (FrameMulti) and never on single/paused/empty. **Fix:** Show OpenInAppBanner only when eventTypes.size > 1 and not paused/empty (mirror iOS's count>1 gate).
- `med`/`extra-element` — SectionOverline('Book a time') is rendered above the paused and empty in-card states (it sits outside the when-branch), but spec FramePaused/FrameEmpty place the card directly in ListArea with no section label. **Fix:** Move the 'Book a time' overline inside the else (event-list) branch so it doesn't show in paused/empty.
- `med`/`state` — Paused/unavailable maps to BookerLandingUiState.Terminal → full-screen PausedExpiredUnavailableState with a 'Go back' button, diverging from spec FramePaused which keeps the banner+header and shows a calm in-list paused card (moon icon, 'This page isn't taking bookings right now'). **Fix:** Route paused into the in-list LandingPausedCard within the normal landing scaffold instead of a separate full-screen terminal state.
- `low`/`icon` — LandingPausedCard uses PantopusIcon.PauseCircle and LandingEmptyCard uses PantopusIcon.CalendarX, whereas spec uses 'moon' (paused) and 'calendar-off' (empty). **Fix:** Switch paused icon to a moon glyph and empty icon to calendar-off to match the spec intent.
- `low`/`color` — PillarBanner uses a 2-stop linear gradient (e.g. primary400→primary800) while the spec banner is a 3-stop gradient (light 0% → accent 58% → dark 100%), making the Android banner read flatter/darker. **Fix:** Use a 3-stop brush (primary300/400 → primary600 → primary800) to match the spec banner ramp.

### C2 Slot picker — iOS `minor` / Android `minor` → better: **ios**
- iOS files: `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Scheduling/Invitee/Discovery/DiscoverySlotPickerView.swift`, `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Scheduling/SharedUI/SlotPicker.swift`, `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Scheduling/SharedUI/SchedulingSlotRow.swift`, `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Scheduling/Invitee/Discovery/DiscoverySupport.swift`
- Android files: `frontend/apps/android/app/src/main/java/app/pantopus/android/ui/screens/scheduling/invitee/discovery/SlotPickerScreen.kt`, `frontend/apps/android/app/src/main/java/app/pantopus/android/ui/screens/scheduling/_shared/SlotPicker.kt`, `frontend/apps/android/app/src/main/java/app/pantopus/android/ui/screens/scheduling/invitee/discovery/NoAvailabilityState.kt`, `frontend/apps/android/app/src/main/java/app/pantopus/android/ui/screens/scheduling/invitee/discovery/DiscoveryComponents.kt`, `frontend/apps/android/app/src/main/java/app/pantopus/android/ui/screens/scheduling/invitee/discovery/SlotPickerViewModel.kt`
- **Verdict:** Both platforms faithfully reproduce the stacked summary-header + month-calendar + Morning/Afternoon slot-row layout with correct accent/today/selected styling; iOS edges ahead because it renders the DST/timezone-change hint (absent on Android) while Android adds a non-spec docked Continue bar, though iOS in turn under-builds the day-full card.
- **Cross note:** Both share the same MonthCalendar/slot-row geometry and both correctly omit in-screen reschedule-banner and slot-taken-toast frames (those live in separate Reschedule/SlotTaken screens). The key divergence: iOS renders the DST hint but Android drops it entirely; Android adds a Continue bar absent from the spec default while iOS keeps the tap-to-advance model but under-builds the day-full card.

**iOS deviations:**
- `low`/`color` — infoCaption (SlotPicker.swift:150) renders the DST hint text in appTextSecondary gray with no border and Radii.sm (6) corners, vs spec's INFO #0369A1 text, INFO_BORDER #BAE6FD 1px border, and 11px radius on an INFO_BG card. **Fix:** Use Theme.Color.info for text, add a 1px info-border, and bump the corner radius to ~11 to match the spec's tz-hint banner.
- `med`/`missing-element` — dayFullCard (SlotPicker.swift:207-221) is a bare centered icon + one line + link, omitting the spec QuietNotice's dashed-border card, circular icon halo, and body copy 'Every slot on this day is booked.' **Fix:** Render day-full with the same dashed-border + circle-halo card shape used for noAvailabilityCard, including the body line.
- `low`/`icon` — noAvailabilityCard (SlotPicker.swift:228) uses .calendarClock as a stand-in; spec frame 4 uses calendar-off and the day-full spec uses calendar-x. **Fix:** Add calendar-off / calendar-x glyphs to PantopusIcon and use them per frame.
- `low`/`spacing` — Summary tile uses Spacing.s3 (12) for both axes; spec is padding 11px 12px and adds a shadow-sm, which iOS omits (border only). **Fix:** Use 11pt vertical padding and add the shadow-sm drop shadow on the summary card and calendar card.

**Android deviations:**
- `med`/`missing-element` — SlotPickerUiState.Content (SlotPickerViewModel.kt:285) has no dstHint field and SummaryHeader (SlotPickerScreen.kt:216) never renders the timezone/DST info banner from spec frame 5 ('Clocks change this weekend — times are adjusted.'). **Fix:** Add a dstHint string to Content and render an INFO_BG/INFO-border caption under the timezone chip when present, mirroring iOS.
- `med`/`extra-element` — A docked ContinueBar (SlotPickerScreen.kt:202-210, 486) appears after a slot is chosen; the spec's default/day-with-slots frame has no footer and advances on the row's chosen check-circle state — only the reschedule-cutoff frame has a footer ('Message host'). **Fix:** Confirm the booking flow truly needs a Continue CTA; the spec selects-then-advances, so consider removing the bar or aligning it to a spec'd footer.
- `low`/`missing-element` — DiscoverySkeletonSlots (DiscoveryComponents.kt:149) draws only a leading icon shimmer + time bar, omitting the spec SkelSlotRow's trailing chevron square that iOS includes. **Fix:** Add a trailing Spacer + 16x16 shimmer square to match the loaded row geometry.
- `low`/`spacing` — Summary tile (SlotPickerScreen.kt:228) uses Spacing.s3 (12) on both axes and no shadow; spec is padding 11px 12px with shadow-sm on the white cards. **Fix:** Use 11dp vertical padding and add an elevation/shadow to the summary and calendar cards.
- `low`/`typography` — MonthCalendarCard month title and DayHeading use PantopusTextStyle.small (14sp) at FontWeight.Bold; spec month title is 13.5px/700 and day heading 13px/700, so they render slightly larger than the design. **Fix:** Use a 13-13.5sp bold inline size for the month title and day heading to match the spec scale.

- **Verdict:** Both render the success/pending hero, summary card, receipt, calendar cluster, manage note and dock faithfully; iOS is closer (correct 104/80 halo, confetti, sending-receipt shimmer) while Android shrinks the halo, drops confetti and the receipt sending state, uses the wrong manage icon, and shows the account nudge on every variant.

**iOS deviations:**
- `med`/`missing-element` — receiptCapsule in InviteeConfirmedView omits the spec's monospace TXN/timestamp line (ReceiptCapsule renders 'TXN_4F9C20A1 · Jun 13, 2026 · 9:41 AM' above the divider). **Fix:** Add a Theme.Color.appTextSecondary monospaced 10pt line with the transaction id + date below the amount row.
- `low`/`sizing` — ConfirmPrimaryButton uses frame(height: 48) but the spec Dock primary button is height:46. **Fix:** Set the dock CTA height to 46 to match the spec.
