- `low`/`color` — Hero body uses Theme.Color.appTextStrong (fg2 #374151) which matches spec E.fg2; acceptable — no change needed but verify against fg3 usages elsewhere. **Fix:** No change; documented for completeness.

**Android deviations:**
- `med`/`sizing` — ConfirmHalo uses size 96dp outer / 74dp inner, but the spec Halo is 104 outer / 80 inner with a third pulse ring. **Fix:** Resize the halo to 104dp/80dp and add the soft pulsing outer ring.
- `high`/`state` — ReceiptCapsule only handles paid/deposit; the spec's 'sending' mode (shimmer bar + mail icon, frame FrameEmailSending) and PriceMode enum (Free/Full/Deposit) have no Sending case, so the email-sending variant is unreachable. **Fix:** Add a sending/processing mode that swaps mail-check for mail and renders a shimmer line instead of 'Receipt emailed'.
- `med`/`missing-element` — ReceiptCapsule omits the spec's monospace TXN/timestamp line ('TXN_4F9C20A1 · Jun 13, 2026 · 9:41 AM') shown above the divider. **Fix:** Add a monospace appTextSecondary caption line with the transaction id and date below the amount row.
- `med`/`icon` — ManageNote uses PantopusIcon.CalendarClock, but the spec ManageNote icon is settings-2 (a gear). **Fix:** Switch the manage-note leading icon to a settings/gear glyph to match settings-2.
- `med`/`extra-element` — AccountNudge is rendered unconditionally in ConfirmedBody, but the spec only shows NudgeCard on the free confirmed frame (paid/deposit/credit/pending frames have no nudge). **Fix:** Gate AccountNudge to the free, signed-out, non-pending variant only.
- `low`/`interaction` — No confetti is played on mount; the spec fires ConfettiSpray on confirmed (non-pending) frames (suppressed under reduced motion). **Fix:** Add a confetti overlay on the confirmed body, disabled when the system reduce-motion setting is on.
- `low`/`missing-element` — No CreditUsedRow (ticket-check 'session credit used') for the package-credit-redeemed frame, and no AppBanner/RedirectPill variants exist. **Fix:** Add a credit-used capsule and the app-user/redirect variants if those frames are in scope.
- `low`/`color` — ApprovalEtaPill tints icon+text with PantopusColors.info; spec EtaPill info tone uses INFO_DK (#0369A1, primary700) for the foreground text, not the brighter info blue. **Fix:** Use primary700 for the ETA pill text/icon to match the darker info-tone foreground.

### D Intake booking form (invitee) — iOS `minor` / Android `major` → better: **ios**
- iOS files: `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Scheduling/Invitee/Confirm/InviteeIntakeFormView.swift`, `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Scheduling/Invitee/Confirm/InviteeIntakeFormViewModel.swift`, `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Scheduling/Invitee/Confirm/ConfirmSupport.swift`
- Android files: `frontend/apps/android/app/src/main/java/app/pantopus/android/ui/screens/scheduling/invitee/confirm/IntakeFormScreen.kt`, `frontend/apps/android/app/src/main/java/app/pantopus/android/ui/screens/scheduling/invitee/confirm/InviteeConfirmFlow.kt`, `frontend/apps/android/app/src/main/java/app/pantopus/android/ui/screens/scheduling/invitee/confirm/ConfirmComponents.kt`, `frontend/apps/android/app/src/main/java/app/pantopus/android/ui/screens/scheduling/invitee/confirm/InviteeConfirmModels.kt`
- **Verdict:** iOS faithfully reproduces all key intake frames (default/prefilled-chip/errors/expired) with only small CTA-sizing and a missing existing-account banner; Android omits the entire prefilled "Booking as" chip + "Not you?" path and the existing-account InfoBanner, and hardcodes the phone field into "Your info" instead of the host-questions section.
- **Cross note:** Both platforms use the correct token palette (sky/primary accent, error/warn/info tones, 8dp input radius, 44dp inputs, alert-circle/check-circle validation icons) and both reproduce the summary card, hold row, validation errors, and add-guests collapsed/expanded states well. Shared divergence: neither nails the CTA at 46 (both 48). Key divergence: iOS implements the prefilled 'Booking as' chip + 'Not you?' and a question-driven phone field, while Android lacks the prefilled chip entirely and hardcodes phone into 'Your info', so iOS covers more of the six spec frames.

**iOS deviations:**
- `med`/`missing-element` — No existing-account InfoBanner frame: the spec's FrameExistingAccount renders an info banner ("You have an account. Open in app…", INFO_BG #F0F9FF / INFO_BORDER #BAE6FD) inside the Your-info section; InviteeIntakeFormView never shows it. **Fix:** Add an info-tone ConfirmBanner under yourInfoSection when the entered email matches a known account, with an 'Open in app' link.
- `low`/`sizing` — ConfirmPrimaryButton uses height 48 while the spec PrimaryCTA is height:46; CTA label is 14.5 vs spec fontSize:14. **Fix:** Set the button frame height to 46 and the label font size to 14 to match the spec.
- `low`/`state` — No submitting/shimmer CTA on this screen (ConfirmShimmerButton 'Submitting your booking' exists but is unused here); acceptable since iOS commits on D2, but the spec FrameSubmitting belongs to D1. **Fix:** If a brief D1→D2 transition is shown, swap the footer to ConfirmShimmerButton('Submitting your booking') and dim the body opacity ~0.85.
- `low`/`color` — Info-banner foreground in ConfirmBanner.info uses primary700; spec body text is #0c4a6e (primary-900) with primary600 link — slightly lighter than the spec ink (only relevant once the banner is added). **Fix:** Use appText/primary900 for the info banner body copy and primary600 for the link to match the spec.

**Android deviations:**
- `high`/`missing-element` — No prefilled 'Booking as <name>' chip: IntakeFormBody always renders the editable first/last/email fields; ConfirmFlowState/IntakeValues have no isPrefilled path, so the spec's FramePrefilled (avatar chip + email + 'Not you?') is entirely absent. **Fix:** Add an isPrefilled flag + BookingAsChip composable (avatar, 'Booking as …', email, 'Not you?' clearing prefill) shown in place of the Your-info fields when a signed-in invitee identity is present.
- `high`/`missing-element` — No existing-account InfoBanner: spec FrameExistingAccount shows an info banner ('You have an account. Open in app…') below the email field; the Android body has no such banner (only an error banner at the top of the flow). **Fix:** Render a ConfirmBanner(tone=Info, icon=Info) with an 'Open in app' action under the email field when the email resolves to an existing account.
- `med`/`layout` — Phone is a hardcoded field inside the 'Your info' section (LabeledField 'Phone number' + helper 'For a text reminder before your booking.'), but the spec places phone under the 'A few questions' overline as a host question; this re-orders/misplaces the section and the helper copy differs from spec ('before the call.'). **Fix:** Drive phone from the host-questions schema (under the 'A few questions' overline) rather than a fixed Your-info field, and align the helper text with the spec.
- `med`/`state` — Submitting shimmer label is wrong for the slot-expired interaction and color-only: when holdExpired the body is dimmed via alpha but the spec FrameExpired dims to opacity 0.5 with a warn ExpiredBanner — Android dims the summary card to 0.55 and shows the banner, but the rest of the form (Your info/questions/guests) is not wrapped in the 0.5 dim group as the spec does. **Fix:** Wrap the whole non-banner body in an alpha(0.5)+disabled group when holdExpired (matching FrameExpired) instead of only dimming the summary card.
- `low`/`typography` — Field label uses fontSize 11.5sp SemiBold (matches), but the host-questions textarea/select all collapse to a plain text input (placeholder 'Type your answer'); spec textarea placeholder is host-interpolated ('A sentence or two helps Maria prepare.') and select shows 'Select one' with a chevron. **Fix:** Render typed widgets for textarea (host-interpolated placeholder) and select (chevron + 'Select one') when the question schema is present, mirroring iOS questionField.
- `low`/`sizing` — FilledCta uses heightIn(min=48.dp); spec PrimaryCTA height is 46. **Fix:** Set the CTA height to 46.dp to match the spec.

### D My bookings (customer) — iOS `minor` / Android `major` → better: **ios**
- iOS files: `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Scheduling/Invitee/Edge/MyBookingsView.swift`, `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Scheduling/Invitee/Edge/MyBookingsViewModel.swift`, `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Scheduling/Invitee/Edge/EdgeComponents.swift`, `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Scheduling/Invitee/Edge/EdgeSupport.swift`, `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Scheduling/SharedUI/SchedulingStatusPill.swift`, `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Core/Design/Components/EmptyState.swift`, `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Core/Design/Radii.swift`
- Android files: `frontend/apps/android/app/src/main/java/app/pantopus/android/ui/screens/scheduling/invitee/customer/MyBookingsScreen.kt`, `frontend/apps/android/app/src/main/java/app/pantopus/android/ui/screens/scheduling/invitee/customer/MyBookingsModels.kt`, `frontend/apps/android/app/src/main/java/app/pantopus/android/ui/components/EmptyState.kt`, `frontend/apps/android/app/src/main/java/app/pantopus/android/ui/theme/Typography.kt`, `frontend/apps/android/app/src/main/java/app/pantopus/android/ui/theme/Radii.kt`, `frontend/apps/android/app/src/main/java/app/pantopus/android/ui/theme/Spacing.kt`
- **Verdict:** Both faithfully ship the chrome + segmented + grouped white-card rows with status pills and the loading/empty/error/loaded states, but neither builds the "Book again" or "Pay/Balance due" affordances; iOS is near-pixel (gradient+initials avatar, correct type sizes) while Android diverges on title size, avatar treatment, overline/pill type tokens, segmented radius/gap, and drops the empty-state CTA.
- **Cross note:** Both platforms omit the same two spec affordances — the 'Book again' past-row footer and the 'Pay $40 / Balance due' action-needed footer (plus the Balance/Approve pill variants) — because the lean /my-bookings payload lacks event/host/manage data; this is a shared, documented backend gap rather than a pure UI miss. Key divergence: iOS keeps spec type sizes and the gradient+initials avatar and ships the empty CTA, whereas Android oversizes the title, uses token type styles that don't match the spec's smaller sizes, substitutes a flat User-icon avatar, and drops the empty-state CTA.

**iOS deviations:**
- `med`/`missing-element` — FrameActionNeeded's pay affordance (footer 'Pay $40' pill + '$40 due at confirm', spec lines 191-195) and FramePast's 'Book again' footer (rotate-ccw + 'Book again', spec lines 184-189) are not rendered — bookingRow only ever draws the status pill + chevron. **Fix:** Add an optional footer row to bookingRow with a top-border divider for the bookAgain link and the payAffordance balance/Pay button.
- `low`/`missing-element` — Row secondary line shows only the {when}; spec line 177 is 'with {host} · {when}', and the primary line should be the event-type name not a synthesized '{Pillar} booking' title (titleLabel, line 169-171). **Fix:** Render event-type name + host once the lean /my-bookings payload joins them; acceptable as a documented backend gap today.
- `low`/`color` — StatusPill maps pending → warning (amber) tone (SchedulingStatusPill tone, lines 81-83), but spec's pending pill is INFO blue (bg #F0F9FF / fg #0369A1, my-bookings StatusPill 'pending', line 157). **Fix:** Give the my-bookings pending status the info tone to match the booker-side spec, or pass an explicit info kind.
- `low`/`color` — Segmented container uses Radii.lg (12) and buttons Radii.sm (6); spec uses 10 (container) and 7 (buttons) (Segmented, lines 70-78). **Fix:** Use a 10pt container radius and 7pt button radius (or accept as <20% nit).
- `low`/`missing-element` — Empty-state hero icon is calendar but spec empty CTA is 'Find something to book' with a leading search glyph (FrameEmpty, lines 275-277); iOS ships the CTA title text but with no leading icon and a no-op action. **Fix:** Add a search leading icon to the EmptyState CTA and wire the discovery destination when available.

**Android deviations:**
- `high`/`typography` — TopBar title uses PantopusTextStyle.h3 = 20sp/SemiBold (line 163); spec top-bar title is 15px/600 (TopBar, line 62) — the title is ~33% oversized. **Fix:** Render the title at 15sp SemiBold (a caption/small-derived style) instead of h3.
- `high`/`missing-element` — EmptyBody() calls EmptyState with no ctaTitle/onCta (lines 361-368), so the primary 'Find something to book' button (spec lines 275-277) is absent on Android, unlike iOS. **Fix:** Pass ctaTitle = "Find something to book" with a search-icon CTA and a discovery handler.
- `med`/`icon` — HostAvatar draws a flat pillar-bg circle with a generic User glyph (lines 300-310); spec HostAvatar is a 135° pillar gradient disc with white initials + a bordered pillar identity dot (HostAvatar, lines 145-151). iOS matches the gradient+initials spec. **Fix:** Use a pillar LinearGradient fill with the host initials text, mirroring iOS EdgePillarAvatar.
- `med`/`typography` — GroupOverline uses PantopusTextStyle.overline = 11sp/SemiBold (lines 250-253); spec overline is 10px/700 with 0.08em tracking (Overline, line 139). **Fix:** Render the overline at 10sp Bold with 0.08em letterSpacing.
- `med`/`typography` — StatusPill label uses PantopusTextStyle.overline (11sp/SemiBold, line 347); spec pill text is 9.5px/700 (StatusPill, line 163), so Android pills read noticeably larger/lighter. **Fix:** Set the pill label to ~9.5sp Bold.
- `med`/`missing-element` — BookingPillKind only has Confirmed/Pending/Past/Cancelled (MyBookingsModels lines 14-18) and BookingRow never renders a footer; spec's 'Balance due'/'Approve pending' pills and the Pay/Book-again footers (spec lines 159-160, 184-195) are unbuildable. **Fix:** Add Balance/Approve pill kinds and an optional row footer for pay + book-again affordances.
- `low`/`spacing` — SegmentedTabs has no inter-button gap (uses Spacing.s0 and md=8 container radius, lines 183-196); spec is gap:3 with container radius 10 and button radius 7 (Segmented, lines 70-78). **Fix:** Add a 3dp gap between the two segment boxes and use a 10dp container / 7dp button radius.
- `low`/`missing-element` — LoadingSkeleton renders 4 ungrouped skeleton rows (lines 371-396); spec loading frame groups 2+2 rows under two shimmer overline bars (FrameLoading, lines 298-313). iOS mirrors the grouped skeleton. **Fix:** Emit a shimmer overline bar before each pair of skeleton rows.

### D Review and confirm — iOS `minor` / Android `major` → better: **ios**

**iOS deviations:**

- `low`/`state` — Dedicated card-error/3DS (warn banner + 'Try again' rotate-ccw CTA) and Stripe-unavailable (info cloud-off banner + disabled CTA) frames are not modeled; the generic confirm() error path shows alertTriangle banners instead. **Fix:** Add inline-banner tones for declined/3DS and Stripe-down with the matching warn/disabled CTA states.
- `low`/`color` — totalsBox uses appSurfaceMuted (#f8fafc) vs the spec's #fafbfc fill — visually negligible but a token approximation. **Fix:** Acceptable; no change needed unless an exact token is added.

Refund policy'); it shows a single non-interactive sentence and no chevron/sheet trigger, unlike the iOS refundLink and the spec RefundLink. **Fix:** Append a primary-600 'Refund policy' span that opens the cancellation-policy sheet, mirroring iOS.

- `med`/`missing-element` — TimeoutBody replaces the spec's info callout card (icon disc + "If the first try did go through, checking again won't charge you a second time.") with a single small pill; the framed info-bg/info-ring callout block is absent. **Fix:** Render a PolicyNoteCard/info callout block with the full reassurance sentence instead of the compact chip.
- `med`/`missing-element` — SucceededBody omits the auto-advance progress bar + pulsing "Confirming your booking" indicator and uses a single "Done" button; spec frame 4 has no button and auto-advances with a progress bar. **Fix:** Add the success progress bar + confirming indicator and drop/secondary-ize the Done CTA to match the auto-advance morph.
- `low`/`icon` — HoldExpired chip uses PantopusIcon.Timer; spec uses timer-off for the released state. **Fix:** Use a TimerOff glyph for the released hold chip.
- `low`/`icon` — Succeeded halo uses PantopusIcon.CheckCircle; spec uses check-circle-2 (the double/filled check) for the success morph. **Fix:** Map the success halo glyph to check-circle-2 to match spec intent.
- `low`/`typography` — EdgeHalo title uses PantopusTextStyle.h3 and body PantopusTextStyle.small rather than the spec's explicit 17/700 title and 12/fg2 body; iOS inlines 19/bold + 12.5 — both diverge slightly but Android is further from the 17px title. **Fix:** Confirm h3 resolves near 17sp bold; otherwise inline the spec sizes.

### E1 Bookings inbox — iOS `minor` / Android `minor` → better: **ios**
- iOS files: `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Scheduling/Bookings/Core/BookingsInboxView.swift`, `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Scheduling/Bookings/Core/BookingRowView.swift`, `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Scheduling/SharedUI/SchedulingStatusPill.swift`

- **Verdict:** Both platforms faithfully reproduce the tabbed list-of-rows shell (top bar, scope pills, segmented control, day-sectioned rows, FAB, empty/loading/error), with iOS edging ahead on state copy/icons while Android wins on scope-pill interactivity; both omit the assigned-member-name chip and the member-gated banner.
- **Cross note:** Shared gaps on both platforms: the assigned-member chip never shows the actual member name and the member-gated info banner (Frame 9) is missing. Key divergence: iOS disables the scope-pill switcher entirely (allowsHitTesting false) while Android keeps it interactive (onSelect wired); conversely Android's error state regresses to a generic AlertCircle/'Something went wrong' surface whereas iOS uses the correct cloud-off + 'Couldn't load bookings'.

**iOS deviations:**
- `med`/`interaction` — Scope pills are rendered with .allowsHitTesting(false) (scopePill, BookingsInboxView.swift:137) so only the active pill works and the All/Personal/Home/Business switcher is non-functional; the spec's horizontally-scrolling switcher is meant to re-scope. **Fix:** Wire pill taps to re-scope via an owner directory, or at minimum allow selecting among resolved owners.
- `med`/`missing-element` — BookingRowView has no AssignedChip — Frames 7/9 show a violet 'Assigned · Priya/Devon/You' member chip beside the owner glyph (AssignedChip in spec); the row only renders BookingOwnerGlyph. **Fix:** Add an assigned-member chip (user-round icon + member name, business-bg) rendered when the booking carries an assignee.
- `low`/`missing-element` — No member-gated banner; Frame 9 shows a blue 'You're seeing bookings assigned to you' info banner (MemberBanner) above the segmented control for member-scoped views. **Fix:** Render an info banner (user-check icon, blue50/blue200) when the viewer is a non-admin member.
- `low`/`other` — Segmented track uses Radii.lg (12) in segmentedTabs (BookingsInboxView.swift:162) vs the spec's 10px container radius (inner buttons 7). **Fix:** Use a 10pt corner radius for the segmented track.
- `low`/`typography` — Top-bar title is .system(size:16) (topBar, BookingsInboxView.swift:61) vs spec 15.5. **Fix:** Set title size to 15.5.

**Android deviations:**
- `med`/`icon` — Error state calls ErrorState(message = s.message, onRetry=…) (BookingsInboxScreen.kt:146) which uses PantopusIcon.AlertCircle and the default headline 'Something went wrong'; spec Frame 6 uses a cloud-off glyph and 'Couldn't load bookings' on an error-red hero circle. **Fix:** Pass headline='Couldn't load bookings' and use a cloud-off icon variant (or a dedicated error scaffold) instead of the generic AlertCircle ErrorState.
- `med`/`missing-element` — AssignedChip() renders a hardcoded 'Assigned' label (BookingsInboxScreen.kt:639) instead of the member name; spec shows the assignee name (Priya/Devon/Unassigned/You). **Fix:** Pass and render row.assignedName in AssignedChip.
- `low`/`missing-element` — No member-gated info banner; Frame 9's 'You're seeing bookings assigned to you' MemberBanner above the segmented control is absent. **Fix:** Add an info banner composable for member-scoped sessions.
- `low`/`color` — Active segment label is always PantopusColors.primary700 (InboxSegmented, BookingsInboxScreen.kt:410); spec ties the active-tab accent to the scope (home green / business violet), e.g. Frame 7 accent #7c3aed, Frame 8 #16a34a. **Fix:** Pass the active scope accent into InboxSegmented and use it for the selected label.
- `low`/`state` — Pending segment is always present (BookingSegment.entries in InboxSegmented); spec Frame 8 (auto-confirm) and Frame 9 (member-gated) hide the Pending segment (hidePending). **Fix:** Filter out the Pending segment when the owner auto-confirms or the viewer is a gated member.
- `low`/`other` — Segmented track uses RoundedCornerShape(Radii.md=8) (InboxSegmented, BookingsInboxScreen.kt:387) vs spec 10 corner radius. **Fix:** Use a 10dp track radius.
- `low`/`sizing` — Top bar height 48dp and icon hit targets 40dp (InboxTopBar/TopBarIcon, BookingsInboxScreen.kt:198,296) vs spec 46 bar height and 34 buttons. **Fix:** Set bar height to 46dp and icon button size to 34dp.

### E2 Booking detail — iOS `minor` / Android `major` → better: **ios**
- iOS files: `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Scheduling/Bookings/Core/BookingDetailView.swift`, `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Scheduling/Bookings/Core/BookingDetailSections.swift`, `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Scheduling/Bookings/Core/BookingDetailViewModel.swift`
- Android files: `frontend/apps/android/app/src/main/java/app/pantopus/android/ui/screens/scheduling/bookings/BookingDetailScreen.kt`, `frontend/apps/android/app/src/main/java/app/pantopus/android/ui/screens/scheduling/bookings/BookingDetailModels.kt`
- **Verdict:** iOS faithfully reproduces all 10 design frames (chrome, pillar header, all banners, every section card incl. status timeline + intake accordion + message button, conflict banner, all 5 status-contextual dock variants, shimmer, error), with only small nits; Android has the same chrome/header/cards but drops the Status timeline card, the requester Message button, the follow-up promo + refund line, the conflict banner, and collapses the dock to just Pending vs a single Reschedule button — so it omits major design content.
- **Cross note:** Both platforms simplify the assigned-member card to a generic label instead of the design's named member with a Reassign action button inline; iOS keeps an inline Reassign text button (Android drops it from the card, relegating reassign to the kebab menu). Neither implements the dedicated frame-7 'Reassign to' member-picker card inline (handled via separate sheets, which is acceptable native idiom).

**iOS deviations:**
- `low`/`missing-element` — Avatar in requesterCard uses BookingAvatar but the design's Avatar carries a white badge-check verified ring (badge-check, pillar-colored) at bottom-right; cannot confirm BookingAvatar renders that badge. **Fix:** Ensure BookingAvatar overlays the 16x16 white circle + badge-check glyph in the pillar accent like design Avatar.
- `low`/`color` — refundLine shows literal text 'Issued' in success color rather than the design's tabular-nums amount (e.g. '$120.00') in SUCCESS_DK with a 'Full refund issued…' subline. **Fix:** Render the refunded amount value + the free-cancellation-window subline when currency/amount is available.
- `low`/`missing-element` — Assigned-member card renders a generic 'Team member' label with a userRound glyph instead of the design's member initials avatar (AV gradient) + member name ('Priya R.'). **Fix:** Show member initials in the gradient avatar and the real member name when available.
- `low`/`layout` — Design orders cards Requester → Location → Intake → Status(timeline); the loaded() VStack orders requester → location → assignedMember → intake → timeline, putting assigned-member between location and intake (acceptable, Business-only) but worth confirming against frame order. **Fix:** Confirm card ordering matches the per-status design frames.

**Android deviations:**
- `high`/`missing-element` — DetailContent has no Status timeline card; design frames 1/3/5 all show a 'Status' card with a vertical check/dashed-node Timeline (Requested→Confirmed→Reminder→Meeting etc). **Fix:** Add a timeline section card mirroring iOS timelineCard with done/not-done nodes and connectors.
- `high`/`missing-element` — DetailDock only renders Pending (Decline+Approve) vs an else branch with a single Reschedule button; design specifies distinct docks for confirmed (Reschedule+Message), past/completed (Rebook+Follow up), no-show (Message+Send rebook link), and cancelled (single Rebook this time). **Fix:** Branch the dock on every BookingStatus and add the missing two-button and single-button variants with correct icons/labels.
- `high`/`missing-element` — RequesterCard omits the trailing 36x36 outlined message-circle icon button (brand blue, Radii.lg border) present in the design AttendeeRow. **Fix:** Add the trailing Message icon-button to RequesterCard like iOS.
- `med`/`missing-element` — No conflict-warning banner (frame 6): warningBg pill with triangle-alert, 'This overlaps another booking' + 'View' action above the dock; isActive/hasConflict path is absent on Android. **Fix:** Add a ConflictBanner composable rendered above the dock when a conflict is present.
- `med`/`missing-element` — Past/completed state shows a generic 'rescheduled' banner only; design frame 3 has a blue 'Send a follow-up' sparkles promo and frame 4 has a Refund card ($120.00 + free-cancellation subline) — both absent. **Fix:** Add the sparkles follow-up promo for completed/past and a Refund card for cancelled-with-payment.
- `med`/`state` — isActive gates the dock to only Pending/Confirmed, so completed, past, no-show, cancelled and declined bookings render NO dock at all (design shows a dock in every one of those frames). **Fix:** Show the dock for terminal/past statuses too and route to the correct actions.
- `low`/`icon` — No-show banner uses PantopusIcon.UserMinus; design uses user-x (user-x glyph) and personalizes copy ('<name> didn't attend') whereas Android hardcodes 'the invitee didn't attend'. **Fix:** Switch to a user-x icon and interpolate the requester's first name.
- `low`/`typography` — CardOverline uses fontSize 10.sp + FontWeight.Bold but omits the design's 0.08em letterSpacing on the uppercase overline; minor but visible. **Fix:** Add letterSpacing ≈ 0.8.sp to the overline Text to match the tracked-caps spec.

### E3 Approve / decline sheet — iOS `matches` / Android `minor` → better: **ios**
- iOS files: `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Scheduling/Bookings/Core/ApproveDeclineSheet.swift`, `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Scheduling/Bookings/Core/BookingSheetComponents.swift`, `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Scheduling/Bookings/Core/BookingRowView.swift`

- **Verdict:** Both render the sheet faithfully (title, requester+badge card, slot card, intake preview, note, reason chips, inline error, spinner-on-submit, decline-expanded mode); iOS is the closer match because Android tints the Approve CTA with the pillar accent (purple) instead of the spec's sky-blue PRIMARY and omits the frame-3 conflict banner that iOS includes.
- **Cross note:** Approve-button color is the key divergence: iOS correct sky-blue PRIMARY, Android wrong pillar-purple. iOS also implements the conflict banner and the propose-another-time link (both gated on optional callbacks) that Android lacks entirely. Both default-hide the propose link unless the host passes the callback.

**iOS deviations:**
- `low`/`other` — BookingSlotCard corner radius uses Radii.lg (12); spec SlotLine borderRadius is 14. **Fix:** Introduce a 14pt radius for the slot/requester cards or accept the 2pt delta.
- `low`/`typography` — IntakeAnswersDisclosure title is size 13 semibold; spec IntakePreview label is fontSize 12.5 weight 600. **Fix:** Drop the intake label to 12.5pt to match spec.
- `low`/`layout` — iOS intake row is a richer disclosure (34pt icon tile + chevron up/down expand); spec IntakePreview is a flat 16px clipboard + 'Intake answers' + 'N answers' + chevron-down with no icon tile. **Fix:** Acceptable enhancement; optionally drop the icon background tile to match the flatter spec row.

**Android deviations:**
- `high`/`color` — PillarFilledButton tints the Approve CTA with state.pillar.accent (purple #7C3AED for business); spec Actions approve button background is PRIMARY = E.blue600 (#0284c7 sky) with a sky shadow rgba(2,132,199,0.28). **Fix:** Use PantopusColors.primary600 for the Approve button background instead of the pillar accent.
- `med`/`missing-element` — No conflict banner is rendered; spec frame 3 (FrameConflict) shows an amber ConflictBanner ('This slot overlaps a confirmed booking' + 'View conflict') above the actions in review mode. iOS has conflictBanner; Android has no equivalent path. **Fix:** Add a warning-tone banner driven by a showConflictWarning flag mirroring iOS's conflictBanner.
- `med`/`missing-element` — Decline mode omits the 'Propose another time' calendar-plus link that spec ReasonChips renders (marginTop:13, primary600, weight 700) below the chips. **Fix:** Add the calendar-plus 'Propose another time' link in decline mode (iOS exposes it via onProposeTime).
- `low`/`sizing` — CTA_HEIGHT is 46.dp for both buttons; spec approve / decline-request primary button height is 48 (only the secondary decline is 46). **Fix:** Make the primary Approve / Decline-request button 48dp tall.
- `low`/`sizing` — NoteField heightIn min = 56.dp; spec NoteInput minHeight is 58. **Fix:** Bump note min height to 58dp.
- `low`/`other` — RequesterCard and SlotLine use Radii.xl (16); spec Requester/SlotLine borderRadius is 14. **Fix:** Use a 14dp (or Radii.lg=12) radius for these cards to match spec.
- `low`/`color` — SlotLine border uses accent.copy(alpha=0.25f); spec strokes 1.5px with the solid identity-bg tint (ID.business.bg #f3e8ff), not an alpha of the accent. **Fix:** Stroke with the pillar's identity-bg token to match the lighter lavender tone.

The divergence is purely visual fidelity: iOS inlines the exact spec px values while Android reuses coarse semantic type-scale tokens (h3/body/small/caption) that don't match the spec's 16.5/13/11.5/11 sizes, plus a wrong green and a dropped users glyph.

- `high`/`color` — MemberConflictNote uses successBg/success (#F0FDF4 bg, #059669 dot+text); spec uses HOME palette: bg #dcfce7, dot #16a34a, text #15803d. **Fix:** Bind to the home/identity-home tokens (homeBg/home/homeDark) instead of success.
- `high`/`icon` — "Pick another member" Text has no leading glyph; spec line 106 prefixes a lucide users icon (15px) before the label. **Fix:** Add a PantopusIconImage(PantopusIcon.Users, size=15) before the label, matching iOS.
- `med`/`sizing` — ExtrasIconDisc DISC_SIZE=44dp / DISC_ICON=22dp; spec disc is 40x40 with a 20px glyph. **Fix:** Set DISC_SIZE=40.dp and DISC_ICON=20.dp.
- `med`/`typography` — ConflictCard title uses style=body (16sp) SemiBold and detail uses caption (12sp); spec title is 13/bold, detail 11/fg3. **Fix:** Use ~13sp Bold for title and ~11sp for detail.
- `med`/`sizing` — ConflictCard icon box is size(34.dp) with a 17.dp wrench; spec card disc is 36x36 radius 9 with an 18px glyph. **Fix:** Set the box to 36.dp (Radii ~9) and icon to 18.dp.
- `low`/`sizing` — Dialog Column uses widthIn(max=320.dp) and uniform padding(Spacing.s5=20) on all sides; spec card maxWidth is 300 with padding 20/18/16 (top/horizontal/bottom). **Fix:** Cap width at 300.dp and use 18dp horizontal / 16dp bottom padding.

Android GroupRosterScreen only calls snackbar.showSnackbar(it) — no success disc, no centered title, no styled dark toast. **Fix:** Render a success overlay inside NudgeSheet (72dp check disc + 'Update sent' + dark count toast) mirroring SendNudgeSheet.successOverlay instead of a plain Snackbar.

- `med`/`color` — ExtrasMessageBox over-limit border uses PantopusColors.error (solid #DC2626) at full weight; spec uses lighter ERR_LIGHT #FCA5A5 for the box border (only counter/text turn full red). **Fix:** Use a lighter error token (#FCA5A5) for the over-limit border, keep counter text at error #DC2626.
- `med`/`typography` — Char counter uses style caption (~12sp) vs spec 10px/700/tabular-nums; channel-row label uses body Medium vs spec 12.5px semibold; header uses h3 (20sp) Bold vs spec 16.5px/700. **Fix:** Inline spec point sizes/weights (counter 10sp bold monospaced, channel label 12.5sp semibold, header 16.5sp bold).
- `low`/`sizing` — ExtrasChannelRow uses Material3 Switch default (~52x32dp) vs spec toggle pill 42x25 with 20dp thumb; ExtrasPillChip selected uses 1.5dp accent border + accent.copy(0.12) fill vs spec borderless fill #e0f2fe. **Fix:** Switch is an acceptable native idiom; for selected chips drop the border and use the lighter personal-bg fill.

### E13 Waitlist join & management — iOS `minor` / Android `major` → better: **ios**
- iOS files: `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Scheduling/Bookings/Extras/Waitlist/WaitlistJoinSheet.swift`, `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Scheduling/Bookings/Extras/Waitlist/WaitlistManagementView.swift`, `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Scheduling/Bookings/Extras/Shared/CapacityRoster.swift`, `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Scheduling/Bookings/Extras/Shared/BookingsExtrasUI.swift`
- Android files: `frontend/apps/android/app/src/main/java/app/pantopus/android/ui/screens/scheduling/bookings_extra/WaitlistScreen.kt`, `frontend/apps/android/app/src/main/java/app/pantopus/android/ui/screens/scheduling/bookings_extra/WaitlistJoinSheet.kt`, `frontend/apps/android/app/src/main/java/app/pantopus/android/ui/screens/scheduling/bookings_extra/CapacityRoster.kt`, `frontend/apps/android/app/src/main/java/app/pantopus/android/ui/screens/scheduling/bookings_extra/WaitlistViewModel.kt`
- **Verdict:** iOS faithfully renders both surfaces (join sheet + host capacity/promote list) with correct tokens and states, missing only the "#3 in line" queue-position badge; Android's host screen replaces the design's capacity strip with an ad-hoc "N people waiting" row, never disables Promote when full, and adds an out-of-spec event-type chip selector.
- **Cross note:** Both platforms drop the design's "#3 in line" queue-position badge in the joined-confirmation and neither implements the frame-3 "already on waitlist" read-only variant. Key divergence: iOS host view correctly uses CapacityHeaderCard + RosterRow with promote-disabled-when-full, while Android's WaitlistContent abandons the shared CapacityHeaderCard, hardcodes enabled=true on promote, and bolts on an extra event-type chip picker not in the spec.

**iOS deviations:**
- `med`/`missing-element` — joinedConfirmation omits the design's "#3 in line" queue-position badge (pill with bold accent #3 + "in line") and shows generic copy instead of "You're #3 — we'll text you if a spot frees up." **Fix:** Add a pill (ID.business.bg background, accent bold position + fg2 "in line") below the headline and surface the queue position in the subcopy.
- `med`/`missing-element` — No "already on waitlist" frame (clock disc, "You're already waiting", joined-date copy, position badge, Leave waitlist) — WaitlistJoinSheet only handles fresh-join vs joined, not the already-joined read-only variant. **Fix:** Add an alreadyJoined branch in the join sheet rendering the clock disc + joined-date copy + position badge.
- `low`/`state` — Joined CTA is a ghost "Done" button; design frames 2/3 use a ghost "Leave waitlist" action. **Fix:** Rename/repurpose the ghost CTA to "Leave waitlist" wired to a leave action, keeping ghost tone.
- `low`/`missing-element` — Join form omits the design's "Preferred time" multi-line textarea (minHeight 42, padded box); iOS uses a single-line 44pt TextField field matching the other inputs. **Fix:** Render preferred-time as a taller multi-line input box to match the design's textarea geometry.
- `low`/`color` — fullyBookedPill warning tone uses Theme.Color.warning (token #D97706) vs design WARN #B45309; close but the design's warn is darker. **Fix:** Acceptable token mapping; optionally add a darker warning-strong token to match #B45309.

**Android deviations:**
- `high`/`missing-element` — Host WaitlistContent never renders CapacityHeaderCard; it builds an ad-hoc Row showing "N people waiting / N seats per session" instead of the design's "11 of 12 seats filled · 3 waiting" strip with a progress fill bar. **Fix:** Replace the ad-hoc Row with CapacityHeaderCard(filled, total, waiting, accent, showStats=false) and compute filled from seatTotal − openSeats.
- `high`/`state` — PromoteSeatButton is always called with enabled=true; the design's frame-5 capacity-full state (grayscale bar + disabled Promote + "Open a seat to promote" caption) is unreachable. **Fix:** Track isFull in WaitlistData and pass enabled=!isFull plus the "Open a seat to promote" caption below the button when full.
- `high`/`extra-element` — WaitlistContent adds an out-of-spec event-type chip selector (ExtrasChipFlow + "Event type" overline) and a per-type loader; the design is a single event's roster with no type picker. **Fix:** Remove the chip selector; the screen should target one event/slot's waitlist like the spec and iOS.
- `med`/`layout` — PromoteSeatButton is a compact inline pill in the row's trailing slot; the design puts a full-width 34pt promote button on its own line below the avatar/name row (column layout with a divider). **Fix:** Render the promote button full-width on a second line inside the row (mirror iOS RosterRow promoteSection) rather than as a trailing pill.
- `med`/`missing-element` — RosterRow lacks the more-vertical kebab (16dp, fg4) the design shows on each waitlist row's trailing edge. **Fix:** Add a kebab IconButton in the row trailing slot before/with the promote action.
- `low`/`sizing` — CapacityHeaderCard fill bar BAR_HEIGHT=8.dp vs design 9px; joined-confirmation disc is 64dp vs design 74; check disc icon 30dp vs 34. **Fix:** Bump bar to 9dp and the joined disc to 74dp / icon 34dp to match the spec.
- `med`/`missing-element` — Join sheet's JoinedConfirmation omits the "#3 in line" position badge and the already-on-waitlist variant, same as iOS but compounded by generic copy. **Fix:** Add the accent position badge + queue copy, and an already-joined branch.
- `low`/`icon` — FullyBookedPill uses PantopusIcon.Users (users) vs design users-round; minor glyph intent match. **Fix:** Use a users-round equivalent if available, otherwise acceptable.

### E6 Mark no-show — iOS `matches` / Android `minor` → better: **ios**
- iOS files: `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Scheduling/Bookings/Extras/MarkNoShow/MarkNoShowDialog.swift`, `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Scheduling/Bookings/Extras/Shared/BookingsExtrasUI.swift`, `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Core/Design/Icons.swift`
- Android files: `frontend/apps/android/app/src/main/java/app/pantopus/android/ui/screens/scheduling/bookings_extra/NoShowSheet.kt`, `frontend/apps/android/app/src/main/java/app/pantopus/android/ui/screens/scheduling/bookings_extra/BookingsExtrasUi.kt`, `frontend/apps/android/app/src/main/java/app/pantopus/android/ui/components/Buttons.kt`, `frontend/apps/android/app/src/main/java/app/pantopus/android/ui/theme/Typography.kt`, `frontend/apps/android/app/src/main/java/app/pantopus/android/ui/theme/Icons.kt`
- **Verdict:** Both platforms faithfully implement the centered no-show confirmation dialog with all four frame variants; iOS mirrors the spec's exact point sizes and uses the correct user-x glyph, while Android leans on its 20sp h3 type token (vs 16.5), a 44dp disc (vs 40), a person-remove icon (vs user-x), and adds an unspec'd note-field leading icon.
- **Cross note:** Both expose all four states (default, group multi-select, submitting spinner, inline error) and share the scheduling.markNoShow test-tag/accessibilityIdentifier. Shared divergence: neither perfectly hits the spec's 13.5px button label; the main divergence is Android relying on coarse type tokens (h3=20, small=14) and a larger 44dp disc where iOS inlines the exact 16.5/13/12.5px sizes and 40px disc from the frame.

**iOS deviations:**
- `low`/`typography` — Group note placeholder is 12px (matches spec 12 fg4) and 1:1 body lineSpacing is 2pt giving ~17pt line height vs spec lineHeight 19px on 13px body. **Fix:** Set .lineSpacing(6) on the 1:1 Body text so total line height reaches ~19pt.
- `low`/`sizing` — Avatar in attendeeRow uses owner.theme.accent fill (e.g. business purple/home green) whereas spec hardcodes the personal sky gradient AV.personal for all roster avatars. **Fix:** Acceptable owner-context choice, but if matching spec exactly use the personal-blue gradient swatch.
- `low`/`color` — Inline error strip border uses Radii.md (8) matching spec error box radius 10 only approximately; spec error radius is 10, attendee radius 11 vs code Radii.lg (12). **Fix:** Optionally add a Radii value of 10/11 for these compact dialog elements; current 8/12 is within tolerance.

**Android deviations:**
- `med`/`typography` — Title uses PantopusTextStyle.h3 (20sp/28) overridden only to Bold; spec title is 16.5px bold with letterSpacing -0.2, so the Android title renders ~20% larger than design. **Fix:** Use a 16.5sp bold custom TextStyle (or PantopusTextStyle.body bolded) instead of h3 for the dialog title.
- `med`/`typography` — Body/subtitle uses PantopusTextStyle.small (14sp); spec 1:1 body is 13px and group subtitle is 12.5px, so copy is slightly oversized and the variants don't differ as in spec. **Fix:** Use ~13sp for the 1:1 body and ~12.5sp for the group subtitle rather than the shared small style.
- `med`/`icon` — ExtrasIconDisc is fed PantopusIcon.UserMinus which maps to Material Icons.Filled.PersonRemove (a person with a minus); spec glyph is lucide user-x (person with an X). iOS correctly uses .userX. **Fix:** Map a UserX icon (lucide user-x equivalent) and pass PantopusIcon.UserX to the disc to match intent.
- `low`/`extra-element` — Group note field (ExtrasInputField) renders a leading PantopusIcon.MessageSquare; the spec note field has no leading icon, just left-aligned placeholder text. **Fix:** Use a plain bordered text field without a leadingIcon for the optional note.
- `low`/`sizing` — ExtrasIconDisc DISC_SIZE=44dp / DISC_ICON=22dp vs spec 40px disc with 20px glyph (~10% large); attendee avatar diameter=34dp and checkbox 22dp vs spec 30/21. **Fix:** Set disc to 40dp/20dp, roster avatar to 30dp, and checkbox to 21dp to match the frame.
- `low`/`spacing` — Card padding is a uniform Spacing.s5 (20dp) on all sides and section gap is a uniform Spacing.s3 (12); spec uses asymmetric padding 20/18/16 and tighter per-element margins (title 8, body 16, etc.). **Fix:** Apply 20 top / 18 horizontal / 16 bottom padding and tune inter-element spacing rather than one spacedBy value.
- `low`/`typography` — Confirm/Keep-open button labels render via PantopusButton body style (16sp); spec button text is 13.5px bold. **Fix:** Lower the shared dialog button label to ~13.5sp bold (or accept the 44dp button with 16sp as a platform idiom).

### E7 Post-meeting follow-up — iOS `matches` / Android `major` → better: **ios**
- iOS files: `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Scheduling/Bookings/Extras/FollowUp/BookingFollowUpSheet.swift`, `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Scheduling/Bookings/Extras/FollowUp/BookingFollowUpViewModel.swift`, `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Scheduling/Bookings/Extras/Shared/BookingsExtrasUI.swift`, `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Scheduling/Bookings/Extras/Shared/BookingsExtrasControls.swift`
- Android files: `frontend/apps/android/app/src/main/java/app/pantopus/android/ui/screens/scheduling/bookings_extra/PostMeetingFollowupScreen.kt`, `frontend/apps/android/app/src/main/java/app/pantopus/android/ui/screens/scheduling/bookings_extra/PostMeetingFollowupViewModel.kt`, `frontend/apps/android/app/src/main/java/app/pantopus/android/ui/screens/scheduling/bookings_extra/BookingsExtrasUi.kt`, `frontend/apps/android/app/src/main/java/app/pantopus/android/ui/theme/Typography.kt`
- **Verdict:** iOS reproduces the design's bottom-sheet near pixel-for-pixel (grabber, header+subtitle, accent chips, PRIMARY rebook chip/toggle, ghost↔solid CTA, full success scrim+disc+toast), while Android rebuilds it as a full-screen Scaffold with a top app bar, drops the header subtitle and the rich success overlay, and inflates several font sizes.
- **Cross note:** Core divergence: iOS treats E7 as the spec's bottom-sheet archetype (sheet chrome + success scrim/toast), Android treats it as a routed full screen (Scaffold + TopAppBar + plain success), so Android loses the header subtitle, the success overlay richness, and uses owner-accent where the spec keeps brand PRIMARY. Android does add real Loading/Error full-screen states (parity-rule compliant) that the design doesn't depict.

**iOS deviations:**
- `low`/`interaction` — Spec frame 4 fires a success scrim then auto-dismisses after the toast; iOS sleeps 1.3s before onClose() which is fine, but the toast offset uses Spacing.s8 (32) bottom vs spec bottom:34 — ~6% off, negligible. **Fix:** Optionally nudge the toast bottom inset from Spacing.s8 to ~34 to match exactly.
- `low`/`sizing` — ExtrasSolidButton/ExtrasGhostButton footer buttons are height 46 vs spec button height 48. **Fix:** Bump the footer button frame height from 46 to 48 to match the spec CTA.

**Android deviations:**
- `high`/`chrome` — PostMeetingFollowupScreen renders a full-screen Scaffold + CenterAlignedTopAppBar (back chevron + centered 'Follow up' title); spec is a bottom sheet with a grabber pill, dim scrim over the parent booking, and rounded top corners — no top app bar. **Fix:** Present as a ModalBottomSheet with a drag handle and the in-body SheetHeader instead of a Scaffold/TopAppBar.
- `high`/`missing-element` — The SheetHeader subtitle ('Garden walkthrough · Mara Reyes · Jun 9', 11.5/fg3) is absent — FollowUpContent jumps straight to the Outcome section; the 16.5/700 'Follow up' title is also moved into the app bar instead of the body. **Fix:** Add an in-body header Column with the 'Follow up' title (16.5sp bold) and the booking·invitee·date subtitle (11.5sp appTextSecondary) above the Outcome section.
- `high`/`state` — FollowUpSuccess shows only a centered disc + single 'Follow-up sent to {name}' line; spec frame 4 has a dimmed scrim, a 72px successBg disc with successLight ring + heavy check, a white 17/700 'Follow-up sent' headline, AND a dark pinned bottom toast with check-circle-2 + 'Follow-up sent to Mara'. **Fix:** Rebuild success as a scrim overlay: 72dp ringed disc, white bold headline 'Follow-up sent', plus a dark pinned bottom toast row mirroring iOS successOverlay.
- `med`/`typography` — ExtrasMessageBox text/placeholder and ExtrasChannelRow label use PantopusTextStyle.body (16sp) vs spec composer/placeholder 12.5 and toggle label 12.5/600; ExtrasPillChip uses small (14sp) vs spec chip 12/700. **Fix:** Introduce 12.5sp styles for the composer/placeholder/toggle label and 12sp/bold for chips instead of body/small.
- `med`/`sizing` — ExtrasMessageBox default minHeight is 96dp and the private-note box is passed 72dp; spec composer is minHeight 84 and private note minHeight 46. **Fix:** Set composer minHeight to 84dp and private-note minHeight to 46dp.
- `med`/`missing-element` — Private-note footer renders a plain 'Only you can see this' caption with no leading eye-off icon (spec has eye-off 11px + 10px muted text); the lock overline icon is 12dp tinted appTextSecondary vs spec 13px appTextMuted. **Fix:** Add the eye-off icon before the caption and use appTextMuted tints to match the spec.
- `med`/`color` — Outcome chips, rebook chip, message-box cursor, and push toggle all use the owner pillar accent (state.pillar.accent); spec keeps the rebook chip, push toggle, and primary CTA on brand PRIMARY (blue600) — only the selected outcome chip uses the home/owner accent. **Fix:** Mirror iOS: pass Theme primary600 to ExtrasChipButton, ExtrasChannelRow, and the CTA; keep owner accent only on the selected outcome chip.
- `low`/`extra-element` — PrimaryButton title is 'Send follow-up'/'Try again' but the default no-outcome ghost CTA uses 'Save note only'; the error CTA icon/rotate-cw glyph from spec isn't explicitly wired on PrimaryButton, and footer button height/radius come from PrimaryButton defaults rather than the spec 48h/13 radius. **Fix:** Ensure the error CTA shows a rotate-cw icon and verify footer button height≈48dp and radius≈13dp to match the spec.

### E8 Group roster & seats — iOS `minor` / Android `major` → better: **ios**
- iOS files: `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Scheduling/Bookings/Extras/Roster/GroupRosterView.swift`, `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Scheduling/Bookings/Extras/Shared/CapacityRoster.swift`

- **Verdict:** iOS is a near-faithful reproduction of all six frames with only small nits, while Android reproduces the same content but reorders/restyles the host controls, drops the pinned capacity header in the empty state, and uses the wrong error icon/copy plus generic shared empty/error scaffolds.
- **Cross note:** Both platforms correctly share a CapacityHeaderCard/RosterRow archetype and cover all six frames (under-capacity/full/waitlist/loading/empty/error); the divergence is that Android leans on generic shared EmptyState/ErrorState scaffolds (losing the pinned capacity header and the cloud-off error identity) and restyles the host controls, while iOS hand-builds each frame to match the JSX.

**iOS deviations:**
- `low`/`color` — RosterRow avatar fills with the flat owner accent (theme.accent) whereas spec uses a 135deg business gradient (#a78bfa→#6d28d9). **Fix:** Render the avatar background as a LinearGradient matching AV.business instead of a solid Circle fill.
- `low`/`chrome` — Top-bar overflow menu offers 'Message all attendees' + 'Mark no-show'; the design overflow is unspecified but the Add-attendee affordance lives only in host controls (matches), so this is acceptable but adds an extra Message-all entry duplicating the FAB. **Fix:** Optional: drop the duplicate 'Message all attendees' menu item since the FAB already covers it.
- `low`/`spacing` — Promote section divider uses spacing Spacing.s2-2 (6pt) gaps vs spec's 10px top padding / borderTop separation; visually slightly tighter than the 10px gap in JSX. **Fix:** Use 10pt top padding above the divider to match promote { gap:10 }.

**Android deviations:**
- `high`/`layout` — CapacityControls renders the Capacity stepper FIRST and 'Add or invite attendee' SECOND; spec HostControls order is Add/invite attendee FIRST then Capacity. **Fix:** Swap the two children in CapacityControls so the add-attendee row precedes the capacity stepper row.
- `high`/`missing-element` — 'Add or invite attendee' is a generic full-width PrimaryButton; spec is a white card row with a 32px primary50 icon tile (user-plus, blue600) on the left, label, and a trailing chevron-right. **Fix:** Replace PrimaryButton with a bordered surface Row carrying a userPlus icon tile + label + chevronRight, mirroring iOS hostControls.
- `high`/`missing-element` — Empty state calls the generic full-screen EmptyState, dropping the capacity header (0 of N seats) that the spec pins above the 'No signups yet' block. **Fix:** Render CapacityHeaderCard pinned at top in the Empty branch, then the users disc + headline + Share CTA below it.
- `high`/`icon` — Error state uses PantopusIcon.AlertCircle with generic copy ('Something went wrong'/connection hint); spec uses a cloud-off glyph in an error disc with 'Couldn’t load the roster' / 'Check your connection and try again.' **Fix:** Pass an explicit cloud-off icon and the spec headline/message to ErrorState (or build a dedicated error block).
- `med`/`chrome` — Top-bar overflow menu contains 'Add or invite attendee' (+ Mark no-show); spec keeps add-attendee in host controls and the overflow is for message-all / no-show, so the add-attendee entry is misplaced into chrome. **Fix:** Remove the 'Add or invite attendee' DropdownMenuItem from the top bar; surface it via the host-controls row instead.
- `med`/`icon` — InitialsAvatar picks from a hashed 5-color palette and uses a green CheckCircle verified badge; spec avatar is the business purple gradient with a badge-check glyph tinted in the owner accent (#7c3aed). **Fix:** Fill the avatar with the business gradient/accent and use PantopusIcon.BadgeCheck tinted with the pillar accent for the verified badge.
- `med`/`extra-element` — 'Open a seat to promote' caption is rendered once below the whole waitlist section when seatsOpen==0; spec attaches the disabled caption beneath each individual promote button. **Fix:** Move the disabled caption into PromoteSeatButton (or per-row) so it appears under each disabled button.
- `low`/`typography` — Capacity headline uses PantopusTextStyle.body (16sp) and stat values use h3 (20sp); spec headline is 14/700 and stat value is 17/800. **Fix:** Use 14sp bold for the headline Text and ~17sp heavy for StatCell values rather than body/h3 styles.

### E9 Booking search & filter — iOS `minor` / Android `major` → better: **ios**
- iOS files: `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Scheduling/Bookings/Extras/Filter/BookingFilterSheet.swift`, `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Scheduling/Bookings/Extras/Shared/BookingsExtrasControls.swift`, `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Scheduling/Bookings/Extras/Shared/BookingsExtrasUI.swift`
- Android files: `frontend/apps/android/app/src/main/java/app/pantopus/android/ui/screens/scheduling/bookings_extra/BookingFilterSheet.kt`, `frontend/apps/android/app/src/main/java/app/pantopus/android/ui/screens/scheduling/bookings_extra/BookingSearchFilterScreen.kt`, `frontend/apps/android/app/src/main/java/app/pantopus/android/ui/screens/scheduling/bookings_extra/BookingsExtrasUi.kt`, `frontend/apps/android/app/src/main/java/app/pantopus/android/ui/components/EmptyState.kt`
- **Verdict:** iOS faithfully reproduces the FilterSheetShell (correct title/overline/chip/footer geometry and a no-results frame that keeps search + active-summary visible), while Android renders chips/title/Clear-all with oversized body/small/h3 type, drops the sticky-footer hairline, and replaces the no-results frame with a full-screen EmptyState that hides the search field and active summary.
- **Cross note:** Both platforms reuse a shared Extras component set; iOS's set encodes the exact spec point sizes (34/30dp chips, 10/700 overline, sticky footer, 60pt no-results disc) while Android's BookingsExtrasUi token-maps to coarser h3/body/small styles and the Android sheet additionally lives under an extra results-list Scaffold screen (CenterAlignedTopAppBar 'Search bookings' + chevron + sliders) that the spec — a pure bottom sheet — does not depict.

**iOS deviations:**
- `low`/`sizing` — Footer CTA uses ExtrasSolidButton with frame(height: 46) and Radii.lg (12); spec CTA is height 48 with cornerRadius 13. **Fix:** Bump the sheet CTA to height 48 and corner radius 13 (or add a 48/13 variant) to match the spec button.
- `low`/`typography` — CTA label font is .system(size: 14, weight: .bold) in ExtrasSolidButton; spec CTA text is 14.5px/700. **Fix:** Set the footer button font to size 14.5 to match spec.
- `low`/`state` — Status chips always pass through chipColors and show a dot for the tinted statuses, but the eventType/dateRange chips never show a dot — matches spec; however Pending uses warning tint correctly while spec Pending uses #B45309/#FFFBEB (warning is #D97706/#FFFBEB). **Fix:** Optional: map Pending status tint to the exact spec amber (#B45309 text) if exact match is required; otherwise acceptable as a token approximation.

**Android deviations:**
- `high`/`state` — No-results renders components/EmptyState (fillMaxSize, 72dp circle, 32dp icon, h3 headline, plus a 'Try removing a filter…' subcopy) and omits the SearchField and Active-filters summary that the spec FrameNoResults keeps visible above a 60dp disc/26px icon/14px headline with no subcopy. **Fix:** Replace EmptyState with an inline centered block (60dp sunken disc, 26dp search-x, 14sp/700 headline, no subcopy, Clear-all link) rendered below the still-visible SearchField + ActiveSummary, mirroring iOS noResults.
- `high`/`chrome` — CTA (PrimaryButton) sits inside the scrolling Column with vertical s4 padding and no top hairline; spec has a sticky footer pinned below the scroll area with a 1px top border on surface. **Fix:** Move PrimaryButton into a non-scrolling footer Box with Divider/top border (mirror iOS ExtrasStickyFooter), outside the verticalScroll Column.
- `med`/`typography` — Title 'Filter bookings' uses PantopusTextStyle.h3 (20sp) and 'Clear all' uses small (14sp); spec is 16.5px title and 13px Clear-all. **Fix:** Use a 16.5sp/Bold title and 13sp/Bold Clear-all instead of the h3/small token styles.
- `med`/`typography` — Pill chips and removable chips render label with PantopusTextStyle.small (14sp); spec pill text is 12px/700 and removable-chip text is 11.5px/700. **Fix:** Set pill chip text to 12sp/Bold and removable-chip text to 11.5sp/Bold.
- `med`/`sizing` — ExtrasPillChip/ExtrasRemovableChip have no fixed height (rely on vertical=Spacing.s2) so heights drift from spec's fixed 34dp (pill) and 30dp (removable); selected chips also add a 1.5dp border the spec selected chips do not have (spec selected = border:none). **Fix:** Pin pill chips to height 34dp and removable chips to 30dp; drop the border on selected chips (border only on unselected).
- `low`/`sizing` — CTA PrimaryButton floors at heightIn(min=44dp) with Radii.lg (12); spec CTA is 48dp tall, radius 13. **Fix:** Force the footer CTA to 48dp height and ~13dp radius.
- `low`/`typography` — ExtrasInputField search placeholder uses PantopusTextStyle.body (16sp); spec search placeholder is 12.5px. **Fix:** Use a 12.5sp text style for the search field value/placeholder.
- `low`/`state` — All facet chips pass showDot=true so Status chips get a selected dot; spec only shows dots on Owner-context chips (and tinted statuses), not a universal dot, and Date-range/Event-type chips never show a dot. **Fix:** Pass showDot=true only for the Owner-context section (and keep it off for plain date/event chips) to match spec dot usage.

## Home

### F1 Home calendar — iOS `matches` / Android `minor` → better: **ios**
- iOS files: `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Homes/Calendar/HomeCalendarView.swift`, `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Homes/Calendar/MonthStripHeader.swift`, `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Scheduling/Home/Calendar/HomeAgendaComponents.swift`, `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Scheduling/Home/Calendar/HomeCalendarCreateMenu.swift`, `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Scheduling/Routing/Stubs/Home/HomeCalendarStubView.swift`
- Android files: `frontend/apps/android/app/src/main/java/app/pantopus/android/ui/screens/homes/calendar/HomeCalendarScreen.kt`, `frontend/apps/android/app/src/main/java/app/pantopus/android/ui/screens/homes/calendar/MonthStripHeader.kt`, `frontend/apps/android/app/src/main/java/app/pantopus/android/ui/screens/homes/calendar/HomeAgendaComponents.kt`, `frontend/apps/android/app/src/main/java/app/pantopus/android/ui/screens/homes/calendar/HomeCalendarCreateMenu.kt`, `frontend/apps/android/app/src/main/java/app/pantopus/android/ui/theme/Typography.kt`
- **Verdict:** Both platforms faithfully reproduce the day-grouped agenda, filter chips, FAB create-menu, and all 7 frame variants; iOS is a near-exact match while Android drifts on the month strip (extra event dots, 3-letter weekday, chevron-down, button-chrome chevrons) and an oversized 20sp top-bar title with an extra "Who's free" text label.
- **Cross note:** Both correctly source home pillar colors from tokens (homeBg/home/homeDark) and ship all 7 frame variants (default, create-menu, empty, loading, error, offline, filtered-empty). Key divergence: iOS month strip is a faithful single-letter, dot-less, chrome-less match while Android's strip adds dots, 3-letter weekdays, a chevron-down, and chevron button-chrome — and Android's top bar is oversized with an extra label.

**iOS deviations:**
- `low`/`chrome` — Top bar uses .navigationTitle("Calendar") with .inline mode, centering the title, whereas the design TopBar has center=false (left-aligned 15.5px title). **Fix:** Acceptable native idiom; if exact parity is wanted, render a leading-aligned custom title via a principal/leading toolbar item.
- `low`/`icon` — First-run empty state uses Icon(.calendar) which matches design's EmptyState icon="calendar"; no issue (noted for cross-platform contrast with Android's CalendarDays). **Fix:** No change needed; keep .calendar.

**Android deviations:**
- `med`/`typography` — CalendarTopBar title text uses PantopusTextStyle.h3 (20sp) but the design TopBar title is 15.5px/SemiBold — roughly 29% too large. **Fix:** Use a 15.5.sp SemiBold style for the top-bar title instead of h3.
- `med`/`extra-element` — CalendarTopBar renders a "Who's free" Text label beside the Users icon; the design's right action is icon-only (label is only a hover tooltip). **Fix:** Drop the trailing Text and keep just the Users icon button (keep the contentDescription for a11y).
- `med`/`extra-element` — MonthStripHeader DotsRow renders 1-3 event-count dots under each day cell, but the home-shell MonthStrip explicitly drops per-day dots. **Fix:** Remove the DotsRow from DayCell to match the spec (eventCount stays in state for tests only).
- `low`/`extra-element` — MonthRow adds a ChevronDown glyph next to the month label; the design month label has no dropdown affordance. **Fix:** Remove the PantopusIcon.ChevronDown from the month label row.
- `low`/`typography` — DayCell weekday uses dowFmt 'EEE' uppercased (e.g. "SUN"/"MON") while design renders single-letter initials (S/M/T/W/T/F/S), matching iOS's single-letter dayOfWeek. **Fix:** Project single-letter weekday initials (take first char) like iOS, or set dowFmt to a single-letter pattern.
- `low`/`chrome` — Prev/next month chevrons are wrapped in 26dp sunken-background ChevronButton boxes; design renders them as plain 17px glyphs (muted/secondary tint) with no button chrome. **Fix:** Render bare PantopusIconImage glyphs (~17dp, appTextMuted/appTextSecondary) without the sunken background box.
- `low`/`typography` — Error and filtered-empty headlines use PantopusTextStyle.h3 (20sp) where the design EmptyState/error title is 15.5px bold. **Fix:** Use a 15.5.sp Bold style for these headlines to match the spec and iOS.
- `low`/`spacing` — MonthStripHeader horizontal padding is Spacing.s4 (16dp) vs the design strip's ~10px horizontal padding. **Fix:** Reduce the strip's horizontal padding to ~10dp to match the design container.

### F15 Permission-gated scheduler — iOS `matches` / Android `minor` → better: **ios**
- iOS files: `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Scheduling/Home/GatedScheduler/GatedSchedulerView.swift`, `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Scheduling/Home/GatedScheduler/GatedSchedulerViewModel.swift`
- Android files: `frontend/apps/android/app/src/main/java/app/pantopus/android/ui/screens/scheduling/home/PermissionGatedSchedulerScreen.kt`, `frontend/apps/android/app/src/main/java/app/pantopus/android/ui/screens/scheduling/home/PermissionGatedSchedulerViewModel.kt`, `frontend/apps/android/app/src/main/java/app/pantopus/android/ui/theme/Icons.kt`
- **Verdict:** Both platforms faithfully render all three design frames (read-only, my-assignments, request-pending) with correct chrome, hint bar, sky-outline assignment rows, "Your slot" pill, and Accept/Decline buttons from the token palette; iOS is pixel-faithful while Android substitutes a shield-check (GppGood) glyph for the design's shield-plus on the "Ask to manage" pill.
- **Cross note:** Both platforms correctly gate the MonthStrip to the read-only/pending frames (shown only when assignments is empty) and omit it in the my-assignments frame, and both add loading/no-access/error states beyond the 3 design frames per the four-state convention (not a deviation). Key divergence: Android uses shield-check/GppGood where iOS uses the design's shield-plus.

**iOS deviations:**
- `low`/`other` — AssignmentRow Accept/Decline use clipShape(RoundedRectangle(cornerRadius: Radii.md)) = 8pt; design buttons are borderRadius:9 (corner-radius nit). **Fix:** Use a literal 9pt cornerRadius for the two action buttons to match spec exactly.
- `low`/`typography` — My-assignments overline uses .tracking(0.6) where design letterSpacing:0.06 is em-relative (~0.66pt at 11pt size); negligible difference. **Fix:** Optionally set tracking to 0.66 for exactness; no functional change needed.

**Android deviations:**
- `low`/`icon` — AskToManagePill uses PantopusIcon.ShieldCheck (maps to Material Icons.Filled.GppGood); design GatedTopBar specifies lucide shield-plus (iOS correctly uses .shieldPlus). **Fix:** Add a ShieldPlus case to Icons.kt (lucide shield-plus) and use it on the Ask-to-manage pill.
- `low`/`other` — ActionButton uses RoundedCornerShape(Radii.md) = 8.dp; design Accept/Decline buttons are borderRadius:9 (corner-radius nit). **Fix:** Use RoundedCornerShape(9.dp) for the action buttons.
- `low`/`spacing` — RequestSentBanner is a hand-rolled Row (clip lg, infoBg, s3 padding) rather than the shared Banner component used in design Frame 3; visually equivalent but diverges from the canonical Banner and iOS HomeInfoBanner. **Fix:** Reuse the shared info Banner component for the pending state to match design and iOS.
- `low`/`sizing` — AssignmentRow time column is fixed Modifier.size(width=42.dp, height=36.dp) and the divider Box is fixed height 36.dp; design divider is alignSelf:'stretch' to row height with no fixed 36, so it will not stretch if the title wraps. **Fix:** Use IntrinsicSize.Min on the Row and Modifier.fillMaxHeight() on the divider instead of a hardcoded 36.dp.

### F2 Home event detail — iOS `minor` / Android `major` → better: **ios**
- iOS files: `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Homes/Calendar/EventDetailView.swift`, `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Scheduling/Routing/Stubs/Home/HomeEventDetailStubView.swift`
- Android files: `frontend/apps/android/app/src/main/java/app/pantopus/android/ui/screens/homes/calendar/EventDetailScreen.kt`
- **Verdict:** Both render every section (header, detail grid, attendees w/ RSVP pills, Your RSVP, notes, footer Edit/Delete) plus loaded/loading/error/deleting/offline/pending/recorded states, and both replace the spec's text "Edit" top-bar action with a pencil icon; iOS is faithful save a few chip/divider nits, while Android ships a non-mirroring loading skeleton, undersized card radii, and a neutral category chip that diverge more.
- **Cross note:** Both platforms substitute a pencil icon for the spec's text "Edit" top-bar action — a shared chrome divergence worth fixing on both. iOS otherwise mirrors the spec (4-state skeleton, 16dp cards, dividers, BYDAY recurrence) more faithfully; Android's loading skeleton and 12dp card radii are the key regressions.

**iOS deviations:**
- `med`/`chrome` — ContentDetailTopBarAction uses a .pencil icon button, but spec TopBar right is a text "Edit" label (14/700, home accent700). **Fix:** Render a text "Edit" trailing action in home-green instead of the pencil glyph.
- `med`/`icon` — CategoryPill renders an Icon(category.icon) glyph, but spec CatChip uses a 7×7 colored dot, not a glyph. **Fix:** Replace the leading Icon with a 7pt Circle filled with the category color.
- `med`/`color` — CategoryPill background is category.background (category accent bg, e.g. green), but spec CatChip background is neutral N.sunken (appSurfaceSunken) with only the dot colored. **Fix:** Set the chip background to Theme.Color.appSurfaceSunken and text to appTextStrong.
- `low`/`missing-element` — DetailGrid stacks DetailRows with Spacing.s1 and explicitly draws no inner dividers, but the spec DetailRow carries a 1px N.border bottom divider between rows. **Fix:** Add a 1px appBorder divider between detail rows (omit on last), matching the attendees card.
- `low`/`spacing` — DetailGrid card uses padding .horizontal s3 / .vertical s1, but spec Card pad is 4px/13px (≈vertical 4, horizontal 13). **Fix:** Use ~13pt horizontal and ~4pt vertical inner padding on the detail card.

**Android deviations:**
- `high`/`state` — LoadingShell body renders two plain 320×120 Shimmer rectangles instead of mirroring the loaded geometry; spec FrameLoading shows a detail-grid card of 4 icon-tile rows + an attendees card of 3 avatar rows. **Fix:** Build skeleton cards of icon-tile rows and avatar rows mirroring DetailGrid/Attendees, as iOS LoadingShell does.
- `med`/`chrome` — topBarAction uses PantopusIcon.Pencil, but spec TopBar right is a text "Edit" label (14/700, home accent700). **Fix:** Render a text "Edit" trailing action in home-green instead of the pencil icon.
- `med`/`sizing` — DetailGrid, SectionCard and YourRsvpCard use RoundedCornerShape(Radii.lg)=12dp, but spec Card borderRadius is 16 (Radii.xl). **Fix:** Use Radii.xl (16dp) for all detail cards.
- `med`/`color` — Detail/Notes cards lack the card drop shadow and the pending RSVP card omits the spec's green glow (boxShadow 0 0 0 4px H.bg50) that iOS approximates; Android pending card only switches border color/width. **Fix:** Add the shadow-sm card elevation and a 4dp home-bg glow ring on the pending RSVP card.
- `low`/`spacing` — NotesSection text is padded horizontal s3 / vertical s2 inside SectionCard which itself adds vertical s2, doubling vertical padding vs spec NotesCard (Card pad 13 with body directly under overline). **Fix:** Drop the extra vertical padding on the notes Text so it matches the 13px card padding.
- `low`/`typography` — NotesSection Text sets fontSize 12.5 but no lineHeight; spec body is 12.5 with lineHeight 18. **Fix:** Set lineHeight = 18.sp on the notes text.
- `low`/`missing-element` — recurrenceLabel returns generic "Weekly" and never resolves BYDAY to "Every Monday"; spec DetailGrid shows "Every Monday" and iOS implements the BYDAY→day mapping. **Fix:** Parse BYDAY and return "Every <Day>" like the iOS weeklyDay mapping.

### F3 Home add-edit event — iOS `minor` / Android `major` → better: **ios**
- iOS files: `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Homes/Calendar/AddEventFormView.swift`, `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Shared/Form/FormShell.swift`, `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Scheduling/Routing/Stubs/Home/HomeEventEditorStubView.swift`
- Android files: `frontend/apps/android/app/src/main/java/app/pantopus/android/ui/screens/homes/calendar/AddEventFormScreen.kt`, `frontend/apps/android/app/src/main/java/app/pantopus/android/ui/screens/shared/form/FormShell.kt`, `frontend/apps/android/app/src/main/java/app/pantopus/android/ui/screens/shared/form/FormFieldGroup.kt`
- **Verdict:** Both render every design section in order via a shared FormShell, but iOS's bespoke EventSection faithfully carries the Home-green overlines, pill chips, round check and 16px bordered cards, whereas Android reuses the generic FormFieldGroup (grey overlines, no border, 12px radius) and ships square check/category chips plus a restructured schedule layout — making Android the weaker match.
- **Cross note:** Both platforms share FormShell, so both inherit two identical deviations: the Save action is sky primary600 instead of Home-green H.accent700, and the leading control is an X icon instead of the design's 'Cancel' text button. Key divergence: iOS built a bespoke EventSection (green overline, pill chips, round check, 16px bordered card) that tracks the design, while Android reused the generic FormFieldGroup and kept square chips/checks and a label-above-pills schedule layout.

**iOS deviations:**
- `med`/`color` — Shared FormShell renders the 'Save' action in Theme.Color.primary600 (sky), but design SheetBar (home-shell.jsx:378) draws Save in Home-green H.accent700; this is the Home pillar so the action should be green. **Fix:** Pass a pillar-accent color into FormTopBar action (or override foregroundStyle to Theme.Color.homeDark) for the F3 form.
- `low`/`chrome` — FormShell leading control is an X icon (.x), but design SheetBar uses a left-aligned 'Cancel' text button (fg2, 13.5/600); native dismiss idiom but text label is the spec. **Fix:** Optionally render a 'Cancel' text leading control for sheet-presented forms to match SheetBar.
- `low`/`interaction` — ScheduleGroup uses a .compact DatePicker pill (AddEventFormView.swift:369) instead of the design's static sunken value pill 'Mon Jun 16 · 6:30 PM'; functionally fine but visually a system picker rather than the styled sunken pill. **Fix:** Acceptable as a native picker; optionally style to match the sunken value pill geometry.
- `low`/`typography` — Centered title uses .body (16pt) via FormShell, while design SheetBar title is 14.5px/700; minor size/weight drift. **Fix:** Use ~14.5pt bold for the form title to match SheetBar.

**Android deviations:**
- `high`/`color` — Section overlines use FormFieldGroup's PantopusColors.appTextSecondary (grey), but design Section overlines (add-event-frames.jsx:13) are Home-green H.accent700; iOS correctly uses homeDark. **Fix:** Render F3 sections with a green overline (mirror iOS EventSection) instead of the generic grey FormFieldGroup header.
- `high`/`icon` — AttendeesGroup CheckMark is a square RoundedCornerShape(Radii.xs) box (AddEventFormScreen.kt:508), but design Check (home-shell.jsx:402) is a round (borderRadius 50%) 20px circle; iOS RoundCheck is correctly circular. **Fix:** Make CheckMark a CircleShape 20dp with green fill + white tick.
- `med`/`sizing` — CategoryChip uses RoundedCornerShape(Radii.md=8) (AddEventFormScreen.kt:274), but design CatPick is a full pill (borderRadius 9999); iOS uses Capsule. **Fix:** Clip CategoryChip with RoundedCornerShape(Radii.pill) to make it a pill.
- `med`/`layout` — ScheduleGroup DateTimeRow stacks label-above two separate full-width date/time PickerChips (AddEventFormScreen.kt:336), whereas design ValueRow puts the label left and a single combined value pill right inline; restructures the row. **Fix:** Use an inline label-left / value-pill-right ValueRow with a single combined date·time value to match the design.
- `med`/`sizing` — FormFieldGroup card has no border and uses Radii.lg(12) radius/no shadow (FormFieldGroup.kt:50), but design Card is 1px appBorder, 16px radius, subtle shadow; iOS EventSection uses Radii.xl + 1px border. **Fix:** Give the F3 section cards a 1px appBorder and Radii.xl(16) radius.
- `med`/`extra-element` — RequestRsvpGroup is wrapped in FormFieldGroup(title='RSVP') (AddEventFormScreen.kt:574), adding an 'RSVP' overline the design omits — its RSVP Section has no overline (add-event-frames.jsx:88); iOS uses an overline-less EventSection. **Fix:** Render the RSVP toggle in a borderless, overline-less section.
- `med`/`color` — Shared FormShell 'Save' action is primary600 (sky) not Home-green H.accent700; same pillar miss as iOS, plus generic discard-dialog instead of the design's styled Discard/Keep-editing dialog. **Fix:** Color the F3 commit action Home-green to match the SheetBar Save.
- `low`/`chrome` — FormShell leading is an X icon, but design SheetBar uses a left-aligned 'Cancel' text button; native idiom but differs from spec. **Fix:** Optionally render a 'Cancel' text leading control for the sheet form.

- **Verdict:** Both platforms faithfully implement the F8 exposure-only boundary screen (context header, Personal-sky deep-link, three exposure toggles + quiet-hours disclosure, footnote, not-set-up/saving/opt-out states); iOS is closer because it uses the spec's bespoke 36x20 home-green toggle, the correct moon icon, and exact font sizes, whereas Android substitutes a larger Material Switch, a sunset glyph, and slightly off font sizes plus an extra pillar accent bar.
- **Cross note:** Both platforms correctly cover all four spec frames (default, not-set-up with info banner + CTA, saving inline spinner, opt-out confirm) and gate the footnote + quiet-hours row on personalIsSetUp exactly as the JSX does; the shared divergence is that Android leans on Material primitives (Switch, AlertDialog, sunset icon) while iOS hand-rolls the spec's exact toggle and uses the moon icon.

- `low`/`sizing` — Row icon tiles (DeepLinkRow/HouseholdToggleRow/DisclosureRow) use Radii.md (8) while the spec sets borderRadius:9 on the 32x32 tiles (and 12 on the 40x40 header tile, where iOS uses Radii.lg=12 correctly). **Fix:** Use an explicit 9pt corner radius for the 32x32 row icon tiles to match spec borderRadius:9.

- `med`/`extra-element` — OwnerPillarHeader renders a Home-green pillar accent bar (ACCENT_BAR_HEIGHT) under the title; the spec's TopBar is a plain neutral bar titled 'My availability' with no accent stripe. **Fix:** Hide the accent bar for this screen (or pass a variant without ACCENT_BAR_HEIGHT) so the chrome is a plain TopBar.
- `med`/`sizing` — ToggleRow uses Material3 Switch (~52x32dp) instead of the spec's bespoke 36x20 ToggleGreen with a 16dp thumb; the control is visibly larger than design (iOS matches with a custom GreenSwitch). **Fix:** Replace Material Switch with a custom 36x20 home-green toggle matching the spec primitive.
- `low`/`typography` — ToggleRow title is 13.sp (spec 12.5), subtitle 11.sp (spec 10.5), and DisclosureRow value 12.sp (spec 11.5) — small but consistent oversizing vs spec. **Fix:** Set toggle/disclosure title to 12.5.sp, subtitle to 10.5.sp, and disclosure value to 11.5.sp.
- `low`/`color` — Material Switch checkedThumbColor is set to appTextInverse (white) which is correct, but the unchecked/disabled track relies on SwitchDefaults rather than the spec's borderStrong (off) / sunken (disabled) track colors. **Fix:** Pass uncheckedTrackColor=appBorderStrong and disabledTrackColor=appSurfaceSunken (moot if the switch is replaced by the bespoke 36x20 toggle).

- iOS files: `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Scheduling/Home/FindATime/FindATimeSetupView.swift`, `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Scheduling/Home/FindATime/FindATimeComponents.swift`

- **Verdict:** iOS faithfully renders all six design frames (default, round-robin, invalid, computing, no-overlap, explainer-expanded) with only small color/radius nits; Android omits the computing spinner, the no-overlap warning + quick-action buttons, and the round-robin rule section entirely, so it covers only 3 of 6 states.
- **Cross note:** Both platforms place sections in the correct spec order and use token colors; the divergence is state coverage — iOS implements all six frames, Android only the static form (default + invalid inline errors) and skips computing, no-overlap, and round-robin-rule. Both use a native top-bar (Android adds a back chevron, iOS uses FormShell .close) which is acceptable as a native idiom versus the spec's pure sheet bar. Android's DateWindow also uses a preset dropdown rather than a real from/to range picker, so the invalid 'end before start' state is effectively unreachable.

- `low`/`color` — Explainer body text uses Theme.Color.appTextStrong (#374151) in FindATimeSetupView.explainer; spec sets the primary line to #075985 (primary-800) at fontWeight 500. **Fix:** Color the explainer headline line with Theme.Color.info/primary-800 to match the spec blue.
