- `low`/`sizing` — FindATimeCard uses Radii.xl (16) corner radius; the spec Card/Section radius is 12 (Radii.lg). **Fix:** Use Radii.lg (12) for the section cards to match the spec.

**Android deviations:**
- `high`/`state` — FindATimeSetupUiState only has Loading/Loaded/Error; the spec 'computing' frame (64dp spinner with users glyph, 'Checking everyone's availability' + three shimmer rows) is entirely absent — submit() just navigates without a composing state. **Fix:** Add a Computing UI state rendering the spinner + headline + shimmer rows that iOS' computingBody mirrors.
- `high`/`missing-element` — The spec no-overlap frame's warning banner ('No time works for all 3') and its two quick-action buttons ('Make Dad optional' user-minus, 'Widen to two weeks' calendar-plus) never render; the VM exposes makeSomeoneOptional()/widenWindow() but SetupFormBody never calls them. **Fix:** Render an FtBanner(Warning) plus the user-minus and calendar-plus action buttons when a no-overlap result is present.
- `high`/`missing-element` — The 'Round-robin rule' section (Segmented 'Fair rotation' / 'By role') from the round-robin frame is missing; SetupFormBody never shows a rule picker even though FindMode.RoundRobin is selectable. **Fix:** Add a Round-robin rule FtCard with an FtSegmented shown when form.mode == FindMode.RoundRobin, matching iOS' ruleSection.
- `med`/`icon` — Explainer's second bullet uses PantopusIcon.Users; the spec uses the 'layers' glyph ('Pantopus overlays everyone…') — iOS correctly uses .layers. **Fix:** Change the second explainer bullet icon to PantopusIcon.Layers.
- `med`/`icon` — Stepper minus button uses PantopusIcon.X (close glyph) in StepperButton; spec/iOS use a minus glyph. **Fix:** Use PantopusIcon.Minus for the decrease button.
- `med`/`layout` — Stepper renders two full-width circular buttons spread across the row with a weighted center label; spec/iOS render a compact inline minus / value / plus control bordered as one unit. **Fix:** Rebuild Stepper as a single bordered inline -/value/+ control matching the spec geometry.
- `low`/`icon` — DateWindow uses PantopusIcon.Calendar; the spec uses 'calendar-range' (iOS uses .calendarRange). **Fix:** Switch the date-window leading icon to a calendar-range glyph.

### F5 Find a time slots — iOS `matches` / Android `minor` → better: **ios**

Shared divergence: neither reproduces the spec's radial-gradient ring behind the sent-success check (both use a solid disc), which is an acceptable native simplification.

- `low`/`chrome` — Spec composing frame keeps the trailing 'Edit' action present-but-muted; FindATimeSuggestedView's canEdit hides Edit entirely during .loading/.sent/.booked instead of showing it muted. **Fix:** Show a disabled/muted Edit on the composing phase to match the spec's right={{text:'Edit', muted:true}}.

- `med`/`missing-element` — SubHeadPlaceholder (loading) renders only one 180x12 shimmer bar, dropping the tz-pill and the second availability line; spec/iOS keep the full SubHead chrome during composing. **Fix:** Render the full SubHead skeleton (note bar + tz pill + second line) so loading mirrors loaded geometry.
- `med`/`sizing` — NoOverlapBody circle is 64dp with a 28dp calendar-x icon; spec is a 56px circle with a 26px icon. **Fix:** Change the no-overlap circle to 56dp and icon to 26dp.
- `low`/`missing-element` — ComposingBody shimmer cards stack two text bars (160x12 + 90x10); spec/iOS show a 12-high title bar then a 56x20 pill + 50x9 bar mirroring the avatar-stack row. **Fix:** Replace the second bar with a 56x20 rounded pill + 50x9 bar to mirror the slot's member row.
- `low`/`typography` — SingleBestCard uses h3 (20sp) for the day and body (16sp) for the time; spec is 19px day and 15px time, and card radius Radii.xl (16) vs spec 18. **Fix:** Set day ~19sp / time ~15sp and bump the single-best card radius toward 18dp.
- `low`/`state` — NoOverlap headline is the static 'No time works for everyone' and body says 'this window'; spec uses the member-count 'No time works for all 3' and 'this week'. **Fix:** Interpolate the required-member count into the headline and use 'this week' to match the window phrase.
- `low`/`icon` — Booked SuccessBody reuses PantopusIcon.Check; iOS booked state uses calendar-check, and the success body line differs ('… is set' vs iOS '<title> · <label>'). **Fix:** Use a calendar-check glyph for the booked state to distinguish it from the proposal-sent check.

### F6 Member poll response — iOS `major` / Android `major` → better: **ios**
- iOS files: `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Scheduling/Home/FindATime/PollResponseView.swift`, `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Scheduling/Home/FindATime/FindATimeComponents.swift`
- Android files: `frontend/apps/android/app/src/main/java/app/pantopus/android/ui/screens/scheduling/findatime/MemberPollResponseScreen.kt`, `frontend/apps/android/app/src/main/java/app/pantopus/android/ui/screens/scheduling/findatime/FindATimeComponents.kt`, `frontend/apps/android/app/src/main/java/app/pantopus/android/ui/screens/scheduling/findatime/MemberPollResponseViewModel.kt`, `frontend/apps/android/app/src/main/java/app/pantopus/android/ui/screens/scheduling/findatime/FindATimeModels.kt`
- **Verdict:** Both faithfully render the organizer header, overline, 3-way vote control and closed/expired frame, but neither implements the design's conflicts-detected frame (per-slot conflict pill + "From your personal calendar" line + info pre-fill banner) and both swap the person-photo avatar for a generic icon disc; iOS is marginally closer because it doesn't inject the off-spec name/email capture form Android adds.
- **Cross note:** Shared gap: neither platform implements the conflicts-detected frame (conflict pill, personal-calendar caption, info pre-fill banner) and both replace the organizer person-photo avatar with a generic icon disc. Divergence: iOS adds a dedicated full-screen submitted state; Android instead adds an off-spec name/email capture form and an inline submitted banner, and ties submit-enablement to email presence rather than to having voted.

**iOS deviations:**
- `high`/`missing-element` — No conflicts-detected frame: PollResponseView has only loading/error/ready/closed/submitted, omitting the design's red 'Conflicts: Dentist' pill (errorBg/#b91c1c) on a slot, the 'From your personal calendar' line (10pt fg3 + calendar icon), and the info pre-fill banner. **Fix:** Add a conflict flag to PollOptionRow and render the conflict pill + calendar caption inside pollSlot(), plus an info-tone banner above the slots when any slot conflicts.
- `med`/`icon` — organizerHeader draws Icon(.users) inside a homeBg circle, but the design uses Avatar m={M.mom} — a person photo for the organizer, not a generic users glyph. **Fix:** Render the organizer's MemberAvatarBadge / photo at 38pt instead of the users icon disc.
- `med`/`spacing` — pollSlot is a FindATimeCard padded Spacing.s4 (16pt) all around; the design PollSlot uses pad 11px/13px and a 9px gap between label and control. **Fix:** Use ~12pt vertical / 13pt horizontal padding for the slot card to match the tighter design rhythm.
- `low`/`state` — Adds a full-screen .submitted success state (84pt circle + 'Response submitted' + Done) that has no corresponding design frame (design just keeps the answered sheet). **Fix:** Acceptable as a confirmation, but verify against intended UX; design shows no separate success screen.
- `low`/`sizing` — voteControl track uses Radii.lg (12) and segments Radii.sm (6); design uses borderRadius 9 for the track and 7 for segments. **Fix:** Use a 9pt track radius and 7pt segment radius (or nearest token) for exact parity.
- `low`/`chrome` — Uses navigationTitle('Respond') on a pushed NavigationStack screen; the design is a Sheet with an explicit 'Close' cancel control in the SheetBar. **Fix:** Present as a sheet with a leading 'Close' button, or confirm push navigation is the intended container.

**Android deviations:**
- `high`/`missing-element` — No conflicts-detected frame: MemberPollResponseScreen lacks the per-slot red 'Conflicts: Dentist' pill, the 'From your personal calendar' line, and the info pre-fill banner that the design's FrameConflicts shows. **Fix:** Add conflict data to PollOptionUi and render the conflict pill + calendar caption in PollOptionCard, plus an Info-tone FtBanner above the slots when conflicts exist.
- `high`/`extra-element` — LoadedPoll injects an off-spec 'Your details' card with name + email FtInputFields (state.needsEmail) and gates submit on a non-blank email (canSubmit requires voterEmail); the design has no email/name capture and disables submit only until a vote is cast. **Fix:** Remove the email/name capture for the member flow (member is signed-in) and gate Submit on at least one vote, matching the design's disabled-until-answered footer.
- `med`/`icon` — OrganizerHeader puts a Vote glyph in a homeBg circle; the design uses the organizer's person photo (Avatar mom) at 38dp. **Fix:** Render the organizer avatar (FtAvatar/photo) at 38dp instead of the Vote icon disc.
- `med`/`extra-element` — After submit, an in-place FtBanner 'Response submitted' appears inside the Loaded list and the CTA flips to 'Update response'; the design's answered frame shows neither an inline success banner nor an Update label. **Fix:** Drop the inline success banner / 'Update response' relabel, or align with the intended confirmation pattern.
- `low`/`sizing` — VoteControl track uses Radii.md (8) and segments Radii.sm (6); design uses 9 (track) and 7 (segments). **Fix:** Adjust to a 9dp track radius and 7dp segment radius for exact parity.
- `low`/`chrome` — FtTopBar uses backIcon = X with a centered 'Respond' title and a 1dp divider; matches the sheet 'Close' intent well, but the design SheetBar 'Close' is a text label rather than an X glyph. **Fix:** Optionally use a 'Close' text control to mirror the SheetBar exactly; the X is an acceptable native idiom.

### F7 Whos free — iOS `matches` / Android `major` → better: **ios**
- iOS files: `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Scheduling/Home/FindATime/WhosFreeView.swift`, `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Scheduling/Home/FindATime/FindATimeComponents.swift`
- Android files: `frontend/apps/android/app/src/main/java/app/pantopus/android/ui/screens/scheduling/findatime/WhosFreeScreen.kt`, `frontend/apps/android/app/src/main/java/app/pantopus/android/ui/screens/scheduling/findatime/WhosFreeViewModel.kt`, `frontend/apps/android/app/src/main/java/app/pantopus/android/ui/screens/scheduling/findatime/FindATimeComponents.kt`
- **Verdict:** iOS faithfully reproduces all five frames and all five cell states with the hatch texture and correct icons; Android drops the Tentative and Off-hours cell states entirely, omits the offline-cached frame, and uses wrong icons, so iOS is materially closer to the design.
- **Cross note:** Both platforms render the tap-to-plan affordance as an inline action card rather than a floating popover; iOS additionally uses a true .popover. Android's biggest gap is reducing the five-tier heat grid to three tiers (no Tentative/Off-hours) and omitting the offline frame, neither of which iOS drops.

**iOS deviations:**
- `low`/`sizing` — popoverCard uses .frame(width: 200) but the design popover is width:134. **Fix:** Reduce the popover frame width toward ~134 to match spec proportions.
- `low`/`missing-element` — offlineBanner body is "Reconnect to refresh availability." — the design's "Last updated 2h ago." lead sentence is dropped. **Fix:** Prepend the last-synced timing sentence to the offline banner body.
- `low`/`color` — Off-hours and unknown cells both fill with appSurfaceMuted, whereas design uses distinct fills (off=#f9fafb vs unknown=#f1f3f5) differentiated mainly by hatch pattern; visually close since both are hatched. **Fix:** Optionally map off-hours to appSurfaceMuted and unknown to a slightly cooler surface to mirror the two base tones.

**Android deviations:**
- `high`/`missing-element` — CellState enum is only Free/Busy/Unknown (WhosFreeViewModel.kt:27); the design's Tentative (#fef3c7) and Off-hours (#f9fafb hatched) cell states are entirely absent, so the heat grid loses two of five availability tiers. **Fix:** Add Tentative and OffHours to CellState, fill amber-bg and muted-surface respectively, and project them from slot data.
- `high`/`missing-element` — No offline-cached frame: WhosFreeScreen has no wifiOff amber banner and the card is never dimmed to 0.6, unlike design Frame 5. **Fix:** Add an offline state that renders the FtBanner(Warning, WifiOff) and wraps the grid card at 0.6 alpha.
- `med`/`missing-element` — Legend() lists only Free/Busy/Unknown (WhosFreeScreen.kt:362); design legend is Free/Busy/Tentative/Off-hours (and swaps Off-hours→Unknown only in the opted-out frame). **Fix:** Render four legend items matching the active cell tiers, swapping Off-hours→Unknown when a member is opted out.
- `med`/`icon` — Head explainer line uses PantopusIcon.Users (WhosFreeScreen.kt:146); design ExplainerLine uses the layers glyph. **Fix:** Swap to PantopusIcon.Layers tinted home green.
- `med`/`icon` — "Tap a free block to plan something" hint uses PantopusIcon.Plus (WhosFreeScreen.kt:209); design uses hand-pointer. **Fix:** Use PantopusIcon.HandPointer (or nearest pointer glyph) to match intent.
- `med`/`color` — Off-hours/unknown cells lack the 45° diagonal hatch texture the design draws (Cell off/unknown backgroundImage); Unknown just fills appSurfaceRaised with a flat "?". **Fix:** Add a diagonal-hatch overlay (mirroring iOS DiagonalHatch) clipped to the cell for off-hours and unknown states.
- `low`/`typography` — Explainer/hint text uses PantopusTextStyle.caption (12sp) where design specifies fontSize 10.5; column headers/labels also map to overline/caption rather than the 9/10.5 spec sizes. **Fix:** Use explicit ~10.5sp for explainer/hint and 9sp bold for column headers to match the dense grid spec.
- `low`/`sizing` — NAME_COL_WIDTH is 64.dp; design name column is 58px. **Fix:** Set NAME_COL_WIDTH = 58.dp.

### F10 Resource editor — iOS `minor` / Android `major` → better: **ios**
- iOS files: `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Scheduling/Home/Resources/ResourceEditorView.swift`, `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Shared/Form/FormShell.swift`, `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Shared/Form/FormFieldGroup.swift`
- Android files: `frontend/apps/android/app/src/main/java/app/pantopus/android/ui/screens/scheduling/resources/ResourceEditorScreen.kt`, `frontend/apps/android/app/src/main/java/app/pantopus/android/ui/screens/scheduling/resources/ResourceComponents.kt`
- **Verdict:** iOS faithfully renders all five sections plus the collapsible booking-rules disclosure, photo row, and the dedicated saving overlay; Android drops the Photo section and the booking-rules collapse/helper, swaps the segmented Who-can-book for chips, and degrades both the saving and delete-confirm frames, making iOS clearly closer to the spec.
- **Cross note:** Both platforms correctly use the home-green pillar, SelectChip type pills, WeekdayPicker, and CounterRow stepper; the key divergence is that iOS implements all five spec frames (create/edit/invalid/saving/delete) faithfully while Android omits the Photo section and the collapsible booking-rules disclosure and falls back to generic Material dialogs/spinner for the saving and delete states.

**iOS deviations:**
- `med`/`extra-element` — detailsGroup wraps the name+type card in FormFieldGroup("Details"), adding a grey 'DETAILS' overline above the first card; the design's first Section has no overline at all. **Fix:** Render the name+type card as a bare Card (no overline label) to match FrameCreate's first Section.
- `med`/`color` — FormFieldGroup renders every section overline in Theme.Color.appTextSecondary (grey, placed above the card), but the spec's Overline uses H.accent700 home-green placed inside the card. **Fix:** Tint section overlines home-green (Theme.Color.homeDark) and keep them inside the card surface as the rules section already does.
- `low`/`interaction` — whoCanBookGroup uses a native SwiftUI .segmented Picker; the spec uses a custom small/full Segmented control with home accent — acceptable native idiom but loses the green selected tint. **Fix:** Optionally use a home-tinted segmented control to match the accent; low priority.
- `low`/`icon` — hoursGroup uses native DatePicker wheels for start/end, whereas the design renders a static sunken pill '7 AM – 10 PM' value row; functional parity but visually heavier than spec. **Fix:** Render a tappable value pill matching N.sunken background per HoursWindow ValueRow, opening a picker on tap.
- `low`/`chrome` — FormShell top bar uses pantopusTextStyle(.body) 16pt title and primary600 (sky) for the enabled Save action; spec SheetBar title is fine but the pillar accent for Save would read home-green. **Fix:** Pass a home accent to the FormShell Save action so the enabled label is home-green, matching the Home-pillar sheet.

**Android deviations:**
- `high`/`missing-element` — EditorBody has no Photo section; the spec's FrameCreate includes a Section overline="Photo" with the dashed 'Add a photo · Optional' PhotoRow (image-plus icon, 34dp tile). **Fix:** Add a SectionCard(overline="Photo") containing a dashed PhotoAddRow mirroring the iOS PhotoAddRow.
- `high`/`missing-element` — Booking rules is a plain always-open SectionCard with no chevron, no collapse, and no smart-defaults helper line; the spec's RulesDisclosure is a collapsible header (chevron-down/up) that shows a defaultHelper (e.g. 'Charger defaults: 4 hr max · No approval') when collapsed. **Fix:** Wrap the rules rows in a collapsible disclosure with a chevron and the ruleHelper subtitle, defaulting collapsed on create like iOS rulesGroup.
- `med`/`interaction` — Who-can-book is rendered as three weight(1f) SelectChip pills, but the spec uses a Segmented control with options All / Specific / Guest link. **Fix:** Replace the chip row with a segmented control matching the design's Segmented small/full component.
- `med`/`state` — Saving state only swaps the top-bar action for a CircularProgressIndicator; the spec FrameSaving dims the form (opacity 0.45) and floats a centered white card with a spinning green loader-circle + 'Saving resource' label. **Fix:** Add a dimmed overlay with a centered rounded white card (radius 16, shadow) showing a home-green spinner and 'Saving resource', mirroring iOS savingOverlay.
- `med`/`state` — Delete confirm uses a default Material AlertDialog; the spec FrameDelete is a custom Dialog with a trash-2 error icon, full-width 44dp red Delete + bordered Keep buttons stacked vertically. **Fix:** Use a custom dialog with the trash-2 error glyph and two stacked full-width 44dp buttons (red Delete, bordered Keep).
- `med`/`missing-element` — The name+type card has no Photo and the invalid frame's name-field error helper text matches, but there is no Type label color/divider parity — the spec separates Name and Type within the first card with marginTop:11 and a 'Type' label; Android stacks them via SectionCard's 12dp gap with no divider (iOS adds a Divider). Minor structural drift inside the first card. **Fix:** Match spec spacing: 11dp gap between name field and the 'Type' label; the design has no divider so this is acceptable but keep the 11dp rhythm.
- `low`/`typography` — SectionCard overline is 10sp; the spec Overline (--type-over) is 11px. Slightly undersized. **Fix:** Bump SectionCard overline fontSize to 11sp to match the overline token.
- `low`/`sizing` — hoursGroup renders two stacked PickerValueRow rows ('Available from'/'Available until') with chevrons; the spec HoursWindow shows a single 'Available hours' value row reading '7 AM – 10 PM'. **Fix:** Collapse to a single 'Available hours' row showing the start–end range, opening a combined picker.

- **Verdict:** iOS faithfully renders all five frames (loaded, loading, fully-booked banner + next-opening CTA, pending-approval badge + inline queue, error), while Android omits the fully-booked and pending-approval states entirely and hardcodes the bookings label, so it covers only loaded/loading/error/approval-queue.

- `high`/`missing-element` — Sticky CTA is always 'Book this' (plus icon); spec Frame 3 swaps it to 'Book next opening · Sat 9 AM' with a calendar-clock icon when fully booked. **Fix:** Branch StickyFooter on isFullyBooked to show the next-opening CTA + calendar-clock icon.
- `high`/`missing-element` — No pending-approval badge in HeaderCard; spec Frame 4 shows an amber clock 'Pending approval (N)' button with chevron-right inside the header card. **Fix:** Add pendingApprovalCount to Loaded and render the warning-bordered badge button in HeaderCard, mirroring iOS pendingApprovalBadge.
- `med`/`state` — Bookings overline is hardcoded 'Upcoming bookings'; spec Frame 4 relabels it 'Confirmed' when the approval queue is shown above. **Fix:** Compute label = if (approvals.isEmpty) "Upcoming bookings" else "Confirmed", as iOS does.
- `med`/`sizing` — BookingRow status dot is Modifier.size(6.dp); spec BookingRow dot is width:5,height:5. **Fix:** Set the dot to 5.dp.
- `low`/`sizing` — HomePrimaryButton/InlineHomeButton corner radius is Radii.md/Radii.sm; spec PrimaryBtn is 12 and Approve/Decline buttons are borderRadius:9. **Fix:** Use Radii.lg (12) for the primary CTA and ~9 for the inline approve/decline buttons.
- `low`/`color` — RuleChipView and approval overline use PantopusColors.home (#16a34a) and PantopusColors.warning; spec uses accent700 for chip text and warning700 for the 'Approval queue · N' overline. **Fix:** Use home-700 for rule chip text and warning-700 for the approval-queue overline.
- `low`/`layout` — Loading state uses generic SchedulingLoadingSkeleton(rows=4) row list; spec Frame 2 is a header-card shimmer (icon tile + name + 3 chips) over 3 booking-row skeletons. **Fix:** Replace with a skeleton mirroring the loaded header-card + booking-row geometry.

### F12 Book a resource — iOS `minor` / Android `major` → better: **ios**
- iOS files: `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Scheduling/Home/Resources/BookResourceView.swift`, `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Scheduling/Home/Resources/ResourceComponents.swift`

- **Verdict:** iOS faithfully reproduces all six design frames (rules chips, hour grid, conflict line, for-whom, notes, dimmed submitting overlay, and both success variants with note pill); Android nails the form/grid/conflict/success core but drops three design elements — the Notes section, the dimmed "Booking the charger" submitting overlay, and the success note pill.

- `high`/`state` — Design Frame 4 (submitting) dims the sheet to opacity 0.45 and overlays a centered rounded card with a spinning loader-circle + 'Booking the charger'; BookForm only passes isLoading to the footer button — no dimmed overlay or spinner card. **Fix:** Wrap BookForm in a Box; when form.isSubmitting, dim content to 0.45/disable hits and overlay a centered Surface(radius 16) with a rotating PantopusIcon.LoaderCircle + 'Booking the charger' text.
- `med`/`missing-element` — Design Frames 5/6 show a success note pill (calendar-check icon + 'Added to the home calendar' / 'EV charger · Sat 9–11 AM') in home-green; BookSuccess has no pill and the VM folds that text into the body string instead. **Fix:** Add a note field to Success state and render a pill (PantopusIcon.CalendarCheck + text, homeBg bg, homeDark text, Radii.pill) between body and the Back-to-calendar button, like iOS successNote.
- `low`/`sizing` — Success disc icon in BookSuccess is size = 26.dp; design SuccessSheet icon is width/height 28 (iOS uses 28). **Fix:** Change the PantopusIconImage size to 28.dp.
- `low`/`chrome` — Design SheetBar carries a trailing 'Submit' action with disabled/saving variants; CenterAlignedTopAppBar exposes only a back chevron + title, submit lives in the sticky footer. **Fix:** Acceptable native idiom; optionally mirror the SheetBar trailing action as a TopAppBar action for state parity.

### F9 Resources list — iOS `major` / Android `major` → better: **android**
- iOS files: `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Scheduling/Home/Resources/ResourceListView.swift`, `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Scheduling/Home/Resources/ResourceListViewModel.swift`, `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Scheduling/Home/Resources/ResourceKit.swift`, `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Shared/ListOfRows/ListOfRowsView.swift`, `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Shared/ListOfRows/RowModel.swift`, `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Core/Design/Components/StatusChip.swift`
- Android files: `frontend/apps/android/app/src/main/java/app/pantopus/android/ui/screens/scheduling/resources/ResourceListScreen.kt`, `frontend/apps/android/app/src/main/java/app/pantopus/android/ui/screens/scheduling/resources/ResourceListViewModel.kt`, `frontend/apps/android/app/src/main/java/app/pantopus/android/ui/screens/shared/list_of_rows/ListOfRowsScreen.kt`, `frontend/apps/android/app/src/main/java/app/pantopus/android/ui/screens/shared/list_of_rows/ListOfRowsUiState.kt`, `frontend/apps/android/app/src/main/java/app/pantopus/android/ui/components/StatusChip.kt`
- **Verdict:** Both platforms route F9 through the shared ListOfRows shell and faithfully reproduce the chrome (centered "Resources" title, back chevron, "Add" trailing) but share the same row-typography/trailing-treatment misses and both drop the design's signature empty-state template quick-start; Android edges ahead by rendering rows as individual cards (matching the design) where iOS groups them into one divider-separated card, though Android alone omits the offline frame entirely.
- **Cross note:** Both screens are driven by the same shared ListOfRows shell, so they share three high-impact misses identically: the empty-state templates quick-start is replaced by a generic EmptyState+CTA, row titles are oversized (16pt/sp semibold vs design 13.5px/700), and the trailing free/booked indicator is a filled pill instead of the design's dot+colored-text. Key divergence: iOS groups rows into a single divider card (style .card) while Android uses flat individual cards (matches design); conversely Android omits the offline banner that iOS provides.

**iOS deviations:**
- `high`/`missing-element` — Empty frame uses the shared EmptyState (icon+headline+subcopy+'Add a resource' CTA button); the design's empty frame is an explainer Card + 'TEMPLATES' overline + 5 tappable template rows (Guest room/Driveway/EV charger/Tools/Other) with NO primary button. VM comment acknowledges the shell can't render it. **Fix:** Add a bespoke templates empty-state slot to ListOfRowsView (or a feature-local empty view) rendering the explainer card + TEMPLATES overline + 5 template rows; drop the CTA button.
- `med`/`layout` — rebuild() emits RowSection with style: .card, so the 5 rows render inside ONE rounded card with hairline dividers; the design renders each resource as a separate Card (gap:9 between them, individual borders/shadows). **Fix:** Pass style: .flat in the RowSection so each row is a standalone card, matching the design and Android.
- `med`/`typography` — Row title renders via RowView titleLine at body 16pt semibold; design name is fontSize 13.5 weight 700. **Fix:** Shell-level: the statusChip template title should render ~13.5pt bold for these rows (or add a compact title variant).
- `med`/`color` — Trailing status renders as a filled StatusChip pill (successBg/homeSunken background); design trailing is a bare 7px colored dot + 11pt colored text ('Free now' in success, 'Booked until…' in fg3) with no pill background. **Fix:** Add a dot+label trailing variant (RowTrailing) that renders a 7pt dot + plain colored text instead of reusing the pill StatusChip.
- `low`/`sizing` — Leading tile uses Radii.md (8pt) corner; design tile radius is 11px. Type badge text is caption (~12pt); design badge is 10px. **Fix:** Use an 11pt corner for the type tile and a 10pt label for the type badge to match the spec.
- `low`/`state` — Offline frame: .offlineBanner shows the strip, but the design also dims each cached row to 0.55 opacity ('Showing cached resources'); rows are not dimmed when offline. **Fix:** Thread an isOffline flag into row building to apply 0.55 opacity to rows while offline.

**Android deviations:**
- `high`/`missing-element` — Empty frame maps to the shared EmptyState (Package icon + headline + subcopy + 'Add a resource' CTA); the design's empty frame is an explainer Card + 'TEMPLATES' overline + 5 tappable template rows with no primary button. **Fix:** Add a templates empty-state slot to ListOfRowsScreen (or render a feature-local empty composable) with the explainer card + TEMPLATES overline + 5 template rows; remove the CTA button.
- `high`/`state` — ResourceListScreen has NO OfflineBanner in its chrome stack, so the design's Frame 5 (amber 'You're offline' banner + dimmed cached rows) is entirely absent; iOS at least shows the offline strip. **Fix:** Wrap the screen body with OfflineBanner (ui/components/OfflineBanner.kt) and dim rows to 0.55 alpha when offline, mirroring iOS.
- `med`/`typography` — Row title renders via ContentColumn at PantopusTextStyle.body (16sp) SemiBold; design name is 13.5px weight 700. **Fix:** Render the statusChip-template title at ~13.5sp Bold for resource rows (compact title variant in the shell).
- `med`/`color` — Trailing status uses the filled StatusChip pill (Success/Neutral background); design trailing is a 7px colored dot + 11px colored text with no pill. **Fix:** Add a dot+label RowTrailing variant rendering a 7dp dot + plain colored text instead of the pill StatusChip.
- `low`/`sizing` — TypeIcon leading tile uses RoundedCornerShape(Radii.md)=8dp; design tile radius is 11px. The type RowChip label is caption (~12sp) vs design 10px. **Fix:** Use an 11dp corner on the type tile and a 10sp label for the type chip.
- `low`/`spacing` — Loaded list uses Flat rows spaced by Spacing.s2 (8dp); design gap between resource cards is 9px (close, acceptable) but row internal padding is Spacing.s3 (12dp all sides) vs design pad 11px×12px. **Fix:** Minor — tighten vertical row padding to ~11dp to match the design's 11×12 card padding.

- **Verdict:** Both platforms intentionally reduced the design's offer-slots/composed-availability engine to a plain concrete-visit form (date+start-time+length) and dropped the weekday grid, time-range presets, shareable-link toggle, and 3 of 5 frame states; Android is marginally closer because it uses the Home-green section overline and the spec's explainer copy, while iOS uses a gray overline and off-spec explainer text.

**Android deviations:**
- `high`/`missing-element` — "Offer these times" WeekdayGrid (7 cells height 30dp radius 8, Home-green selected) + preset chips ("Mornings only"/"9 AM – 12 PM") from spec FrameDefault are absent; the "When" SectionCard only has Date/Start time/Visit length rows. **Fix:** Add a WeekdayGrid composable + preset chip FlowRow under a "Offer these times" SectionCard.
- `high`/`missing-element` — "Generate a shareable booking link" toggle section (spec FrameDefault final Section: ValueRow + Toggle) is missing entirely. **Fix:** Add a trailing SectionCard with a ValueRow + Switch bound to a generateLink form field.
- `high`/`state` — VisitSetupLoadState only has Loading/Ready/Error; the spec's no-host-available (warning banner + add-host/widen-window buttons), generating (door-open spinner + "Building the slots you'll offer" + shimmers), and link-created success (check medallion + copy-link row + Share button) frames are unimplemented (VM marks the engine out of scope). **Fix:** Add NoHostAvailable/Generating/LinkCreated states and screens mirroring FrameNoHost/FrameGenerating/FrameLinkCreated.
- `low`/`layout` — "Who must be home" subtitle is static "Required at home" and lacks the spec's contextual "Free: none in this window" plus the "Add another host" CTA shown in the no-host frame. **Fix:** Drive member subtitle from availability and add the host CTA when implementing the no-host state.

### F14 Visit detail — iOS `major` / Android `major` → better: **ios**
- iOS files: `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Scheduling/Home/Resources/VisitDetailView.swift`, `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Scheduling/Home/Resources/VisitDetailViewModel.swift`
- Android files: `frontend/apps/android/app/src/main/java/app/pantopus/android/ui/screens/scheduling/visits/VisitDetailScreen.kt`, `frontend/apps/android/app/src/main/java/app/pantopus/android/ui/screens/scheduling/visits/VisitDetailViewModel.kt`
- **Verdict:** Both platforms deliberately collapse the design's 9-state offer/reserve/link lifecycle into just Confirmed/Done (no backend), so both drop the ShareManage card and all link/banner states; iOS is closer because it renders the 4-step Status timeline and the Completed terminal chip, both of which Android omits.
- **Cross note:** Both platforms share the same documented backend limitation: F14's offer/reserve/link lifecycle (ShareManage card + 7 of 9 states) has no v1 backend, so neither renders it — this is the largest shared gap. Key divergence: iOS implements the Status timeline and Completed terminal chip and correctly suppresses the Done banner, while Android drops the timeline, omits the terminal chip, and adds a non-spec 'Visit complete' Done banner.

**iOS deviations:**
- `high`/`missing-element` — ShareManage card (link status pill, monospace link row, Copy/QR buttons, Slots counter, Revoke/Extend/Preview text-btns) is entirely absent; design shows it in 6 of 9 states (offered/reserved/active-link/expired/revoked). **Fix:** Add a ShareManage SectionCard when an offer/booking link exists, with the link state pill, link code row, Copy/QR actions, slots line, and Revoke/Extend/Preview footer.
- `high`/`state` — Only confirmed/done lifecycles modeled; the design's offered, reserved, cancelled, no-show, active-link, expired-link, revoked states (each with distinct banner, time tone, terminal chip and footer CTAs) are not rendered. **Fix:** Extend Lifecycle to cover offered/reserved/cancelled/no-show/link states once backend exists; map each to its banner, timeColor, terminalChip and footer per spec.
- `med`/`missing-element` — Reserved-state amber 'Visitor picked a time' Banner and Confirm/Decline footer, plus cancelled/no-show error/warning banners, are not implemented; only the confirmed 'On the home calendar' home banner exists. **Fix:** Add reserved/cancelled/no-show banner variants and the Confirm+Decline footer pairing keyed off lifecycle.
- `low`/`typography` — Status overline uses tracking(0.6) at size 10; design Overline is fontSize 9–11 with letterSpacing 0.06em (~0.6–0.66px) — close, acceptable, but Done-state body banner is suppressed correctly. **Fix:** No change needed; tracking is within tolerance.
- `low`/`icon` — Header avatar uses categoryUnboxing gradient as a proxy for the design's fixed teal #2dd4bf→#0d9488 'PV' badge; intent matches but token is a category alias not the visit-teal. **Fix:** Confirm categoryUnboxing maps to teal 2dd4bf/0d9488; if not, introduce a dedicated visit-teal token.

**Android deviations:**
- `high`/`missing-element` — The Status timeline card (4-step Offered→Reserved→Confirmed→Done with numbered/check circles and connectors) is completely absent from VisitLoaded; iOS renders it and the design makes it the second card in every state. **Fix:** Add a StatusTimeline composable (Status overline + row of 22dp step circles, check icon when done, 2dp connectors, home accent fill) and place it after the banner.
- `med`/`extra-element` — LifecycleBanner renders a 'Visit complete' banner for the Done state, but the design's Completed state has no banner — only the header terminal chip plus timeline at Done. **Fix:** Return no banner (skip the Row) when lifecycle == Done, matching the design and iOS.
- `med`/`missing-element` — Done-state header omits the green 'Completed' terminal chip; HeaderCard never renders a terminalChip, whereas the design (and iOS) show a successBg/check pill for completed/cancelled/no-show. **Fix:** Add a terminalChip slot in HeaderCard's top row rendered for Done (Completed, check, successBg/#047857).
- `high`/`missing-element` — ShareManage card and the offered/reserved/cancelled/no-show/active-link/expired/revoked states are not implemented (same backend gap as iOS). **Fix:** Once the offer/link backend exists, add a ShareManage card and the remaining lifecycle banners/footers per spec.
- `low`/`color` — Done-state timeText uses appTextSecondary (fg3) as the muted tone; design's muted time tone is fg3 (#6b7280) so this matches, but the absent timeline means the Done progress affordance is lost. **Fix:** Resolved by adding the timeline; time color is fine.

### G5 Business scheduling settings — iOS `minor` / Android `major` → better: **ios**
- iOS files: `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Scheduling/Business/Settings/BusinessSchedulingSettingsView.swift`, `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Scheduling/Business/Shared/BusinessKit.swift`, `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Core/Design/Spacing.swift`, `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Core/Design/Colors.swift`
- Android files: `frontend/apps/android/app/src/main/java/app/pantopus/android/ui/screens/scheduling/business/BusinessSchedulingSettingsScreen.kt`, `frontend/apps/android/app/src/main/java/app/pantopus/android/ui/screens/scheduling/business/BusinessKit.kt`, `frontend/apps/android/app/src/main/java/app/pantopus/android/ui/screens/scheduling/_shared/SchedulingStateScaffolding.kt`, `frontend/apps/android/app/src/main/java/app/pantopus/android/ui/theme/Color.kt`, `frontend/apps/android/app/src/main/java/app/pantopus/android/ui/theme/Spacing.kt`
- **Verdict:** Both platforms reproduce all five frames with the correct section order (Intro · Confirmation · Scheduling · Policy · Notifications · Payments) and gated/auto/payments variants; iOS is a faithful hand-built mirror with only icon-glyph and overline nits, while Android has a wrong loading-skeleton geometry and an off-palette Stripe disc that push it to major.
- **Cross note:** Both share the same two icon-glyph misses (Buffers should be git-commit-horizontal; iOS gets Booking-horizon right with calendarRange but Android wrongly uses CalendarDays). Key divergence: iOS faithfully mirrors the 1/4/2 shimmer geometry and uses a real Stripe-brand token, whereas Android falls back to a generic 5-card skeleton and a violet magicBg disc — the two reasons it lands at major while iOS is minor.

**iOS deviations:**
- `low`/`icon` — Buffers row uses Icon(.arrowRightLeft); spec SRow icon is git-commit-horizontal (the buffers/commit glyph). **Fix:** Add a gitCommitHorizontal PantopusIcon case and use it for the Buffers row.
- `low`/`typography` — BizOverline renders font size 10 / tracking 0.8; spec Overline token is 11px, weight 600, letter-spacing 0.06em (≈0.66 at 11px). **Fix:** Set BizOverline to .system(size: 11, weight: .semibold) with tracking ~0.66.
- `low`/`color` — Stripe disc background is stripeBrand.opacity(0.10) derived; spec uses a dedicated C.stripeBg / C.stripe pair — acceptable since stripeBrand is a real token, but the 0.10 wash is lighter than the spec's solid stripeBg. **Fix:** Define an explicit stripeBg token and pass it as iconBg rather than a 0.10 opacity of the glyph color.
- `low`/`state` — iOS adds an error frame (BizSettingsError) that the spec does not show; this is required by the four-state rule but is an extra vs the 5 design frames. **Fix:** Keep it — additive per state-rule; no change needed, noted for completeness.

**Android deviations:**
- `high`/`state` — Loading uses generic SchedulingLoadingSkeleton(rows=5) — five identical plain cards with two text shimmers each; spec FrameLoading is three ShimGroups of 1/4/2 rows, each row a 32x32 disc + two stacked text lines, with a 90x9 overline shimmer above each group. **Fix:** Build a feature-local 1/4/2 ShimGroup skeleton with overline shimmer + 32dp disc + two text lines per row, mirroring iOS BizSettingsSkeleton.
- `high`/`color` — Stripe disc uses PantopusColors.magicBg (#EDE9FE lavender) with categoryTask (#4F46E5 indigo) glyph; spec uses Stripe-brand C.stripeBg/C.stripe, and iOS uses a stripeBrand token — Android reads as a violet magic chip, not the Stripe swatch. **Fix:** Add a stripeBrand/stripeBg color token and use it for the Stripe payments disc bg + glyph.
- `med`/`icon` — Booking horizon row uses PantopusIcon.CalendarDays; spec SRow icon is calendar-range. **Fix:** Use a CalendarRange icon for the Booking horizon row.
- `low`/`icon` — Buffers row uses PantopusIcon.ArrowRightLeft; spec icon is git-commit-horizontal. **Fix:** Add a GitCommitHorizontal icon and use it for the Buffers row.
- `med`/`sizing` — Connect button is a Box with vertical=6.dp padding and no fixed height (caption text style); spec button is height 28, horizontal padding 13, font 11.5/700. **Fix:** Constrain the Connect button to height 28.dp with 13.dp horizontal padding and 11.5sp bold label.
- `low`/`typography` — Confirmation description and SettingsRow sub use PantopusTextStyle.caption (12sp); spec description is 10.5px and row sub is fontSize 11. **Fix:** Use ~10.5sp for the confirmation description and 11sp for row sub-labels.
- `low`/`chrome` — BizTopBar height is 48.dp (TOP_BAR_HEIGHT); spec/iOS top bar is 46pt. **Fix:** Set TOP_BAR_HEIGHT to 46.dp to match the spec frame height.
- `low`/`spacing` — loadedBody/SettingsBody uses horizontal padding Spacing.s4 (16) while iOS uses Spacing.s3 (12) and the spec Scroll inset is the kit's standard gutter; the wider 16dp gutter narrows cards vs spec. **Fix:** Align outer horizontal padding to 12.dp to match the spec gutter and iOS.

## Packages

### G10 Buy package — iOS `minor` / Android `minor` → better: **ios**
- iOS files: `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Scheduling/Business/Packages/BuyPackageView.swift`, `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Scheduling/Business/Packages/PackagesKit.swift`, `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Core/Design/Icons.swift`
- Android files: `frontend/apps/android/app/src/main/java/app/pantopus/android/ui/screens/scheduling/packages/BuyPackageScreen.kt`, `frontend/apps/android/app/src/main/java/app/pantopus/android/ui/screens/scheduling/packages/PackagesKit.kt`, `frontend/apps/android/app/src/main/java/app/pantopus/android/ui/theme/Icons.kt`
- **Verdict:** Both platforms are faithful, near-identical mirrors of the 4-frame checkout sheet (logged-in/guest/declined/upsell) plus added loading/paid/error states; both adapt the spec's mock VISA card chip to a neutral "Add a payment method" placeholder, and Android alone uses two wrong icon glyphs in the eligibility and upsell rows.
- **Cross note:** Both platforms intentionally replace the spec's mock data (Marlow & Co. owner, VISA ••4242, fixed prices, named service list) with backend-driven content and a neutral payment-method placeholder, and both add a PkgTopBar over the spec's SheetFrame — these are shared, deliberate adaptations, not regressions. The only genuine per-platform divergence is Android's two wrong icon glyphs (BadgeCheck for ticket-check, Tag for ticket) which iOS gets right; iOS's only edge is the missing footnote line-height that Android sets.

**iOS deviations:**
- `low`/`chrome` — Design renders this as a SheetFrame (label header only, no nav bar); BuyPackageView wraps it in PkgTopBar with back chevron + centered 'Buy package' title — an acceptable native presentation but adds chrome not in the spec. **Fix:** Acceptable as native sheet/nav adaptation; optionally present as a sheet to match the modal framing.
- `low`/`extra-element` — payMethodRow renders a neutral credit-card glyph + 'Add a payment method' instead of the spec's VISA gradient chip (34x24, blue gradient, 'VISA') + 'Visa ••4242' label; saved-card backend is deferred. **Fix:** When card-on-file is wired, render the brand chip + masked PAN per spec.
- `low`/`typography` — footnote sets font size 10.5 but omits an explicit line-height; spec footnote is lineHeight 15px (Android sets lineHeight=15.sp). **Fix:** Add .lineSpacing or a 15pt line height to the footnote Text to match.
- `low`/`missing-element` — eligibleRow body shows 'All of this provider's services'/'The selected service' rather than the spec's concrete service list ('Haircut · Beard trim · Kids cut'); acceptable as data-driven content. **Fix:** None needed; backend-driven service list is a reasonable substitution for mock copy.

**Android deviations:**
- `med`/`icon` — EligibleRow uses PantopusIcon.BadgeCheck (a verified-seal/VerifiedUser glyph) but the spec's eligibility row icon is ticket-check; iOS correctly uses .ticketCheck. **Fix:** Use PantopusIcon.Ticket (closest available; no TicketCheck enum) for the EligibleRow leading icon.
- `med`/`icon` — UpsellBanner uses PantopusIcon.Tag, but the spec's already-owns-credits banner icon is ticket; iOS correctly uses .ticket and PantopusIcon.Ticket exists on Android. **Fix:** Change the UpsellBanner icon from PantopusIcon.Tag to PantopusIcon.Ticket.
- `low`/`chrome` — Design is a SheetFrame (no nav bar); BuyPackageScreen adds PkgTopBar with back chevron + centered 'Buy package' title — acceptable native adaptation but extra chrome vs spec. **Fix:** Acceptable; optionally present as a bottom sheet to match modal framing.
- `low`/`extra-element` — PayMethodRow renders a neutral credit-card glyph (tinted info blue) + 'Add a payment method' instead of the spec's VISA gradient chip + 'Visa ••4242'; saved-card backend deferred. **Fix:** When card-on-file is wired, render the brand chip + masked PAN per spec.
- `low`/`color` — PayMethodRow card-chip icon is tinted PantopusColors.info while iOS tints it Theme.Color.stripeBrand; minor cross-platform inconsistency on a placeholder element. **Fix:** Align the placeholder tint between platforms (use a shared brand/stripe token).

### G11 My packages — iOS `major` / Android `major` → better: **ios**
- iOS files: `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Scheduling/Business/Packages/MyPackagesView.swift`, `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Scheduling/Business/Packages/PackagesKit.swift`
- Android files: `frontend/apps/android/app/src/main/java/app/pantopus/android/ui/screens/scheduling/packages/MyPackagesScreen.kt`, `frontend/apps/android/app/src/main/java/app/pantopus/android/ui/screens/scheduling/packages/PackagesKit.kt`
- **Verdict:** Both platforms render a faithful active/spent/empty card but each omits the design's two signature elements — the collapsible redemption-history sub-section and the card-level amber expiring-soon banner — and both replace the spec's "Expires/Ended {date}" caption and real owner names with a "Purchased {date}" caption and a "Business provider" placeholder; iOS edges ahead only because Android uses the wrong empty-state icon.
- **Cross note:** Both screens were clearly built from the same simplified projection: identical card layout, identical 'Purchased {date}' caption, identical owner placeholder, and both drop the redemption-history sub-section and the expiring-soon amber banner. Fixes should land in parallel on both platforms; the only divergence is Android's wrong empty-state icon (Tag vs the spec ticket, which iOS gets right).

**iOS deviations:**
- `high`/`missing-element` — CreditCard has no redemption-history section; spec Frame 1/4 PkgCard renders a collapsible 'REDEMPTION HISTORY' overline + chevron-up + HistoryRow rows (check icon, service, date, '1 credit'). **Fix:** Add a history block under the CTA gated on credit history: overline (10/700 uppercase fg3), chevron-up, and rows with Icon(.check, 13, success), service 11.5 fg2, date 10.5 fg4, '1 credit' 10/700 fg3.
- `high`/`missing-element` — No expiring-soon variant; spec Frame 4 adds a card-top amber banner (clock-alert 14, warnBg fill, warnBorder hairline, 'N credits expire in N days — book soon.' 11/600 warn). **Fix:** Render a leading banner row inside the card when expiringSoon: HStack(clockAlert + warn text) on Theme.Color.warningBg with bottom warningLight border.
- `med`/`missing-element` — Spent state never distinguishes Expired from All used; spec shows an 'Expired' pill when credits remain but the package lapsed vs 'All used' when left==0, plus greyed meter via borderStrong. **Fix:** Branch on expired-vs-used in the model and show PkgChip(text:'Expired') for the expired case alongside the existing 'All used'.
- `med`/`typography` — Caption reads 'Purchased {date}' (size 10.5); spec caption is 'Expires {date}' for active and 'Ended {date}' for spent (10.5 fg3). **Fix:** Replace the purchased caption with expiry copy keyed off spent: 'Expires …' / 'Ended …'.
- `med`/`other` — Owner label is the placeholder '\(ownerTheme.title) provider' (e.g. 'Business provider'); spec OwnerRow shows the real owner name ('Marlow & Co.', 'Pawfect'). **Fix:** Surface the real owner display name from the credit/package DTO instead of the pillar placeholder.

**Android deviations:**
- `high`/`missing-element` — CreditCard omits the redemption-history section that spec Frame 1/4 PkgCard renders (collapsible 'REDEMPTION HISTORY' overline + chevron-up + HistoryRow rows with check icon, service, date, '1 credit'). **Fix:** Add a history block below the CTA: overline (10.sp/Bold uppercase appTextSecondary), chevron-up, and rows with PantopusIcon.Check (13.dp, success), service 11.5.sp appTextStrong, date 10.5.sp, '1 credit' 10.sp/Bold.
- `high`/`missing-element` — No expiring-soon variant; spec Frame 4 prepends a card-level amber banner (clock-alert 14.dp on warningBg, warningLight border, 'N credits expire in N days — book soon.' 11.sp/600 warning). **Fix:** Render a banner Row at the top of the card when expiring soon, using PantopusIcon.ClockAlert + warning text on PantopusColors.warningBg.
- `med`/`icon` — Empty state uses PantopusIcon.Tag; spec EmptyHero icon is 'ticket' and PantopusIcon.Ticket already exists in Icons.kt. **Fix:** Change EmptyState icon to PantopusIcon.Ticket to match the spec ticket disc.
- `med`/`missing-element` — Spent cards never show an 'Expired' pill — code only emits 'All used' when remaining==0; spec distinguishes Expired (credits remain but lapsed) from All used. **Fix:** Compute expired vs used in the VM and render PkgChip(text='Expired', tone=Neutral, uppercased=true) for the expired case.
- `med`/`typography` — Caption renders 'Purchased {date}' (10.5.sp); spec caption is 'Expires {date}' (active) / 'Ended {date}' (spent). **Fix:** Replace purchased caption with expiry copy keyed off spent state.
- `med`/`other` — Owner label is placeholder '${pillar.providerLabel()} provider' (e.g. 'Personal provider'); spec OwnerRow shows real owner names. **Fix:** Render the real owner display name from credit.bookingPackage instead of the pillar placeholder.
- `low`/`typography` — Count uses FontWeight.Black (~900); spec is fontWeight:800 and iOS uses .heavy (800). **Fix:** Use a SemiBold/ExtraBold weight closer to 800 to match the spec and iOS.

### G8 Packages list — iOS `matches` / Android `minor` → better: **ios**
- iOS files: `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Scheduling/Business/Packages/PackagesListView.swift`, `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Scheduling/Business/Packages/PackagesKit.swift`, `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Core/Design/Components/EmptyState.swift`, `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Core/Design/Radii.swift`, `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Core/Design/Icons.swift`
- Android files: `frontend/apps/android/app/src/main/java/app/pantopus/android/ui/screens/scheduling/packages/PackagesListScreen.kt`, `frontend/apps/android/app/src/main/java/app/pantopus/android/ui/screens/scheduling/packages/PackagesKit.kt`, `frontend/apps/android/app/src/main/java/app/pantopus/android/ui/components/EmptyState.kt`, `frontend/apps/android/app/src/main/java/app/pantopus/android/ui/theme/Radii.kt`, `frontend/apps/android/app/src/main/java/app/pantopus/android/ui/theme/Icons.kt`
- **Verdict:** Both platforms render all five spec states (active / empty / payouts-gate / archived / loading) with token-accurate chrome, segmented filter, paper-card rows, chip + sold count, and amber Stripe gate; iOS is pixel-faithful while Android substitutes a Package glyph for the spec's layers icon and renders a full-width empty CTA the spec constrains to 200pt.
- **Cross note:** Shared (non-regression): both platforms shimmer the filter segment in the loading state where the spec keeps the live FilterSeg, and both render a full-width empty CTA where the spec constrains it to width 200. Key divergence: iOS uses the correct lucide 'layers' glyph (its Icon enum has .layers) while Android lacks a Layers glyph and falls back to PantopusIcon.Package across the row disc, empty hero, and payouts gate.

**iOS deviations:**
- `low`/`missing-element` — loadingBody replaces the filter segment with Shimmer(height:36); the spec FrameLoading keeps the real FilterSeg (value='Active') above the skeleton card and only shimmers the rows. **Fix:** Render the live PkgSegmented (disabled) in loadingBody instead of a 36pt shimmer bar.
- `low`/`sizing` — emptyActive uses the shared EmptyState whose PrimaryButton is full-width; the spec wraps the empty CTA in a width:200 container. **Fix:** Constrain the empty-state CTA to ~200pt to match the centered fixed-width button in the spec.
- `low`/`interaction` — Active rows open a SwiftUI Menu (Edit / Archive) on the ellipsis; the spec's actions menu lists Edit / Duplicate / Archive (HTML caption names all three). **Fix:** Add a Duplicate action to the row's Menu to match the documented Edit / Duplicate / Archive set.

**Android deviations:**
- `med`/`icon` — PackageRow, EmptyActive and PayoutsGate use PantopusIcon.Package (a box glyph); the spec uses the lucide 'layers' icon for the row disc and empty hero, and iOS correctly uses .layers. **Fix:** Add a Layers glyph to PantopusIcon (Icons.kt) and swap Package→Layers in the row disc, EmptyActive, and PayoutsGate.
- `low`/`sizing` — EmptyActive's shared EmptyState renders a full-width PrimaryButton; the spec constrains the empty CTA to width:200. **Fix:** Pass a width-200 modifier (or a CTA-width param) so the empty CTA matches the fixed-width spec button.
- `low`/`missing-element` — PackagesLoadingBody replaces the filter segment with Shimmer(height=36); the spec FrameLoading keeps the real Active/Archived FilterSeg and only shimmers the rows. **Fix:** Render the live PkgSegmented in the loading body instead of a 36dp shimmer bar.
- `low`/`layout` — EmptyState uses fillMaxSize()+Arrangement.Center inside the loaded scroll Column which also applies padding(top=s10); the centered fill can fight the column's top padding/scroll, unlike the spec's top-anchored EmptyHero. **Fix:** Have EmptyActive/EmptyArchived use a content-height (wrapContentHeight) layout with top padding rather than fillMaxSize centering inside the scrollable column.
- `low`/`interaction` — Active row DropdownMenu offers only Edit / Archive; the spec actions menu is Edit / Duplicate / Archive. **Fix:** Add a Duplicate DropdownMenuItem to PackageRowMenu.

### G9 Create/edit package — iOS `minor` / Android `minor` → better: **equal**
- iOS files: `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Scheduling/Business/Packages/PackageEditorView.swift`, `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Scheduling/Business/Packages/PackagesKit.swift`, `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Scheduling/Business/Packages/PackageEditorViewModel.swift`
- Android files: `frontend/apps/android/app/src/main/java/app/pantopus/android/ui/screens/scheduling/packages/PackageEditorScreen.kt`, `frontend/apps/android/app/src/main/java/app/pantopus/android/ui/screens/scheduling/packages/PackagesKit.kt`, `frontend/apps/android/app/src/main/java/app/pantopus/android/ui/screens/scheduling/packages/PackageEditorViewModel.kt`
- **Verdict:** Both platforms are near-identical, faithful renders of the create/edit form — correct section order, cards, per-session math, and infoBlue edit note — but both omit Frame 4 (has-active-buyers: warning lock note + locked sessions/eligibility) and both render the section overlines gray instead of the spec's pillar-violet accent.
- **Cross note:** iOS and Android are deliberate 1:1 mirrors (same PkgCard/PkgStepper/PkgSegmented/PkgToggleRow kit, same section order, same VM shape), so they share every deviation — most importantly the entirely missing has-active-buyers (locked) variant and the gray-instead-of-violet section overlines. Neither is closer to the spec.

**iOS deviations:**
- `high`/`state` — Frame 4 (has-active-buyers) is unimplemented: PackageEditorView never renders the warning PkgNote ('12 people own credits…' with lock icon) and never passes a locked flag to redeemCard/sessionsCard, so sessions+eligibility can't be locked. **Fix:** Add a lockedByBuyers flag from the VM (sold/active-credit count); render PkgNote(tone:.warning, icon:.lock, …) above the Redeems card and disable PkgStepper + EventTile when locked.
- `med`/`color` — PkgCard overline uses Theme.Color.appTextSecondary (gray #6b7280); the event-editor Card spec paints the overline in the pillar accent (business violet #7c3aed) — the kit's stated non-negotiable. **Fix:** Pass the owner pillar accent (Theme.Color.business) to PkgCard's overline foreground instead of appTextSecondary.
- `low`/`sizing` — PkgStepper renders a borderless sunken-filled pill (radius 8, no dividers); design Stepper is a 1.5px-bordered box with divider lines, minus tinted fg2 and plus tinted blue600. **Fix:** Give PkgStepper a 1.5px appBorder, internal divider hairlines, and tint the plus glyph primary600 to match the event-editor Stepper.
- `low`/`icon` — EventTile uses .calendar (and .layers for an injected 'All services' tile); design RedeemCard tiles use a scissors glyph and contain no 'All services' tile. **Fix:** Use a service/scissors-style glyph for real event tiles; keep the synthetic 'All services' tile but acknowledge it's an addition beyond the four spec tiles.
- `low`/`sizing` — PkgToggleRow icon disc is 32×32 radius 9 with a constant gray sunken bg; design ToggleRow disc is 30×30 radius 8 and tints blue50 bg + blue600 icon when on. Label 13 vs spec 12.5, sub 11 vs 10.5. **Fix:** Shrink disc to 30/radius8, tint it blue50/blue600 in the on state, drop label to 12.5 and sub to 10.5.

**Android deviations:**
- `high`/`state` — Frame 4 (has-active-buyers) is unimplemented: EditorCards never renders the warning PkgNote ('12 people own credits…' lock icon) and RedeemTiles/PkgStepper receive no locked flag, so sessions+eligibility can't be locked. **Fix:** Expose a lockedByBuyers flag on PackageEditorUiState.Content; render PkgNote(tone=Warning, icon=Lock) before the Redeems card and pass enabled=false to PkgStepper + disable EventTile clicks when locked.
- `med`/`color` — PkgCard overline uses PantopusColors.appTextSecondary (gray); spec event-editor Card overline is the pillar accent (business violet #7c3aed). **Fix:** Color the overline with state.pillar.accent (PantopusColors.business) instead of appTextSecondary.
- `low`/`sizing` — PkgStepper is a borderless sunken pill; design Stepper is a 1.5px-bordered, divider-segmented box with plus tinted blue600. **Fix:** Add a 1.5dp appBorder + internal divider lines to PkgStepper and tint the plus glyph primary600.
- `low`/`sizing` — PkgSegmented uses outer radius Radii.md(8)/inner Radii.sm(6) and 30dp segment height; design Segmented is outer 9 / inner 7 with 32px height. **Fix:** Set the segmented outer shape to ~9dp, inner to ~7dp, and segment height to 32dp.
- `low`/`icon` — RedeemTiles use PantopusIcon.Calendar (and Package for the injected 'All services' tile); design tiles use scissors and have no 'All services' entry. ToggleRow disc 32/radius8 stays gray when on vs spec 30/radius8 tinted blue50+blue600. **Fix:** Use a service/scissors glyph for event tiles; tint the toggle icon disc blue50/blue600 in the on state and shrink to 30dp.
