### G6 Payments setup — iOS `minor` / Android `major` → better: **ios**
- iOS files: `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Scheduling/Business/Payments/PaymentsSetupView.swift`, `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Scheduling/Business/Payments/PaymentsKit.swift`, `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Scheduling/Business/Settings/BusinessSchedulingSettingsView.swift`
- Android files: `frontend/apps/android/app/src/main/java/app/pantopus/android/ui/screens/wallet/scheduling/PaymentsSetupScreen.kt`, `frontend/apps/android/app/src/main/java/app/pantopus/android/ui/screens/scheduling/_shared/OwnerPillarChrome.kt`
- **Verdict:** Both faithfully reproduce the status-hero + readiness-pills + Account/Tax groups across all five frames, but iOS nails the chrome and Stripe-brand badge while Android diverges on top-bar (left title + extra accent bar), badge color, and row-value placement.
- **Cross note:** Both platforms make the same two intentional content simplifications (descriptor \"Managed on Stripe\" instead of the on-receipt monospace value; Collect-tax chevron instead of the spec toggle). Key divergence: iOS top bar and Stripe-brand badge match the spec, while Android's shared OwnerPillarHeader (left title + accent bar) and violet badge do not.

**iOS deviations:**
- `med`/`missing-element` — Connected statement-descriptor row shows sub "Managed on Stripe"; spec Receipt renders the on-receipt value "MARLOW CO" in a monospace sunken pill with a receipt glyph, and the Payouts row sub is "Bank ••4291 · daily". **Fix:** Render the descriptor value as a monospace chip and surface the masked bank/payout cadence in the Payouts sub.
- `med`/`interaction` — Tax group "Collect tax" connected trailing is a chevron (rowTrailing); spec SRow trailing is a Business-violet IToggle (on). **Fix:** Render an on Toggle tinted Theme.Color.business in the connected Collect-tax row instead of a chevron.
- `low`/`other` — ReadinessPill uses Radii.md (8) for its background corner radius; spec ReadyPill borderRadius is 10. **Fix:** Use a 10pt corner radius on the pill (or a Radii token equal to 10).
- `low`/`color` — On-pill bg uses Theme.Color.successBg; spec ReadyPill on bg is C.okBg (the success-bg tone) — verify the token maps to #F0FDF4. **Fix:** Confirm successBg maps to the spec okBg value.

**Android deviations:**
- `high`/`chrome` — OwnerPillarHeader left-aligns the title at PantopusTextStyle.h3 (~20sp) and appends a pillar accent bar; spec TopBar centers the title at 15sp/semibold (tracking -0.2), 46dp tall with only a 1dp bottom border and a trailing slot, no accent bar. **Fix:** Use a centered 15sp/semibold title, drop the accent bar, add a trailing slot, and match the 46dp bar with a bottom border.
- `med`/`color` — Stripe badge Box background is PILLAR.accent (business violet #7C3AED); spec StripeBadge background is C.stripe (#635bff Stripe indigo). **Fix:** Add a stripeBrand color token (#635bff) and use it for the badge background, matching iOS.
- `med`/`layout` — PaymentRow renders the connected value (USD, "Managed on Stripe", "automatic") as right-aligned trailing text; spec SRow shows the value as a sub line beneath the label (left-aligned) with a chevron on the right. **Fix:** Move value into a 11sp sub line under the label and keep the chevron as the sole trailing element.
- `med`/`missing-element` — Connected descriptor/payout rows omit the spec Receipt monospace "MARLOW CO" pill and the "Bank ••4291 · daily" payout detail (uses "Managed on Stripe"/null). **Fix:** Render the descriptor as a monospace chip and the masked bank/cadence on the Payouts row.
- `med`/`interaction` — Tax "Collect tax" connected trailing is a chevron→dashboard; spec trailing is a Business-violet IToggle (on). **Fix:** Render an on Switch tinted PILLAR.accent in the connected Collect-tax row.
- `low`/`color` — On-pill and "Connected" chip backgrounds use PantopusColors.successLight (#D1FAE5); spec ReadyPill/Chip success bg is C.okBg (the softer success-bg tone). **Fix:** Use the success-bg token for the on-pill and Connected-chip backgrounds.

### G7 Payouts and earnings — iOS `minor` / Android `minor` → better: **android**
- iOS files: `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Wallet/Scheduling/PayoutsEarningsView.swift`, `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Wallet/Scheduling/PayoutsEarningsViewModel.swift`, `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Core/Design/Components/BalanceHero.swift`, `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Wallet/Components/PayoutMethodCard.swift`, `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Scheduling/Business/Payments/PaymentsKit.swift`, `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Core/Design/Radii.swift`
- Android files: `frontend/apps/android/app/src/main/java/app/pantopus/android/ui/screens/wallet/scheduling/PayoutsEarningsScreen.kt`, `frontend/apps/android/app/src/main/java/app/pantopus/android/ui/screens/wallet/scheduling/PayoutsEarningsViewModel.kt`, `frontend/apps/android/app/src/main/java/app/pantopus/android/ui/components/BalanceHero.kt`, `frontend/apps/android/app/src/main/java/app/pantopus/android/ui/screens/wallet/components/PayoutMethodCard.kt`, `frontend/apps/android/app/src/main/java/app/pantopus/android/ui/screens/scheduling/payments/CancellationRefundPolicyScreen.kt`
- **Verdict:** Both faithfully reproduce the Wallet hero + source-filter + grouped earnings rows + payout tile + tax row + sticky withdraw across all four frames; Android nails the spec's literal radii/heights (13/14/48) while iOS rounds them up via shared Radii tokens, so Android is marginally closer.
- **Cross note:** Shared issues on both: the reused BalanceHero oversizes the balance (44 vs spec 38) and the PayoutMethodCard shows a generic 'Bank account ••••' rather than the spec's 'Chase checking ••7421'. All four design frames (populated / on-hold-reverify / payouts-not-enabled / empty) are covered on both via the same payoutState branches inside Loaded; the separate 'Payments coming soon' scaffold (iOS PaidSurfaceGate, Android PaymentsComingSoon) is a feature-flag gate, not the spec's not-enabled frame, so it does not displace Frame 3.

**iOS deviations:**
- `low`/`sizing` — PayoutsWithdrawButton uses height 52 and Radii.xl (16) corner; spec Withdraw is height 48 / radius 13. **Fix:** Set frame(height: 48) and use a 13pt corner radius for the withdraw button (and locked variant).
- `low`/`typography` — Withdraw label/amount font is 15pt and icon size 17; spec is 14px text with a 16px arrow-down-to-line icon. **Fix:** Drop withdraw text to 14pt and the icon to 16pt.
- `low`/`sizing` — earningsList / connect-tile / empty card use Radii.xl (16) corner; spec card radius is 14. **Fix:** Use a 14pt radius for the tx list, connect-Stripe tile, and empty card.
- `low`/`typography` — Shared BalanceHero renders the balance at 44pt/heavy; spec hero amount is 38px/weight 800 (~16% oversized), and currency chip/overline are 10pt vs spec 9.5pt. **Fix:** Reduce hero amount to ~38pt and chip/overline to 9.5pt in BalanceHero.
- `low`/`color` — Payout tile body shows generic 'Bank account ••••' rather than the spec's 'Chase checking ••7421'; data-driven so acceptable, but last4 renders as '••••' placeholder. **Fix:** Plumb the real bank name + last4 from the connect account into WalletPayoutMethod.

**Android deviations:**
- `low`/`layout` — EmptyEarnings body Text omits center alignment and the spec's 200px maxWidth, so the copy left-aligns full-width inside the dashed card instead of centered/clamped. **Fix:** Add textAlign = TextAlign.Center and widthIn(max = 200.dp) to the empty-state body text.
- `low`/`sizing` — Filter chips use vertical = 7.dp padding instead of a fixed 30dp height; chip height drifts with text metrics vs spec's exact height 30. **Fix:** Replace vertical padding with Modifier.height(30.dp) and center the label.
- `low`/`typography` — Shared BalanceHero renders the balance at 44sp/ExtraBold; spec hero amount is 38px/800, and the currency chip/overline are 10–10.5sp vs spec 9.5px. **Fix:** Reduce hero amount to ~38sp and chip/overline to 9.5sp in BalanceHero.kt.
- `low`/`color` — Payout tile body shows generic 'Bank account ••••' instead of spec 'Chase checking ••7421'; last4 is a '••••' placeholder. **Fix:** Plumb real bank name + last4 from the connect account into WalletPayoutMethod.

## Invoices

### G12 Invoices list — iOS `major` / Android `major` → better: **equal**
- iOS files: `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Scheduling/Business/Invoices/InvoicesListView.swift`, `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Scheduling/Business/Invoices/InvoicesListViewModel.swift`, `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Scheduling/Business/Invoices/InvoicesKit.swift`
- Android files: `frontend/apps/android/app/src/main/java/app/pantopus/android/ui/screens/scheduling/invoices/InvoicesListScreen.kt`, `frontend/apps/android/app/src/main/java/app/pantopus/android/ui/screens/scheduling/invoices/InvoicesListViewModel.kt`, `frontend/apps/android/app/src/main/java/app/pantopus/android/ui/screens/scheduling/invoices/InvoicesKit.kt`
- **Verdict:** Both platforms are near-identical mirror implementations that nail the chrome, layout order, spacing, and loading/empty/gate states, but both omit the design's defining row elements — the trailing status pill and the payer display name — and relabel the summary KPIs, due to a shared lean-InvoiceDTO gap.
- **Cross note:** iOS and Android are deliberate mirror implementations: same states (loading/comingSoon/gate/empty/error/loaded), same shared PkgTopBar/PkgCard/PkgRowCard/PkgStripeGate/EmptyState components, identical row geometry (34dp avatar, 11dp gaps, sizes 13/10.5/13.5), and the exact same documented InvoiceDTO gap driving the missing status pills, missing payer names, and relabeled summary KPIs. Neither is closer.

**iOS deviations:**
- `high`/`missing-element` — InvoiceRow's trailing VStack renders only the amount; the design's required status pill (Paid/Sent/Overdue/Void/Refunded, fontSize 9 bold uppercase, bg/fg per STATUS map) is omitted — explicitly deferred in a comment pending a DTO status field. **Fix:** Add a PkgChip status pill below the amount in the trailing column once status is available; surface it from totals/status data.
- `high`/`missing-element` — InvoiceRow primary line shows the mono INV- reference (font .monospaced size 13 semibold); the design's bold payer name (size 13 weight 600) is the primary line with the reference relegated to the mono sub-line `INV-… · service`. **Fix:** Render payer display name as the primary line and move the mono reference into the caption next to the service.
- `med`/`typography` — summary stat labels read 'Invoices' and 'Total invoiced'; the design's Summary shows 'Outstanding' ($642, amber when overdue) and 'Collected · month' ($3,180). **Fix:** Wire Outstanding/Collected KPIs from status+paid_at and keep the amber overdue treatment that hasOverdue already supports.
- `low`/`state` — selectFilter is view-only (selectedFilter never filters the list since the DTO lacks status), so Paid/Sent/Overdue/Refunded chips render but do nothing — the design implies functional filtering (frame 3 Overdue). **Fix:** Apply the selected status filter to the invoice list once status lands.
- `low`/`color` — Day section header uses appTextMuted (fg4 #9ca3af) which matches the design's E.fg4 grouping label — correct; no fix needed (noted for completeness). **Fix:** None.

**Android deviations:**
- `high`/`missing-element` — InvoiceRow renders avatar + reference/service + amount only; the design's trailing status pill (9sp bold uppercase, per-status bg/fg) is absent — deferred pending a status field on InvoiceDto. **Fix:** Add a status pill chip beneath the amount in the trailing column once status is decoded.
- `high`/`missing-element` — InvoiceRow primary line is the FontFamily.Monospace INV- reference (13sp SemiBold); design's primary is the bold payer name with the mono reference in the `INV-… · service` caption. **Fix:** Use the payer display name as the primary text and move the mono reference into the secondary caption.
- `med`/`typography` — SummaryCard Stat labels are 'Invoices' and 'Total invoiced'; design Summary is 'Outstanding' (amber-when-overdue) and 'Collected · month'. **Fix:** Switch to Outstanding/Collected KPIs and add the amber overdue recolor matching the design's Summary overdue variant.
- `low`/`state` — selectFilter only updates _filter; the list is never filtered (DTO has no status), so the Paid/Sent/Overdue/Refunded chips are non-functional vs the design's filtered Overdue frame. **Fix:** Filter sections by the selected status once the field is available.
- `low`/`layout` — Section day headers sit inside a single PkgRowCard with HorizontalDivider between sections; design draws each day group as its own Card with a top hairline between groups — visually close but groups share one card here. **Fix:** Acceptable as a minor simplification; optionally split each day into its own card to match Grouped's per-section Card.

### G13 Invoice detail — iOS `major` / Android `major` → better: **equal**
- iOS files: `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Scheduling/Business/Invoices/InvoiceDetailView.swift`, `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Scheduling/Business/Invoices/InvoiceDetailViewModel.swift`
- Android files: `frontend/apps/android/app/src/main/java/app/pantopus/android/ui/screens/scheduling/invoices/InvoiceDetailScreen.kt`
- **Verdict:** Both platforms ship the same intentionally-simplified invoice detail (mono header, total hero, payer/payee cards, line-items table, payment terms, Share+Send dock) and both omit the same large set of design sections — status pill, linked booking row, subtotal/service-fee/tax fee block, timeline, receipt capsule, note-from-sender, and all six non-default status frames — so neither is meaningfully closer to the spec.
- **Cross note:** Identical scope: both implement the same simplified subset and both explicitly document (iOS VM comment) that status/timeline/due/memo/payer-name design sections are omitted because the InvoiceDTO lacks those fields. The only platform divergence is Android's hardcoded-padding baseline hack on the hero vs iOS's correct firstTextBaseline.

**iOS deviations:**
- `high`/`missing-element` — TopBar (PkgTopBar) has no trailing StatusPill; spec puts a status pill (Draft/Sent/Paid/Deposit paid/Overdue/Void/Refunded) in the top bar trailing slot. **Fix:** Add a StatusPill trailing view to PkgTopBar driven by invoice.status with the 7 PILL bg/fg color pairs.
- `high`/`missing-element` — No BookingRow: spec shows a linked-booking card (calendar icon tile, service title, date, chevron) between payer/payee and Line items; iOS jumps straight to lineItemsSection. **Fix:** Insert a tappable BookingRow card after payerPayee that pushes the linked booking route.
- `high`/`missing-element` — ItemsTable omits the fee block — spec's raised footer lists Subtotal, Service fee (3%), Tax (5.7%) above a divider before Total; iOS table jumps from line rows straight to the Total row. **Fix:** Render subtotal/service-fee/tax rows in the appSurfaceRaised footer above the Total divider.
- `high`/`missing-element` — No Timeline section (icon=activity): spec shows a payment timeline (Created/Sent/Paid/Deposit/Refunded/Voided dots + mono timestamps) that scales with status. **Fix:** Add a Timeline section component fed by invoice lifecycle events.
- `med`/`missing-element` — No ReceiptCapsule: spec shows a success-bg 'Paid with Pantopus Pay' capsule with shield-check icon + mono receipt id when status=paid. **Fix:** Render a ReceiptCapsule below Timeline when status is paid.
- `med`/`missing-element` — No 'Note from sender' section (icon=message-square-quote) with italic raised-bg quote; present in 6 of 7 design frames. **Fix:** Add a conditional sender-note Section when the invoice has a memo.
- `high`/`state` — Only a single default render: hero never shows the paid check-prefix / warn-orange overdue / split balance-due (partial) / business-violet refunded variants, and the dock is fixed to Share+Send instead of the per-status docks (Mark paid+Resend+Overflow, Share+Download PDF, Send balance, etc.). **Fix:** Drive hero color/prefix/split, totalLabel, and dock button set from invoice.status across the 7 spec states.
- `low`/`typography` — Mono header omits the '· due Jun 18' segment — iOS renders only reference + 'issued' (issuedLabel), dropping the due date the spec shows. **Fix:** Append ' · due <dueLabel>' to the monospace header string.

**Android deviations:**
- `high`/`missing-element` — PkgTopBar has no trailing StatusPill; spec puts a status pill (Draft/Sent/Paid/etc.) in the top bar trailing slot. **Fix:** Add a trailing StatusPill composable to PkgTopBar driven by state.status with the 7 PILL color pairs.
- `high`/`missing-element` — No BookingRow linked-booking card between the payer/payee Row and the Line items SectionHeader. **Fix:** Insert a clickable BookingRow (calendar tile + title + date + chevron) after the identity Row.
- `high`/`missing-element` — ItemsTable lacks the fee block — spec footer shows Subtotal / Service fee (3%) / Tax (5.7%) rows above the Total divider; Android goes from line rows straight to the Total row. **Fix:** Add subtotal/service-fee/tax rows in the appSurfaceRaised footer above Total.
- `high`/`missing-element` — No Timeline section (activity icon) rendering the payment-lifecycle dot list with mono timestamps. **Fix:** Add a Timeline composable fed by lifecycle events between line items and payment terms.
- `med`/`missing-element` — No ReceiptCapsule ('Paid with Pantopus Pay', shield-check, mono receipt id) shown when status=paid. **Fix:** Render a success-bg ReceiptCapsule when state is paid.
- `med`/`missing-element` — No 'Note from sender' italic-quote section (message-square-quote icon) present in 6 of 7 design frames. **Fix:** Add a conditional sender-note SectionHeader + italic raised-bg text when a memo exists.
- `high`/`state` — Single default render only: hero never shows paid check-prefix / overdue warn color / partial split-balance / refunded violet, and dock is fixed to Share+Send instead of per-status docks (Mark paid+Resend+Overflow, Share+Download PDF, Send balance). **Fix:** Branch hero color/prefix/split, totalLabel, and dock buttons on state.status across the 7 spec states.
- `low`/`layout` — Hero baseline is faked with Alignment.Bottom + a hardcoded bottom-padding 4.dp on the 'total · USD' label instead of true text-baseline alignment (spec uses alignItems:baseline); iOS uses firstTextBaseline correctly. **Fix:** Use Alignment alignByBaseline (Row with alignBy(LastBaseline)) and drop the manual 4.dp padding.

## Automations

### H1 Default reminders — iOS `matches` / Android `matches` → better: **equal**
- iOS files: `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Scheduling/Automations/Reminders/DefaultRemindersView.swift`, `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Scheduling/Automations/Shared/AutomationsKit.swift`
- Android files: `frontend/apps/android/app/src/main/java/app/pantopus/android/ui/screens/scheduling/automations/RemindersQuickSetupScreen.kt`, `frontend/apps/android/app/src/main/java/app/pantopus/android/ui/screens/scheduling/automations/AutomationsKit.kt`
- **Verdict:** Both platforms reproduce the H1 Default-reminders sheet near-pixel-perfectly (header, helper, 6-row check-circle card with Push/Email chips, dashed add-custom chip, sticky Save, and all four frames); the only shared divergence is rendering the saved-success confirmation as a floating bottom toast instead of the spec's slim dark banner stacked inside the footer above Save.
- **Cross note:** Both platforms share the identical (minor) divergence: the Frame-3 saved confirmation is a floating bottom toast rather than the spec's inline dark banner stacked above Save inside the footer. All four spec frames (default, first-open copy, saved, push-off banner) are covered on both, plus extra loading/error states. Shared kits (AutoCard radius 16/Radii.xl, header 17/bold + 12 subhead, channel chips h24 fs10.5, dashed chip h34 1.5px dash, Save 46h radius-lg fs14.5 bold) match spec values 1:1 on both platforms.

**iOS deviations:**
- `low`/`state` — Frame 3 success confirmation is rendered as a floating bottom toast (AutoToast overlay, padding(.bottom,92)) rather than the spec's slim dark #0f172a banner stacked above the Save button inside the footer. **Fix:** Optionally render the saved message as an inline footer banner above AutoPrimaryButton to match Frame 3 layout, or accept native toast idiom.
- `low`/`color` — Toast check-circle uses Theme.Color.success (#059669) vs spec emerald #34d399, and toast bg uses appText (#111827) vs spec #0f172a. **Fix:** Acceptable token substitution; no change needed unless exact emerald is required.
- `low`/`extra-element` — customStepper expansion (Custom reminder card with stepper + Add time) is built but is not depicted in any of the four spec frames, which only show the static dashed 'Add custom time' chip. **Fix:** Out-of-spec enhancement; keep, it is a reasonable expansion of the chip's intent.

**Android deviations:**
- `low`/`state` — Frame 3 success confirmation is a floating bottom AutoToast (align BottomCenter, padding bottom 92.dp) instead of the spec's inline dark banner above Save in the footer. **Fix:** Optionally move the saved message inline into AutoSheetFooter above AutoPrimaryButton, or accept native toast idiom.
- `low`/`color` — Push-off banner copy says 'Push is off in system settings.' vs iOS spec text 'Push is off in iOS Settings.' (intentional platform wording; iOS code keeps 'iOS Settings'). **Fix:** Acceptable platform-correct wording; no change needed.
- `low`/`color` — Toast tint uses PantopusColors.success (#059669) vs spec #34d399 and bg appText (#111827) vs #0f172a. **Fix:** Token substitution; acceptable.
- `low`/`extra-element` — CustomStepper card (stepper + segmented unit + Add time) appears on chip tap but is not in any spec frame, which only show the dashed chip. **Fix:** Out-of-spec enhancement mirrored from iOS; keep.

### H2 Workflows list — iOS `matches` / Android `minor` → better: **ios**
- iOS files: `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Scheduling/Automations/Workflows/WorkflowsListView.swift`, `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Scheduling/Automations/Workflows/WorkflowsListViewModel.swift`, `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Scheduling/Automations/Shared/AutomationsKit.swift`, `frontend/apps/ios/Pantopus/Features/Scheduling/SharedUI/SchedulingStatusPill.swift`
- Android files: `frontend/apps/android/app/src/main/java/app/pantopus/android/ui/screens/scheduling/automations/WorkflowsListScreen.kt`, `frontend/apps/android/app/src/main/java/app/pantopus/android/ui/screens/scheduling/automations/WorkflowsListViewModel.kt`, `frontend/apps/android/app/src/main/java/app/pantopus/android/ui/screens/scheduling/automations/AutomationsSupport.kt`, `frontend/apps/android/app/src/main/java/app/pantopus/android/ui/screens/scheduling/automations/AutomationsKit.kt`
- **Verdict:** Both platforms faithfully reproduce the spec's chrome (top bar + plus action), A08 underline tab strip, pinned Default-reminders card, Your-workflows group, FAB, and all five frames; Android differs only in using a Sparkles empty-state icon (spec/iOS use workflow) and a few small geometry nits, so iOS is marginally closer.

**iOS deviations:**
- `low`/`state` — statusKey() returns only "active"/"paused"; spec WfRow also defines a third "draft" (warning-tone) chip that the list can never render. **Fix:** Surface a draft state (e.g. when workflow.isActive is null/unpublished) so SchedulingStatusPill can show the Draft variant the spec draws.

**Android deviations:**
- `med`/`icon` — WorkflowsEmpty passes PantopusIcon.Sparkles to AutoInlineEmpty, but the spec FrameEmpty (and iOS) uses the lucide "workflow" glyph in the 56px circle. **Fix:** Change both AutoInlineEmpty calls in WorkflowsEmpty to PantopusIcon.Workflow to match the spec glyph.
- `low`/`sizing` — AutoErrorView asCard "Try again" button uses padding(vertical = 9.dp) rather than the spec's fixed 38px button height (iOS frames the Text at height 38). **Fix:** Give the retry button a fixed 38.dp height (heightIn(min=38.dp)) to match the spec/iOS button geometry.
- `low`/`state` — AutoStatusChip(active:) renders only Active/Paused; the spec WfRow defines a third Draft (warning) chip that is unreachable. **Fix:** Extend AutoStatusChip to a tri-state (Active/Paused/Draft) and feed it a status derived from the workflow, mirroring the spec's three tones.
- `low`/`color` — AutoErrorView non-card branch and other shared paths are fine, but the error retry CTA text/copy ordering is identical to spec; no extra issue — included only to note the asCard error card matches spec chrome (radius 16, 1px border, 48px sunken circle, filled-sky button). **Fix:** No change needed; verified parity for the error frame.
